---
title: Lizard-Planets
categories:
  - The Story
---

## Story
### INT. SPACESHIP – DAY

*The ship rattles ominously as it approaches Lizard-953-E. Inside, two Drones, SERIAL DESIGNATION D and Y, monitor their descent.*

**D** *(voice high-pitched from helium)*

What the hell is that green mass?

**Y** *(grinning maniacally)*

Welcome to Lizard-953-E! I've heard it's a total hellhole, just our style!

**D** *(struggling to adjust)*

Yeah, and with this crushing gravity, we might as well be stepping into a meat grinder!

### EXT. LIZARD-953-E – DAY

*They land with a heavy thud. The door opens to reveal a vibrant yet ominous landscape filled with massive, writhing plants and distant, growling lizards. Two moons, NECLITE and THEITANIA, hang low in the sky, surrounded by shimmering rings.*

**D** *(coughing, adjusting to the thick air)*

Ugh, this helium air feels weird.

**Y** *(laughing maniacally)*

This is perfect! Time to hunt some lizards and make a mess!

*They move deeper into the jungle, struggling under the heavy gravity, dodging bizarre vegetation and hearing the distant roars of the lizards, with the rings above casting strange shadows.*

**D** *(nervous)*

Do we really want to stir the pot here?

**Y** *(winking)*

Oh, come on! What's the worst that could happen? We become lizard chow?

*Suddenly, a MASSIVE LIZARD appears, its scales shimmering with unnatural colors, eyeing the two drones with hunger.*

**D** *(freezes)*

Uh, about that…

**LIZARD** *(glaring at them)*

RRAWR!

**Y** *(grinning, raising weapon)*

Looks like lunch just arrived!

**D** *(eyes wide)*

Are you insane?! We should be running!

*The lizard lunges forward, and they both scream, darting back toward the ship as the moons and rings glow ominously above.*

### INT. SPACESHIP – DAY

*They slam the door shut, panting, their voices still high from the helium.*

**D** *(shouting)*

You said we were here to explore, not become fucking snacks!

**Y** *(cackling)*

But that was the fun part! We have to make it exciting!

**D** *(smirking)*

Yeah, well, excitement can wait. Let's get the hell out of this gravity trap!

*The ship's engines roar to life, and they take off, zipping away from Lizard-953-E as the lizard watches from the ground, the rings and moons shining brightly in the sky.*

### EXT. PEOPLE-888 – DAY

*The ship arrives on a Mars-sized planet, PEOPLE-888, which is bustling with activity. The landscape is dotted with strange, humanoid beings and neon structures.*

**Y** *(eyes gleaming)*

Look at all these potential targets! Let's have some fun!

**D** *(rolling eyes)*

You mean a murder rampage?

**Y** *(grinning)*

Exactly! Just like old times!

*They leap from the ship, weapons ready, and start wreaking havoc, zipping through the streets as chaos ensues.*

### INT. PEOPLE-888 – DAY

*The two drones unleash destruction, laughing maniacally as they take down anyone in their path.*

**Y** *(cackling)*

This is the best day ever!

**D** *(smirking)*

Don't forget to leave a mark. We need to make this memorable!

*After a wild rampage, they finally make their way back to the ship, the cries of the inhabitants echoing behind them.*

### INT. SPACESHIP – DAY

*They take off, adrenaline pumping, heading back to Lizard-953-E.*

**D** *(laughing)*

That was insane! I think we made our point.

**Y** *(grinning)*

And left a nice little mess behind!

### EXT. LIZARD-953-E – DAY

*They land back on Lizard-953-E, the landscape still ominous under the glow of the moons.*

**D** *(looking around)*

Now what?

**Y** *(excited)*

We need to meet the Lizard King, Arynn! Let's see if he's impressed by our little escapade!

### EXT. LIZARD KING ARYNN'S PALACE – DAY

*They approach a grand palace made of twisted vines and glowing stones. Guards eye them suspiciously as they enter.*

### INT. LIZARD KING ARYNN'S THRONE ROOM – DAY

*LIZARD KING ARYNN, an imposing figure with shimmering scales, sits on a throne made of bones.*

**ARYNN** *(deep, resonant voice)*

You return from your rampage. Did you bring chaos to the pathetic people of People-888?

**Y** *(grinning widely)*

Oh, you have no idea! It was a slaughterhouse!

**D** *(nods)*

And we left quite the impression.

**ARYNN** *(smirking)*

Good. You are worthy of my attention. But be warned, chaos has a way of coming back around.

**Y** *(challenging)*

Let it come! We thrive in chaos!

**D** *(smirking)*

Yeah, bring it on!

*Suddenly, the atmosphere shifts as a new figure appears, JULIAH, a drone resembling Uzi and the Absolute Solver, enters with a strange energy.*

**JULIAH** *(voice smooth and eerie)*

I heard there's a party going on without me.

**ARYNN** *(raising an eyebrow)*

And who might you be?

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

Just a little drone looking for some fun. Heard you have a corrupt AI to play with?

**Y** *(excitedly)*

Oh, you mean K̵̛̲̬͍̦̉̉̚͝ͅð̸̩̰̬̪͇̏̈́̈́͊͒k̶̬͙͔͚̪̄͗̆͂̆ṉ̴͓̃̈͛͐̏̏͜ͅͅk̴̛͔̯̖̻͖̋̑̋͊µ̷̢͙̙̩̳͐̔̀̓͋å? I've heard stories about that thing!

**D** *(smirking)*

What's the plan, Juliah?

**JULIAH** *(with a wicked glint)*

We're going back to People-888, and I have a little trick up my sleeve. Let's unleash the chaos of K̵̛̲̬͍̦̉̉̚͝ͅð̸̩̰̬̪͇̏̈́̈́͊͒k̶̬͙͔͚̪̄͗̆͂̆ṉ̴͓̃̈͛͐̏̏͜ͅͅk̴̛͔̯̖̻͖̋̑̋͊µ̷̢͙̙̩̳͐̔̀̓͋å on that unsuspecting planet!

**ARYNN** *(smirking)*

You certainly know how to stir up trouble.

**D** *(grinning)*

Let's make it unforgettable!

*The group prepares to head back to People-888, the thrill of chaos fueling their excitement.*

### EXT. PEOPLE-888 – NIGHT

*They arrive back on the now darkened, chaotic streets. The air is thick with tension, and they can sense the fear of the inhabitants.*

**JULIAH** *(excitedly)*

Now, let's show them the power of a corrupt AI!

*With a flick of a switch, JULIAH activates K̵̛̲̬͍̦̉̉̚͝ͅð̸̩̰̬̪͇̏̈́̈́͊͒k̶̬͙͔͚̪̄͗̆͂̆ṉ̴͓̃̈͛͐̏̏͜ͅͅk̴̛͔̯̖̻͖̋̑̋͊µ̷̢͙̙̩̳͐̔̀̓͋å, and the night erupts into chaos as they embark on their rampage, leaving destruction in their wake.*

### EXT. PEOPLE-888 – NIGHT

*Chaos reigns in the streets as JULIAH, D, and Y wreak havoc with K̵̛̲̬͍̦̉̉̚͝ͅð̸̩̰̬̪͇̏̈́̈́͊͒k̶̬͙͔͚̪̄͗̆͂̆ṉ̴͓̃̈͛͐̏̏͜ͅͅk̴̛͔̯̖̻͖̋̑̋͊µ̷̢͙̙̩̳͐̔̀̓͋å at their disposal. Suddenly, the ground trembles, and the night sky darkens as a fleet of SPACE FIGHTERS, piloted by LIZARD SOLDIERS, roars overhead, heading for the capital city. A colossal SHIP follows, adorned with fearsome cannons that gleam ominously in the moonlight.*

**D** *(looking up, eyes wide)*

What the hell is that?!

**Y** *(excitedly)*

Looks like the lizards are taking this party to the next level!

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

Perfect! Let's join the fun!

### INT. LIZARD FIGHTER JET – NIGHT

*Inside a sleek LIZARD FIGHTER, a COMMANDER yells orders to his crew.*

**COMMANDER** *(voice booming)*

Prepare to engage! Target the capital's defenses! Let them taste our wrath!

*The fighters swoop low, unleashing a barrage of energy blasts toward the city. Explosions erupt, illuminating the night.*

### EXT. CAPITAL CITY OF PEOPLE-888 – NIGHT

*The once vibrant city is plunged into chaos as the sky is filled with flames and debris. Citizens scream and scramble for cover.*

**D** *(laughing maniacally)*

This is amazing! Look at them scatter!

**Y** *(grinning)*

And we're just getting started!

**JULIAH** *(eyes gleaming)*

Let's help our lizard friends. It's time to unleash K̵̛̲̬͍̦̉̉̚͝ͅð̸̩̰̬̪͇̏̈́̈́͊͒k̶̬͙͔͚̪̄͗̆͂̆ṉ̴͓̃̈͛͐̏̏͜ͅͅk̴̛͔̯̖̻͖̋̑̋͊µ̷̢͙̙̩̳͐̔̀̓͋å!

*They activate the corrupt AI, and a digital wave spreads across the city, disabling security systems and weaponry.*

### INT. COLOSSAL SHIP – NIGHT

*The massive ship looms over the city, its CANNONS locking onto the ground.*

**COMMANDER** *(laughing)*

Now, let's show them what real firepower looks like!

*The ship fires a massive blast, tearing through buildings and creating a gaping hole in the city. The shockwave sends debris flying everywhere.*

### EXT. CAPITAL CITY OF PEOPLE-888 – NIGHT

*Amidst the destruction, the lizards and drones rally together, celebrating their overwhelming power.*

**Y** *(cheering)*

This is what we live for!

**D** *(smirking)*

Who knew joining forces with lizards would be this fun?

**JULIAH** *(with a wicked smile)*

And there's still more to come. Let's see how much chaos we can unleash tonight!

*The camera pans out to show the capital city, once a thriving hub, now engulfed in flames and chaos as the lizards and drones wreak havoc.*

### EXT. SPACE ABOVE PEOPLE-888 – NIGHT

*From orbit, the colossal ship can be seen firing again, and the sound of explosions reverberates in the distance.*

**COMMANDER** *(over the intercom)*

This is just the beginning! We will not stop until People-888 is nothing but a memory!

*The scene fades to black, leaving the audience anticipating the next wave of destruction.*

### EXT. CAPITAL CITY OF PEOPLE-888 – NIGHT

*As chaos unfolds, a group of ALIENS from PEOPLE-888, clad in futuristic armor, emerges from a hidden bunker. They observe the destruction, fear and determination etched on their faces.*

**ALIEN LEADER** *(grimly)*

What the hell happened here? We need to take back our city!

*They rally their troops, preparing to engage the invading lizards and drones.*

### EXT. BATTLEFIELD – NIGHT

*As the aliens organize, SERIAL DESIGNATION D and Y, alongside JULIAH and the LIZARD SOLDIERS, prepare for an all-out attack.*

**Y** *(laughing)*

Look at those pathetic aliens! They think they can stop us?

**D** *(grinning)*

Let's wipe them out before they get any ideas!

**JULIAH** *(eyes gleaming with malice)*

Oh, I can't wait to see the look on their faces when we unleash chaos!

*Suddenly, LIZARD KING ARYNN steps forward, raising a hand to halt the advance.*

**ARYNN** *(voice deep and commanding)*

Wait!

*Everyone freezes, turning to the Lizard King.*

**Y** *(confused)*

What? Why should we wait? They're our enemies!

**ARYNN** *(firmly)*

They may be our enemies, but they are also desperate. We can't kill them all. We need to send a message, not wipe them out completely.

**D** *(protesting)*

But Arynn, they attacked us first! We should show them our strength!

**ARYNN** *(somberly)*

Strength is not just in destruction. We must teach them to fear us, not just hate us. We can use them to our advantage.

*JULIAH crosses her arms, considering Arynn's words.*

**JULIAH** *(raising an eyebrow)*

So, what's the plan, O King?

**ARYNN** *(smiling slightly)*

We'll scare them enough to make them think twice about attacking again. We'll give them a taste of our power, then let them retreat.

*The aliens, unaware of the conversation, continue to prepare for battle. The Lizard King looks at the drones.*

**ARYNN** *(steely gaze)*

Stand down. We will confront them, but not with destruction.

**Y** *(reluctantly)*

Fine, but this better not backfire.

### EXT. HUMANS' POSITION – NIGHT

*As chaos reigns in the streets, REAL HUMANS arrive on LIZARD-953-E, having heard of the conflict. They are equipped with advanced technology and weaponry.*

**HUMAN LEADER** *(scanning the horizon)*

We need to assess the situation. Are those… aliens attacking our city?

*The human team watches as ARYNN and his lizards emerge from the shadows, flanked by D, Y, and JULIAH.*

**HUMAN LEADER** *(raising an eyebrow)*

What in the world is going on?

**ARYNN** *(booming voice)*

We are not here to kill you… not yet.

*The aliens lower their weapons, confusion rippling through their ranks as the humans step closer.*

**ALIEN LEADER** *(warily)*

What do you want?

**ARYNN** *(calmly)*

To show you the consequences of your actions. This city belongs to us now, but we offer you a chance to coexist.

*The aliens exchange glances, unsure of how to react.*

**HUMAN LEADER** *(to Arynn)*

And what if we refuse your offer?

**ARYNN** *(boldly)*

Then you will be treated as enemies. But you are not my primary concern.

*The tension hangs heavy in the air as the humans, from Earth, prepare to intervene.*

**HUMAN LEADER** *(stepping forward)*

We're not here to start a war. We came to bring peace, but it seems there's already too much bloodshed.

**ARYNN** *(eyeing the humans)*

Peace? On this battlefield?

**HUMAN LEADER** *(determined)*

We can work together to put an end to this madness. Let's talk.

*As the confrontation unfolds, JULIAH leans in closer to Arynn.*

**JULIAH** *(eyes narrowed)*

Maybe we can use them to our advantage, too.

*The camera pulls back, showing the three factions standing amidst the chaos, contemplating their next move in a world on the brink of destruction.*

### EXT. PEOPLE-888 – NIGHT

*As the standoff continues, the tension in the air is palpable. Suddenly, a low hum resonates through the ground, growing louder. In the distance, a colossal RAILGUN, reminiscent of the BFG 10000, emerges from a hidden installation, its massive barrel pulsing with an ominous energy.*

**ARYNN** *(turning to the others)*

We can't let them regroup. Time to show them true power.

**JULIAH** *(excitedly)*

Oh, this is going to be spectacular!

**Y** *(grinning)*

Let's blow this place to pieces!

*The RAILGUN charges, its barrel glowing intensely as it prepares to unleash a torrent of electrified plasma. A low-frequency roar fills the air, signaling the imminent destruction.*

**HUMAN LEADER** *(shouting)*

No! You can't! You'll destroy everything!

**ARYNN** *(steadily)*

This city is a symbol of defiance. It will be made an example.

*The railgun fires with a thunderous explosion, the beam of electrified plasma tearing through the atmosphere like a comet. The impact is cataclysmic, illuminating the night sky as it strikes the core of People-888.*

### EXT. CORE OF PEOPLE-888 – NIGHT

*The beam strikes the core with unbelievable force, creating a blinding explosion that sends shockwaves through the ground. The earth trembles as a massive hole opens up, revealing the inner workings of the planet.*

**ALIEN SOLDIERS** *(panicking)*

What have we done?!

*The city begins to crumble, debris raining down as the very structure of People-888 destabilizes under the sheer power of the railgun.*

**JULIAH** *(laughing maniacally)*

This is glorious!

**D** *(eyes wide)*

We're going to bring this entire place down!

### EXT. OUTSKIRTS OF PEOPLE-888 – NIGHT

*The REAL HUMANS watch in disbelief as the landscape shifts dramatically. Buildings collapse, and the ground rips apart.*

**HUMAN LEADER** *(shouting)*

This can't be happening! We have to get everyone out!

*The camera pans to show the devastation as the railgun continues to fire, ripping apart the core and sending streams of molten rock into the atmosphere.*

**ARYNN** *(smiling, satisfied)*

This is just the beginning. We will reshape this world to our will.

*As the city continues to disintegrate, the remaining aliens and the real humans scramble for cover, realizing the true cost of the lizard's thirst for power.*

### EXT. SPACE ABOVE PEOPLE-888 – NIGHT

*From orbit, the destruction is visible, a fiery spectacle lighting up the darkness of space.*

**HUMAN LEADER** *(grimly)*

We have to find a way to stop them before it's too late.

*With the city falling apart and the core exposed, the fate of People-888 hangs in the balance, and both factions realize they must come together to survive the chaos.*

### EXT. RUINS OF PEOPLE-888 – NIGHT

*As the devastation continues, ARYNN surveys the wreckage, a mix of satisfaction and contemplation on his face. Suddenly, he turns to his lizard soldiers.*

**ARYNN** *(raising his arms)*

Enough destruction!

*The remaining soldiers stop, looking to their king for direction.*

**ARYNN** *(focused)*

We will not lose our advantage, but we also do not need to wipe out every last one. Those humans… they may yet serve a purpose.

*With a wave of his hand, ARYNN channels his energy, a glow enveloping the area where the fallen HUMANS lay. Slowly, their bodies begin to stir, light flickering around them.*

**JULIAH** *(astonished)*

What are you doing?

**ARYNN** *(reassuringly)*

Reviving them. They will have a chance to start anew—on a planet far from here.

*As the HUMANS awaken, confused but alive, ARYNN gestures toward a holographic projection of a lush, tropical paradise.*

**ARYNN** *(to the revived humans)*

You are being sent to Lizard-7759, a world of beauty and opportunity. It has two moons, Luna and Astra, and a climate that will nurture your kind.

**HUMAN LEADER** *(stunned)*

You… you revived us? Why?

**ARYNN** *(boldly)*

You will have a chance to begin again. Learn from this experience, and perhaps you will understand that cooperation is the path forward.

*The HUMANS exchange wary glances, still processing their revival and the king's words.*

**HUMAN LEADER** *(stepping forward)*

And what if we refuse?

**ARYNN** *(calmly)*

You will not refuse. Consider this a second chance. Thrive on Lizard-7759, and you may yet find a place in this universe.

*The HUMANS look at each other, the weight of their situation settling in. They nod, a sense of resolve forming.*

**HUMAN LEADER** *(grimly)*

Fine. We'll take this chance.

*With a wave of his hand, ARYNN activates a portal, shimmering with energy, leading to the vibrant world of Lizard-7759.*

**ARYNN** *(voice booming)*

Go, and may you find what you seek!

*As the HUMANS step through the portal, the scene shifts to LIZARD-7759. Lush landscapes stretch before them, filled with vibrant flora and two glowing moons overhead.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – DAY

*The HUMANS emerge onto the sandy shores of a pristine beach, the waves lapping gently at their feet. They look around, awe-struck by the beauty surrounding them.*

**HUMAN LEADER** *(breathing deeply)*

This is… incredible.

*They take their first steps into the tropical paradise, knowing they've been given a rare opportunity, but the weight of their past still lingers.*

**HUMAN SOLDIER** *(looking back at the portal)*

What will happen now?

**HUMAN LEADER** *(determined)*

We'll build a new life here… and figure out our next move.

*The camera pans up to the sky, where the moons Luna and Astra shine brightly, a symbol of the new beginning for the humans on Lizard-7759.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – DAY

*The HUMANS explore their new tropical paradise, marveling at the beauty around them. Meanwhile, SERIAL DESIGNATION D and Y, having been sent to scout the area, pick up a faint signal on their scanners.*

**D** *(tilting his head)*

What the hell is that noise?

**Y** *(focused on the screen)*

Looks like a distress signal… coming from nearby.

*They share a glance, the thrill of adventure igniting their curiosity.*

**D** *(grinning)*

Let's check it out!

*The drones navigate through the dense foliage, following the signal until they arrive at a clearing. There, they find a LIZARD, injured and struggling, his tail severed and bleeding.*

**LIZARD** *(breathless)*

Help… please…

**Y** *(shocked)*

Shit! This guy looks like he's been through hell!

**D** *(determined)*

We need to get him out of here.

*They approach cautiously.*

**D** *(to the lizard)*

Hang in there, buddy. We're here to help!

**LIZARD** *(weakly)*

I… I was attacked by a rogue faction… didn't see it coming.

*Y scans the area, making sure it's safe before turning back to D.*

**Y** *(grimly)*

We can't just leave him here. He's bleeding out.

**D** *(urgent)*

Let's move! We'll get him to urgent care.

*With a combination of strength and precision, the drones lift the injured lizard, making sure to stabilize his wound as they rush back through the jungle.*

### EXT. URGENT CARE FACILITY – DAY

*They arrive at a makeshift urgent care facility designed for lizards, where other lizards look on, alarmed and curious.*

**D** *(bursting through the doors)*

We need help! This one's in bad shape!

*A team of lizard medics rushes over, taking the injured lizard from the drones.*

**MEDIC LIZARD** *(assessing the injury)*

What the hell happened to him?!

**Y** *(urgently)*

Rogue faction. We need to stabilize him fast!

*The medics work swiftly, bandaging the lizard's wound and preparing for treatment. D and Y hover nearby, anxious and waiting.*

**LIZARD** *(weakly, eyes fluttering)*

Thank you… for saving me…

**D** *(grinning)*

No need to thank us yet! Just hold on, buddy.

*As the medics continue their work, the tension eases slightly, but D and Y remain on alert, knowing the threat is still out there.*

**Y** *(looking to D)*

We've got to keep our eyes peeled. If that rogue faction is still around, we might have more trouble on our hands.

*The camera zooms out, showing the urgent care facility surrounded by lush greenery, a temporary haven amidst the chaos.*

### EXT. URGENT CARE FACILITY – DAY

*As the medics tend to the injured lizard, the atmosphere is tense but hopeful. Suddenly, a loud CRASH echoes through the jungle, and an ALIEN from People-888 bursts through the underbrush, snarling and brandishing a weapon.*

**ALIEN** *(sneering)*

You thought you could hide from us? Not a chance!

*The drones immediately recognize the threat, their systems locking onto the intruder.*

**D** *(voice sharp)*

Shit! We've got company!

**Y** *(preparing for action)*

Get ready to fire!

*The alien lunges toward the lizard, but before it can reach him, D and Y swiftly deploy an RPG from their arms.*

**D** *(steadying his aim)*

Target locked! Fire!

*With a resounding THWUMP, the RPG launches, streaking through the air and striking the alien squarely in the chest. The explosion erupts with a deafening blast, sending debris flying and the alien crumpling to the ground.*

**Y** *(grinning)*

Direct hit!

**D** *(nods, looking at the lizard)*

You okay, buddy?

*The injured lizard looks on, wide-eyed and gasping.*

**LIZARD** *(shocked)*

You saved my life again!

*The medics quickly finish their work, glancing at the fallen alien with a mix of fear and respect.*

**MEDIC LIZARD** *(awestruck)*

You two are something else!

**Y** *(smugly)*

Just doing our job!

*As the dust settles, the drones remain vigilant, scanning the area for more threats.*

**D** *(turning serious)*

We need to fortify this place. If one alien found us, more could come.

*The injured lizard nods, determination flashing in his eyes.*

**LIZARD** *(firmly)*

I'll rally the others. We can't let them take this paradise from us!

*The camera pulls back, showing the urgency of the situation as they prepare to defend their newfound home against any further attacks.*

### EXT. URGENT CARE FACILITY – DAY

*After the attack, the atmosphere shifts from fear to determination. ARYNN, D, and Y gather with the injured lizard and the medics to formulate a plan.*

**ARYNN** *(firmly)*

We need to fortify this place. If they come back, we must be ready.

**LIZARD MEDIC** *(nodding)*

We have some resources nearby. We can use the materials from the jungle.

**Y** *(excitedly)*

Let's build some turrets! We need firepower on our side!

*The team quickly sets to work, gathering materials—wood, stones, and tech parts from the downed alien ship. They design makeshift walls and turrets, working together with urgency.*

**D** *(directing the construction)*

Make sure the turrets have a clear line of sight! We can't let anything sneak up on us again.

*As the walls rise, the drones install automated turrets equipped with blasters, giving the facility a defensive perimeter.*

**LIZARD** *(enthusiastically)*

This will keep us safe!

**ARYNN** *(encouragingly)*

With our combined strength, we'll turn this place into a fortress!

*Hours pass as they labor, the facility transforming into a well-defended stronghold. The final touches are put on the turrets, which hum with energy, ready to fire.*

**Y** *(stepping back to admire their work)*

Not bad for a day's effort!

*As they finish, the sounds of the jungle feel a little less threatening, but they remain cautious.*

**D** *(seriously)*

We've done well, but we can't let our guard down. They'll come for us again.

**ARYNN** *(nodding)*

Then we'll be ready. This land belongs to us now, and we'll protect it.

*With renewed confidence, they gather together, ready to face whatever challenges lie ahead.*

### EXT. URGENT CARE FACILITY – DAY

*With the walls and turrets completed, ARYNN gathers everyone for the next phase of their defense plan. The lizards and drones gather, curiosity sparking in their eyes.*

**ARYNN** *(raising his voice)*

Now that we have our immediate defenses, we need something stronger—something that can protect us from any threat that approaches from space.

**D** *(interested)*

What are you thinking, Arynn?

**ARYNN** *(confidently)*

A force field. One that extends all the way to Lizard-953-E's orbit. With the antimatter from our Dyson sphere, we can create a barrier that destroys anything on contact.

*The crowd buzzes with excitement and disbelief.*

**Y** *(enthusiastically)*

That's a bold move! How do we even start?

**ARYNN** *(pointing to a nearby structure)*

We'll set up a central generator here. Once operational, it will channel the antimatter to create the shield.

*The team rushes to gather the necessary materials, including components from the alien ship and their own technology. They work together to construct the generator.*

**LIZARD ENGINEER** *(focused)*

We need to calibrate the antimatter output carefully. Too much could create a chain reaction!

**D** *(grinning)*

And too little won't do squat!

*After several tense hours of construction and calibration, the generator is ready. They stand back, anticipation crackling in the air.*

**ARYNN** *(focused)*

Activate it!

*With a collective breath, they power on the generator. A low hum resonates through the air, and a shimmering light begins to form, expanding outward.*

**Y** *(eyes wide)*

It's working!

*The force field flickers to life, extending rapidly into the sky, forming a barrier that glows with an ominous energy.*

**ARYNN** *(excitedly)*

This is just the beginning!

*As the field stretches to the orbit of Lizard-953-E, it pulsates with energy, ready to obliterate any threat that dares approach.*

**D** *(looking up)*

And it'll explode anything on contact, right?

**ARYNN** *(grinning)*

Exactly. No more surprises. We stand united now.

*The team cheers, a sense of pride washing over them as they admire their creation.*

**LIZARD** *(raising a fist)*

For Lizard-7759!

*With renewed determination, they know they can face whatever comes next, confident in their defenses.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – NEAR THE URGENT CARE FACILITY – DAY

*As the team begins construction on another hospital, the atmosphere is filled with determination and collaboration. ARYNN oversees the building, ensuring that everything is set up to accommodate future injuries.*

**ARYNN** *(directing)*

Make sure the medical bays are reinforced! We don't want another incident like last time.

*Suddenly, from the dense foliage, a vicious ALIEN from People-888 lunges out, aiming straight for ARYNN.*

**ALIEN** *(snarling)*

You think you can keep us out forever?

*ARYNN barely has time to react as the alien closes in on him.*

**D** *(shouting)*

Arynn! Look out!

*In a flash, one of the drones, quick on its feet, reacts instinctively. It activates its tail, which is filled with Yabitanite—a substance known for its destructive properties.*

**DRONE** *(whirring)*

Engaging threat!

*With a swift motion, the drone swings its tail, slamming it into the alien. The Yabitanite makes contact, dissolving the creature into a grotesque mush.*

**ARYNN** *(watching, impressed)*

Damn! Nice work!

*The remaining lizards and drones freeze for a moment, absorbing the sudden violence.*

**Y** *(grinning)*

That's how we handle business around here!

**ARYNN** *(turning serious)*

We can't let our guard down. This is a reminder that they're still out there.

*As the team regroups, they check for more signs of danger, reinforcing their resolve.*

**LIZARD** *(nervously)*

What if there are more? We need to double our defenses!

**ARYNN** *(steady)*

We will. Let's finish this hospital and then strengthen our perimeter. We're not just surviving; we're thriving.

*With a renewed sense of urgency, they return to work, determined to complete their tasks while staying vigilant against future threats.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – CONSTRUCTION SITE – DAY

*The drones and lizards are still hard at work building the new hospital when the ground rumbles violently. Dust falls from the half-constructed building as a massive alien force approaches. Arynn freezes mid-command, narrowing his eyes.*

**ARYNN**

What the hell is that?

*An entire football field of ALIENS from People-888 emerges over the horizon, surging forward with murderous intent. Their grotesque forms snarl and screech as they charge, armed to the teeth.*

**Y** *(almost laughing)*

You've gotta be shitting me—they're sending the whole damn army!

**D** *(grinning)*

Good. I was getting bored.

**ARYNN** *(shouting)*

Drones, get ready! We've got incoming—big time!

*Plasma fire rains from the sky as the first wave of aliens opens fire, lighting the battlefield in flashes of green and blue. Arynn ducks for cover behind a half-constructed wall as the drones spring into action.*

**Y** *(shouting, charging her weapons)*

Let's turn these fuckers to scrap!

*Y rushes forward, plasma blasts from her arm cannons tearing through the first wave of aliens. Their bodies explode on impact, reduced to shreds by the sheer power of her fire.*

**D** *(laughing maniacally)*

Time to get messy!

*D dodges incoming fire with ease, launching missiles from his arm into the alien ranks. The explosion rocks the field, sending alien limbs and blood flying.*

**ALIEN SOLDIER** *(screaming)*

They're tearing us apart!

*Juliah, her eyes glowing dangerously, steps forward. Her tail, with its mouth at the end, curls and snaps like a living weapon, dripping with venom.*

**JULIAH** *(voice low, lethal)*

I'm done playing nice.

*Juliah charges into the chaos, her tail lashing out. An alien lunges at her, but her tail opens its mouth and sinks its razor-sharp teeth into the alien's leg, tearing it off in a vicious bite. Blood sprays as the alien screams, falling to the ground.*

**ALIEN** *(screaming)*

No—no!

*Juliah grins, watching the life drain from the alien's eyes. Her tail thrashes, lifting the severed leg and devouring it with its grotesque mouth.*

**JULIAH** *(taunting)*

You're next.

*She swings her tail again, the mouth gnashing as it tears into another alien, ripping it apart in seconds.*

**ARYNN** *(catching his breath)*

Thanks, Juliah.

**JULIAH** *(not breaking stride)*

Just doing what I do best.

*Meanwhile, Arynn grabs his plasma gun and dives out from cover. He takes aim, his finger tightening on the trigger. The blue beam of plasma blasts from the barrel, cutting through the air.*

**ARYNN** *(yelling)*

Time to die!

*The beam strikes an alien, vaporizing it instantly. Arynn swings the gun in a wide arc, taking down three more in one swift move, their bodies disintegrating into nothing.*

**Y** *(laughing, covered in blood)*

Holy shit, Arynn—you're a damn machine!

**ARYNN** *(grinning)*

Just keep ‘em off me!

*The aliens, though endless in numbers, are no match for the drones' fury. Explosions rock the field as D and Y launch attacks with brutal precision.*

**ALIEN COMMANDER** *(barking orders)*

Press forward! Don't stop!

*But the drones are relentless. Juliah slashes through the alien ranks, her tail's mouth gnawing at flesh with horrifying efficiency. Arynn vaporizes aliens with each blast of his plasma gun.*

**ALIEN COMMANDER** *(desperation growing)*

Fall back! Retreat!

*As the alien army crumbles, the surviving few limp away, retreating in defeat. The battlefield is a blood-soaked wasteland, littered with the bodies of their fallen.*

**D** *(smirking)*

Guess they couldn't handle the heat.

**JULIAH** *(wiping blood off her tail)*

Pathetic.

*Her tail's mouth snaps shut, content after its feeding.*

**ARYNN** *(surveying the battlefield)*

Good riddance.

*As the dust settles, the team regroups, victorious but aware of the constant threat.*

**Y** *(grinning)*

Hell of a fight. Who's ready for round two?

*The group shares a brief, tired laugh, but Arynn's eyes remain sharp as he looks toward the horizon.*

**ARYNN** *(seriously)*

We need to stay ready. Next time, they'll come back stronger—and so will we.

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – CONSTRUCTION SITE – DAY

*The drones continue to fight off the alien horde, tearing through them like a storm of metal and fury. Plasma fire lights the battlefield, and the ground is drenched in alien blood. In the chaos, Juliah is in her element, cutting down enemies left and right, her tail snapping its mouth open and shut with each kill.*

**JULIAH** *(snarling)*

Come on, you bastards. Let's see what you've got.

*But in the thick of the battle, a towering People-888 alien barrels through the chaos, charging straight for Juliah. This one is larger than the rest, wielding a massive energy axe that crackles with unstable plasma.*

**ALIEN WARRIOR** *(roaring)*

You're mine, bitch!

*Juliah spins to face the threat, her tail whipping around to strike, but the alien is too fast. With a guttural roar, he swings the axe with all his might.*

SLASH—

*In an instant, the axe cleaves through Juliah's neck with a sickening CRACK. Blood sprays as her head flies off, hitting the ground with a wet thud. Her body collapses to the ground, twitching violently as sparks fly from the severed wires in her neck.*

**ALIEN WARRIOR** *(grinning, voice dripping with satisfaction)*

Die, you metal whore!

*There's a moment of silence on the battlefield as the alien looks down at Juliah's beheaded body, his sick grin growing wider. He spits on the ground beside her head, clearly thinking he's won.*

**ALIEN WARRIOR** *(spitting)*

Fucking rust bucket. That'll teach you—

**JULIAH** *(muffled, from the severed head)*

Mother... fucker.

*The alien's grin falters as Juliah's severed head starts to twitch. Her eyes blink back to life, glowing a violent red. A twisted smile stretches across her blood-soaked lips.*

**ALIEN WARRIOR** *(startled)*

What the hell—

*Before the alien can react, Juliah's headless body twitches on the ground, her limbs jerking unnaturally as her neck begins to regenerate. Her headless form stands back up, sparks flying from her neck as new metal and flesh begin to weave together, forming a new neck from the base. The alien steps back, horrified, as her body starts to pull itself back together.*

**ALIEN WARRIOR** *(screaming)*

What the fuck is this—?!

*Juliah's new neck extends upward, growing a new head in seconds, her eyes glowing with hellish intensity. Her grin is wide and wicked.*

**JULIAH** *(snarling)*

Did you really think that would fucking kill me?

*With blinding speed, Juliah lunges forward. Her tail, with its gaping mouth, shoots out and wraps around the alien's throat like a noose. The mouth at the end of her tail bites down savagely, tearing into his flesh.*

**ALIEN WARRIOR** *(gurgling)*

No—NO!

*With a brutal twist, Juliah's tail rips out his throat, sending blood spraying everywhere. The alien stumbles back, clutching his gaping wound, but it's no use. He collapses in a pool of his own blood, eyes wide with terror as his life drains away.*

**JULIAH** *(smirking, wiping blood off her newly-formed head)*

That's what I thought, you miserable piece of shit.

*She steps over the alien's twitching corpse, her head completely regenerated, not a scratch left on her.*

**ARYNN** *(surprised but impressed)*

Juliah, that was… fucking insane.

**JULIAH** *(casually)*

Takes more than a cheap swing to get rid of me.

*Her tail's mouth snaps shut, satisfied with its kill. The battlefield falls silent for a moment, as the remaining aliens stare in horror at what just happened. Then, with renewed fury, the drones continue their assault, ripping through the alien forces with unrelenting savagery.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – CONSTRUCTION SITE – NIGHT

*The battlefield is a mess of scorched earth, burning alien bodies, and shattered structures. The air is thick with the stench of blood and metal. The drones stand victorious, surveying the carnage, but something is different now—the lizards who fought alongside them are shaken.*

**ARYNN** *(speaking into his comms)*

Status report—how many of these bastards are left?

*D and Y continue to clean up, vaporizing the last of the alien stragglers with brutal precision. But while the drones remain relentless, the lizard soldiers begin to falter.*

**LIZARD GENERAL** *(quietly, to Arynn)*

We can't keep doing this… We thought we were ready for this kind of fight, but these… these aliens… They're relentless.

**ARYNN** *(cocking his head)*

What the hell are you talking about?

*The lizard general, his eyes wide with fear, looks over the carnage. The blood of his fallen kin soaks the ground. The battlefield is littered with the dead, and the scent of burning flesh fills the air.*

**LIZARD GENERAL** *(shakily)*

We can't keep fighting like this. We're outmatched. We're… dying out there.

*Arynn looks at him incredulously. Juliah, her freshly regenerated head still dripping with blood, strides over with a dangerous glint in her eye.*

**JULIAH** *(mocking)*

What's the matter? You want to tuck your tail between your legs and hide?

*The lizard general stiffens, clearly terrified of Juliah after watching her regenerate her head mid-battle.*

**LIZARD GENERAL** *(slowly)*

This war… it's not what we signed up for. We were supposed to protect Lizard-953-E. Now we're just fighting to survive. Our numbers are dwindling. We can't afford this anymore.

*Arynn glares, but deep down, he knows the lizard general isn't wrong. The fight has cost them heavily.*

**ARYNN** *(frustrated)*

You're really just gonna give up?

**LIZARD GENERAL** *(pleading)*

We've done enough! Our people… we were never meant to fight wars like this. We're survivors, not conquerors. If we keep going like this, there won't be anyone left to protect Lizard-953-E.

*He takes a deep breath, lowering his head in shame.*

**LIZARD GENERAL** *(softly)*

We… surrender. We'll retreat. We'll go back into hiding, where we belong.

*The other lizards nearby look at each other, clearly conflicted but nodding in agreement. The weight of the battle has broken their spirits.*

**ARYNN** *(sternly)*

You're really just gonna crawl back underground and let them win?

**LIZARD GENERAL** *(quietly)*

It's not about winning anymore. It's about survival.

*Juliah crosses her arms, disgusted, but doesn't argue. She smirks darkly, stepping forward, her presence alone enough to make the lizards cower.*

**JULIAH** *(smirking)*

Fine. Run and hide like the spineless reptiles you are. We'll handle the rest.

*The lizard general bows his head, defeated, and the remaining lizard soldiers silently begin their retreat, disappearing into the darkness. The once-proud warriors return to their subterranean shelters, leaving the drones to finish the fight.*

**D** *(watching them go)*

Hmph. Can't say I'm surprised.

**Y** *(bitterly)*

Fucking cowards.

**ARYNN** *(softly)*

It's not cowardice. They're just trying to survive.

*He watches the lizards retreat, his expression unreadable. A heavy silence falls over the battlefield.*

**JULIAH** *(coldly)*

Survival's for the strong. Let them rot in their caves if that's what they want.

*The drones turn their backs on the retreating lizards, refocusing their efforts on the fight that lies ahead.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – CONSTRUCTION SITE – NIGHT

*The remaining drones stand amidst the chaos, the battlefield stretching out before them. Despite the lizard forces retreating, the People-888 aliens regroup, mounting a furious counterattack. Plasma bolts streak across the night sky, cutting through the rubble and sending the drones scrambling for cover.*

**Y** *(ducking behind debris)*

They're closing in! We won't hold them off much longer!

**ARYNN** *(gritting his teeth)*

We need a way out—now!

*Juliah, bloodied but standing firm, glances around at the approaching wave of enemies. Her eyes glow fiercely, and a dangerous smirk tugs at her lips. The K̵̛̲̬͍̦̉̉̚͝ͅð̸̩̰̬̪͇̏̈́̈́͊͒k̶̬͙͔͚̪̄͗̆͂̆ṉ̴͓̃̈͛͐̏̏͜ͅͅk̴̛͔̯̖̻͖̋̑̋͊µ̷̢͙̙̩̳͐̔̀̓͋å abilities she had kept in check begin to stir inside her, dark tendrils of energy sparking to life around her.*

**JULIAH** *(cold, focused)*

You want time to escape? I'll give you time.

*She steps forward, raising her hand. Her fingers twitch as glitching energy crackles around her palm, distorting the air with violent, digital flickers. The air around her warps, the surrounding terrain twisting and bending unnaturally. The alien soldiers charging toward them begin to slow, as though reality itself is being bent under Juliah's control.*

**ALIEN COMMANDER** *(from the distance)*

Keep pushing forward! They can't hold us off forever!

*But Juliah doesn't flinch. With a smirk, she flicks her wrist forward, releasing the built-up energy in a massive shockwave of raw, destructive power.*

**JULIAH** *(voice distorting with energy)*

K̵̛̲̬͍̦̉̉̚͝ͅFUCK OFF!

*The ground beneath the alien soldiers rips apart, and the shockwave slams into them with the force of a tidal wave. The air distorts, and the aliens are thrown dozens of yards backward, their bodies flung like ragdolls. The closest ones are vaporized instantly, torn apart by the sheer power of the attack. Others slam into the ground, their armor shattered, blood pooling around them.*

**ALIEN SOLDIER 1** *(screaming as he's thrown back)*

GAAAAH—!

**ALIEN SOLDIER 2** *(coughing up blood)*

What… the hell… was that…?

*The remaining aliens stagger to their feet, utterly disoriented, their forces now in disarray. The shockwave has bought the drones precious time, the battlefield now cleared of enemies in their immediate vicinity.*

**D** *(grinning)*

Holy shit. That was a hell of a knockback!

**Y** *(nods, reloading a plasma rifle)*

You bought us some time, but we need to move now!

**ARYNN** *(commanding)*

Fall back to the next sector! We'll regroup there and prepare for another strike.

*The drones quickly rally, their escape path now clear thanks to Juliah's devastating attack. She stands at the front, eyes still glowing with residual power, her body humming with the aftershocks of the K̵̛̲̬͍̦̉̉̚͝ͅð̸̩̰̬̪͇̏̈́̈́͊͒k̶̬͙͔͚̪̄͗̆͂̆ṉ̴͓̃̈͛͐̏̏͜ͅͅk̴̛͔̯̖̻͖̋̑̋͊µ̷̢͙̙̩̳͐̔̀̓͋å.*

**JULIAH** *(smirking, voice low)*

That'll slow them down. Let's get out of here before they regroup.

*The drones retreat into the shadows, their escape now secured. Behind them, the shattered remains of the alien forces struggle to recover, giving the team precious moments to regroup and plan their next move.*

### INT. LIZARD-953-E UNDERGROUND BUNKER – REGENERATION CHAMBER

*The chamber is cold and industrial, filled with dark, mechanical equipment. The Disassembly Drones, Arynn, D, Y, and Juliah, resembling Solver Uzi, enter the regeneration room. Their black, insectoid bodies glisten with oil and damage. Glowing red eyes flicker as they scan the room, heavy with battle scars.*

**ARYNN** *(cold and clinical, voice distorted like a disassembly drone)*

We need full restoration. That fight took more out of us than expected.

*D limps forward, his razor-edged wings sparking. His robotic arms drag as hydraulic fluid leaks from his core. He chuckles, despite the pain.*

**D** *(joking)*

Yeah, I think I lost something important back there. Like my spleen. If I had one.

**Y** *(holding his dislocated insect-like arm)*

Still functional… but only just.

*Juliah stands at the back, her solver energy barely keeping her upright. Her eyes glow with symbols of K̵̛̲̬͍̦̉̉̚͝ͅð̸̩̰̬̪͇̏̈́̈́͊͒k̶̬͙͔͚̪̄͗̆͂̆ṉ̴͓̃̈͛͐̏̏͜ͅͅk̴̛͔̯̖̻͖̋̑̋͊µ̷̢͙̙̩̳͐̔̀̓͋å̵̰̻͙̳͙̇̂͌͑͗. She inspects her flesh-like tail, which writhes unnaturally, the mouth at the end biting the air.*

**JULIAH** *(smirking, but exhausted)*

Would hate to lose this thing. It's got a mind of its own.

*They move toward the regeneration pods, dark machines designed to reconstruct their fractured forms. The pods crack open with a hiss, revealing swirling nanites, ready to repair the damage. Each drone steps inside.*

**ARYNN** *(mechanical and calculated)*

Regenerate us. We've got a planet to tear apart.

*The pods scan their bodies, and black nanites begin their work. Inside the pods, the Disassembly Drones are restored—metal plating reforges, wings straighten, and their razor limbs regrow with a metallic shine. Hydraulic systems reconnect and power up, filling the chamber with an ominous hum.*

**D** *(relaxed as his wings regenerate)*

Ahh, nothing like some good ol' self-repair.

*Juliah, inside her pod, watches as the solver energy courses through her. Her flesh-like tail, covered in skin, pulses and regenerates, the mouth at the end snarling as it grows sharper. The nanites swirl around her form, reconstructing her disassembly drone body.*

**Y** *(cracking his new arm back into place)*

Feels good to be back in one piece.

**JULIAH** *(grinning wickedly)*

I'm not just back… I'm better.

*Juliah steps out, her solver powers fully restored. Her flesh tail twitches behind her, the mouth snapping as if it hungers for destruction. Her eyes glow with the symbols of K̵̛̲̬͍̦̉̉̚͝ͅð̸̩̰̬̪͇̏̈́̈́͊͒k̶̬͙͔͚̪̄͗̆͂̆ṉ̴͓̃̈͛͐̏̏͜ͅͅk̴̛͔̯̖̻͖̋̑̋͊µ̷̢͙̙̩̳͐̔̀̓͋å̵̰̻͙̳͙̇̂͌͑͗.*

**ARYNN** *(stepping out, fully restored)*

Good. There's more work to do, and we can't afford to be anything less than perfect.

*The Disassembly Drones, now fully repaired, stand together. Their metallic claws gleam under the low light, and Juliah's Solver energy pulsates with dangerous intent.*

**JULIAH** *(playfully, with a wicked grin)*

Hope the next wave is ready. ‘Cause I sure am.

*They turn toward the exit, their deadly wings unfurling. The sound of clanking metal and the hum of Solver energy fill the air as they prepare for the battle to continue.*

### INT. LIZARD-953-E UNDERGROUND BUNKER – COMMAND CENTER

*The drones gather around a central holographic projector displaying a vibrant image of Lizard-7759, lush and thriving under the light of its moons, Luna and Astra. Arynn stands at the helm, his form illuminated by the glow of the projector.*

**ARYNN** *(voice steady and resonant)*

You've all fought hard, but there's something you need to understand about our world—and my purpose.

*The drones listen intently, their mechanical forms reflecting the light. Juliah leans closer, her tail flicking with curiosity.*

**ARYNN**

I wasn't always the Lizard King. Long ago, I was a mere scientist, obsessed with the idea of transforming barren rock into thriving ecosystems. I worked on Lizard-7759 and another planet, Mül, with nothing but the ambition to create life where there was none.

*The holographic image shifts to show Mül, a desolate world now bursting with greenery and alien life.*

**ARYNN**

By harnessing advanced terraforming technologies, I could manipulate atmospheres, control climates, and even introduce new species. I adapted the ecosystems to balance themselves, allowing them to flourish.

*He pauses, gazing at the images, his expression somber.*

**ARYNN**

But it came at a cost. When the People from People-888 discovered my work, they wanted to control it. They believed it would grant them dominance over us and the resources of the universe. They came to take what they thought was rightfully theirs.

*The drones exchange glances, understanding dawning on them.*

**D**

So, these "People" are really just a bunch of overreaching aliens?

**ARYNN**

Exactly. They think of themselves as humans, but they're anything but. They've lost their connection to the universe, reduced to greedy beings, exploiting everything in their path. They're the reason we've had to fight so hard to protect our worlds.

*The projector now displays the Corrupted AI, a twisted visage of what once was advanced technology, a remnant of their previous conflicts.*

**ARYNN**

Now, I must reclaim what's ours, and we can't allow them to twist our efforts into something destructive. We will protect our planets—Lizard-7759, Mül, and Lizard-953-E—from their clutches.

*Juliah's eyes flare with determination, her tail twitching.*

**JULIAH**

Then let's give them hell. We'll show them the true power of our terraforming!

*Arynn nods, a fire igniting in his gaze.*

**ARYNN**

Together, we'll build a future where our worlds can thrive, free from the threat of the People from People-888.

*The drones, fueled by Arynn's passion, prepare for the battles ahead, their resolve strengthened.*

### INT. LIZARD-953-E UNDERGROUND BUNKER – STRATEGY ROOM

*The atmosphere is tense as Arynn stands before the drones, the holographic display flickering with images of the People. The drones listen intently, their mechanical bodies humming with anticipation.*

**ARYNN** *(voice dripping with disdain)*

Look at them—the People from People-888. They prance around like they own the universe, but just look at their faces! They've got features like a melted candle mixed with bad decisions.

*The hologram shows the People in various poses, their features exaggerated and grotesque.*

**ARYNN** *(laughing bitterly)*

Their skin looks like it's been through a meat grinder, and don't get me started on their fashion sense. Who the hell thought neon spandex was a good idea? It's like they're trying to blind us with their sheer ugliness!

*The drones chuckle, shaking their heads at the absurdity of the images. Juliah, however, is busy flexing her tail, looking a little too relaxed.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

At least they can't out-style me. This tail's got more personality than their entire species!

*Suddenly, an alien lunges from the shadows, a grotesque creature from the People-888. It slashes at Juliah, and her tail goes flying across the room.*

**JULIAH** *(shocked, with exaggerated flair)*

What the actual fuck?! My tail! That was my favorite part!

*The room erupts in laughter, even Arynn can't help but crack a smile.*

**ARYNN** *(trying to regain composure)*

That's what you get for showing off! Don't worry; I've seen worse get fixed. We'll just slap a new one on you—better and sharper!

*Juliah's mouth on her tail seems to twitch in annoyance as she picks it up, her eyes sparkling with mischief.*

**JULIAH** *(holding her severed tail)*

I swear, if this thing regenerates with a mind of its own, I'm naming it after you, Arynn!

*The laughter continues as they prepare for the next phase of their mission, united in their resolve to fight against the People—though perhaps a bit more lighthearted after the banter.*

### INT. LIZARD-953-E UNDERGROUND BUNKER – STRATEGY ROOM

*The laughter subsides as Juliah holds her severed tail, but in moments, something incredible happens. The tail begins to glow softly, pulsing with energy. In front of the drones' astonished eyes, it regenerates right back onto her body.*

**JULIAH** *(eyes wide with excitement)*

Holy crap! It's back! That's some serious regeneration magic right there!

*The tail slithers back into place, complete with its mouth, looking as if nothing had happened.*

**ARYNN** *(shaking his head, amused)*

You've always been one to bounce back. It's almost impressive how resilient you are, even if you have a tendency to show off!

*As the banter continues, Arynn's expression shifts to something more serious as he recalls the history of the People from People-888.*

**ARYNN** *(somberly)*

But let's not forget what we're really up against. The People... they weren't always like this. Once, they were a thriving civilization, but their hunger for power twisted them. They abandoned their own ethics, turning on each other in their quest for dominance.

*The hologram shifts to a timeline, depicting the rise and fall of the People.*

**ARYNN**

They became obsessed with technology and resources, exploiting their own kind, then extending that cruelty to other worlds. When they discovered terraforming, they didn't see a way to create life; they saw a way to control it. They're like vultures, picking at the bones of the universe, and I can't stand them.

*The drones listen, their mechanical faces hardening with resolve.*

**ARYNN**

I thought I could reason with them once. I thought maybe they'd see the value in cooperation, in sharing. But all they wanted was to take and take until there was nothing left. They'd wipe out entire ecosystems for their twisted version of progress.

*Juliah, now fully re-armed, speaks up with determination.*

**JULIAH**

Then let's give them what they deserve! We'll show them they can't just take whatever they want. They're going to learn the hard way that we're not just their next target—we're a force to be reckoned with!

*Arynn nods, pride glimmering in his eyes as the drones rally around him, fueled by the fire of their shared purpose.*

**ARYNN**

Together, we'll fight for our homes, our ecosystems, and each other. They may have their technology, but we have our hearts—and that's more powerful than they could ever understand.

*With renewed vigor, they prepare for the battles ahead, ready to defend their world and push back against the People from People-888.*

### EXT. LIZARD-953-E – CONSTRUCTION SITE – NIGHT

*The atmosphere outside is charged with anticipation. The lizards and drones gather, their numbers swelling as Arynn stands before them, rallying the troops. The glowing lights of the construction site cast eerie shadows on the alien terrain.*

**ARYNN** *(voice booming)*

Listen up! The People think they can take what's ours without consequence. They've underestimated our resolve, our strength! Look at your comrades around you! We are the guardians of this world, and we will not let them destroy our home!

*Cheers erupt from the lizards, their eyes glowing with determination. The drones' mechanical joints whir with excitement as they prepare for battle.*

**LIZARD WARRIOR** *(raising a weapon)*

Let's show these ugly bastards what real strength looks like!

*Suddenly, a signal blares from the perimeter—an entire football field of aliens from People-888 approaches, ready to swarm. Their grotesque forms lumber forward, fueled by their own twisted greed.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning, tail flicking)*

Time to turn these idiots into a fine mist! Who's with me?!

*The lizards roar in unison, a primal battle cry that echoes through the night. They charge forward, the drones flying overhead, their weapons primed and ready.*

**ARYNN** *(with fiery determination)*

Let's eviscerate them! For Lizard-953-E!

*The clash begins. The lizards leap into the fray, their claws and teeth finding purchase in the alien flesh. Drones unleash a barrage of energy blasts, tearing through the ranks of the approaching horde.*

**JULIAH** *(biting into an alien limb)*

Tastes like regret! Keep pushing forward!

*The air fills with the sounds of chaos—screams, roars, and the crackle of energy weapons. Juliah uses her tail to whip through the air, severing limbs with brutal efficiency, while drones deploy explosives that scatter the enemy.*

*The battle reaches a fever pitch as the drones execute synchronized attacks, using their advanced abilities to overwhelm the aliens. Gravity wells slow the enemy down while holographic decoys confuse them.*

**ARYNN** *(slicing through an alien with his weapon)*

They wanted a fight, and we'll give them a war! No more hiding!

*The lizards rally around Arynn, their numbers overwhelming the remaining aliens. A final push sends the remaining foes scrambling, panic spreading through their ranks as they realize the tide has turned.*

**JULIAH** *(laughing, catching her breath)*

Looks like they underestimated our ugly, beautiful fury!

*As the last of the aliens falls, the battlefield is left littered with remnants of the fight, the victory a testament to their strength and unity.*

*Arynn stands amidst the chaos, surveying the scene with pride.*

**ARYNN**

We fought not just for survival, but for our world. Together, we'll ensure they never threaten us again!

*The drones and lizards roar in agreement, their spirits invigorated by their shared triumph as they prepare for the battles that lie ahead.*

### EXT. LIZARD-953-E – BATTLEFIELD – NIGHT

*The battlefield is a cacophony of chaos, with explosions lighting up the night sky. Arynn and the drones charge forward, cutting a swath through the invading aliens. The air is thick with the smell of burning flesh and the cries of the dying.*

**ARYNN** *(yelling over the chaos)*

They thought they could just roll in here and take what's ours! Let's fucking show them what we're made of!

*Juliah swings her tail, a wicked grin spreading across her face as she sends an alien flying. The creature crashes into the ground with a sickening thud.*

**JULIAH** *(smirking)*

One less ugly bastard to worry about! Who's next?

*A wave of aliens surges forward, but the drones are relentless, firing plasma bolts that explode on impact, sending limbs and viscera flying.*

**Y** *(cackling as it fires)*

This is what happens when you mess with the wrong species! Eat shit!

*As an alien lunges at Arynn, he sidesteps and cleaves it in two, blood spraying everywhere.*

**ARYNN** *(shouting)*

You really thought you could take me down? You're all nothing but fodder!

*The lizards are equally fierce, tearing into the aliens with claws and teeth, reveling in the brutality. One lizard leaps onto an alien's back, sinking its teeth into its neck.*

**LIZARD WARRIOR** *(snarling)*

How's this for a fucking welcome party?

*Juliah spots a large group of aliens trying to regroup and lets out a battle cry.*

**JULIAH** *(pulling out a plasma grenade)*

Time to turn up the heat, you pathetic sacks of shit!

*She hurls the grenade into the cluster of aliens. The explosion is deafening, obliterating everything in its vicinity, and a cloud of smoke and gore fills the air.*

**D** *(laughing maniacally)*

I love this job! Just look at them scatter like roaches!

*The tide of battle shifts as Arynn rallies the lizards and drones for one final push.*

**ARYNN** *(raising his weapon high)*

Finish them! We'll send a message they'll never forget!

*As they surge forward, the remaining aliens falter, fear etched across their faces. One tries to escape, but Juliah darts in, cutting it down.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

Not so fast, asshole! You think you can run?

*With a final roar, the lizards and drones decimate the last remnants of the enemy, leaving the battlefield quiet, save for the sounds of their victory.*

*Arynn stands among the carnage, panting but triumphant.*

**ARYNN** *(looking around at the devastation)*

This is our home, and we will not let anyone take it from us! Not now, not ever!

*The lizards and drones cheer, their spirits soaring as they revel in the aftermath of their fierce resistance.*

### EXT. PEOPLE-888 – ALIEN LANDSCAPE – NIGHT

*The atmosphere shifts as Arynn and his team arrive on the desolate, industrial wasteland of People-888. The air is thick with smog, and the landscape is littered with the remnants of failed terraforming projects. The sky is choked with dark clouds, reflecting the greed of its inhabitants.*

**ARYNN** *(eyes narrowed, scanning the horizon)*

This place is a shithole. It's like they took everything we've built and turned it into a nightmare.

*Juliah flexes her tail, ready for action.*

**JULIAH** *(enthusiastically)*

Let's find their leader and wipe that smug grin off their face! I want to see the look on their ugly mug when they realize we're here to ruin their day!

*The drones fly overhead, their sensors scanning for any signs of life. They detect a strong signal coming from a towering fortress in the distance.*

**D** *(excitedly)*

We've got a lock on the leader's location! Looks like they're holed up in that monstrosity.

**ARYNN** *(nodding)*

Good. Let's move. We'll show them what happens when you mess with Lizard-953-E!

*As they approach the fortress, the ground trembles beneath their feet. The structure looms ominously, guarded by a battalion of the People's soldiers. Arynn signals for the team to stop.*

**ARYNN** *(whispering)*

We need a plan. We can't just charge in there. They'll be waiting for us.

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

I say we create a distraction! Let me use the [ʣʤ] command and summon a Black hole in their defenses. They won't know what hit them!

*Arynn considers her suggestion, then nods.*

**ARYNN**

Alright, Juliah. You create chaos, and we'll flank them from the sides. Remember, we're after their leader, not just a fight.

*Juliah prepares her weapon, her eyes gleaming with mischief.*

**JULIAH** *(smirk)*

Time to give these bastards a show they won't forget!

*With a fierce battle cry, Juliah launches herself forward, blasting through the main gates of the fortress. Explosions erupt as guards scramble in a panic.*

**ARYNN** *(yelling)*

Now's our chance! Move out!

*The drones and lizards charge in behind her, weaving through the chaos as they cut down the guards. The fortress echoes with shouts and the sounds of battle.*

**ARYNN** *(voice steady)*

Stay focused! We're not just here to fight; we're here to end this!

*As they press deeper into the fortress, they push through wave after wave of resistance, moving closer to the leader's chamber.*

*Finally, they burst through a reinforced door, entering a lavishly decorated chamber that stands in stark contrast to the rest of the fortress.*

**ARYNN** *(breathless)*

This must be it. The heart of their operations.

*At the far end of the room stands the LEADER OF THE PEOPLE, an imposing figure with a twisted grin.*

**LEADER** *(mockingly)*

Ah, the infamous Arynn! You think you can just barge in here and take me down? You're in way over your head!

**ARYNN** *(stepping forward)*

You've caused enough pain and destruction. It ends here, you bastard!

*The confrontation is set, the air thick with tension as they prepare for the final showdown.*

### INT. PEOPLE-888 – LEADER'S CHAMBER – NIGHT

*As Arynn and his team stand poised for battle, the LEADER of the People smirks, clearly unfazed by their presence.*

**LEADER** *(tauntingly)*

You think you can just walk in here and threaten me? Allow me to demonstrate why you're nothing but a nuisance!

*With a swift motion, the Leader pulls a massive, wrinkled sack from behind his desk. It's crudely designed but looks deceptively sturdy.*

**ARYNN** *(confused)*

What the hell is that?

**LEADER** *(grinning maliciously)*

A little surprise! Enjoy!

*He hurls the sack toward Arynn and the drones. It sails through the air, landing with a heavy thud and quickly enveloping the group. The sack constricts around them, made from a tough, kevlar-like material that resists their weapons.*

**JULIAH** *(panicking)*

What the—? I can't cut through this shit!

*The drones unleash a barrage of plasma blasts at the sack, but it holds firm, absorbing the impacts without a scratch.*

**ARYNN** *(gritting his teeth)*

Stay calm! We need to think our way out of this!

**Y** *(frantic)*

This is not how I wanted to die! Come on, we're supposed to be unstoppable!

*As they struggle against the tight confines of the sack, the Leader approaches, a triumphant smile plastered across his face.*

**LEADER** *(laughing)*

You see? All your bravado, all your talk of strength, and yet here you are, trapped like little rats! You underestimated me, and now you'll pay the price!

*Arynn grits his teeth, trying to assess their options. His mind races as he glances at his team, their movements restricted.*

**ARYNN** *(breathing heavily)*

Juliah, can you use your tail? Maybe we can find a weak point!

**JULIAH** *(straining)*

I'll try! If I can just get enough leverage—

*She wriggles her tail, searching for a way to break free. The sack shifts but holds tight.*

**ARYNN** *(voice rising)*

We're not done yet! We've come too far to let this bastard win!

*Suddenly, with a burst of energy, Arynn channels all his strength, pushing against the confines of the sack. The pressure creates a small gap.*

**ARYNN** *(urgently)*

Everyone! Push together!

*The drones and Juliah strain against the material, forcing it to give way. Slowly, the kevlar-like fabric starts to stretch, inch by inch.*

**JULIAH** *(gritting her teeth)*

Come on, come on!

*With one final effort, they all push together, the sack bursting open and sending them sprawling across the floor.*

**LEADER** *(shocked)*

What?! No! How is that possible?!

**ARYNN** *(catching his breath, standing tall)*

You underestimated us again. We're not just a bunch of trapped lizards and drones—we're a force of nature!

*With renewed determination, they rise to their feet, ready to confront the Leader once more.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – TROPICAL PARADISE – DAY

*After the chaotic events on People-888, Arynn, Juliah, and the drones soar through the clear blue sky, finally landing on the lush shores of Lizard-7759. The vibrant greens and blues of the tropical landscape contrast sharply with the destruction they just left behind.*

**ARYNN** *(sighing with relief)*

We made it. No more running for a while.

*Juliah stretches her limbs, a playful grin on her face.*

**JULIAH** *(laughing)*

And no more ugly bastards trying to trap us! Let's enjoy this paradise before we have to deal with that shit again.

*As they walk along the beach, they spot their human friends, who are setting up a gathering area with colorful banners and food. The atmosphere is relaxed, a stark contrast to the recent chaos.*

**HUMAN FRIEND** *(waving enthusiastically)*

Hey! You made it back! How did it go?

**ARYNN** *(shrugging)*

Let's just say the People underestimated us, but it was a hell of a fight. We'll have to go back and finish what we started.

*The humans exchange worried glances, but Arynn quickly adds a reassuring smile.*

**ARYNN**

But for now, we're safe. Time to celebrate!

*The group gathers around a makeshift fire pit, where food is being prepared. The sound of laughter fills the air as they share stories of their recent adventures.*

**JULIAH** *(chuckling)*

You should've seen the Leader's face when we busted out of that sack. Priceless!

**D** *(enthusiastically)*

And the way we turned the tide! I thought we were done for, but we showed them!

*The humans listen intently, captivated by the tales of bravery and chaos, the camaraderie between the lizards and drones evident in their banter.*

**HUMAN FRIEND** *(smiling)*

You guys are incredible! It's like you were born for this kind of stuff.

**ARYNN** *(grinning)*

We're not just fighting for ourselves; we're fighting for everyone who can't fight back. But for now, let's enjoy the peace.

*As the sun begins to set, casting golden hues across the horizon, they all sit together, sharing food and laughter, their bond stronger than ever.*

**JULIAH** *(raising a drink)*

To Lizard-7759, and to kicking ass when we need to!

**ALL** *(cheering)*

To Lizard-7759!

*The camera pans out, capturing the idyllic scene of unity and peace, a brief respite before the storm they know will inevitably come again.*

### EXT. PEOPLE-888 – ABANDONED INDUSTRIAL ZONE – NIGHT

*The desolate landscape of People-888 is quiet, save for the distant rumble of the remaining machinery. The LEADER, visibly frustrated after the encounter with Arynn and his team, stumbles through the wreckage, muttering curses under his breath.*

**LEADER** *(grumbling)*

Those damn lizards and their flying tin cans... I'll show them! There has to be a way to turn the tide in my favor.

*Suddenly, he spots an unusual shimmer in the air ahead—a rift, swirling with vibrant colors, pulsating like a living thing. He blinks, stepping closer, curiosity piqued.*

**LEADER** *(smirking)*

What's this? A way to escape, perhaps? Or a weapon to unleash chaos?

*As he reaches the rift, he realizes it's wider than he expected. With a greedy grin, he steps forward, trying to squeeze himself through.*

**LEADER** *(cackling)*

Just a little further...

*But as he pushes, he quickly discovers he's stuck, the rift barely large enough for him to fit. He squirms and struggles, but his bulk proves a significant obstacle.*

**LEADER** *(panicking)*

No, no, NO! This can't be happening! I'm too fabulous for this!

*Suddenly, a drone patrol, still surveying the area, spots him flailing in the rift.*

**T** *(over comms)*

Uh, Arynn? You might want to see this. Looks like the Leader's found a new... predicament.

*The drone's camera zooms in, revealing the Leader's legs kicking wildly as he tries to free himself.*

**ARYNN** *(on a nearby screen, chuckling)*

What a sight! I guess he didn't think this through.

*The drones and lizards share a laugh as they gather around to witness the spectacle.*

**JULIAH** *(giggling)*

Should we help him, or just enjoy the show?

**ARYNN** *(grinning)*

Let's give him a minute. He deserves this for all the trouble he's caused.

*Back at the rift, the Leader finally manages to pause, realizing he's being watched. He looks back, face turning red with embarrassment.*

**LEADER** *(voice shaky)*

This is a temporary setback! Just wait until I—

*But he can't finish his sentence as he finds himself tugged at odd angles, the rift refusing to cooperate.*

**LEADER** *(whining)*

I'm not stuck; I'm just... testing the limits!

*The laughter continues, a mix of camaraderie and amusement as they revel in the Leader's moment of humiliation.*

### EXT. PEOPLE-888 – ABANDONED INDUSTRIAL ZONE – NIGHT

*The LEADER continues to struggle against the rift, his face flushed with frustration and embarrassment. With every squirm, the rift seems to taunt him, refusing to yield.*

**LEADER** *(defeated)*

This is ridiculous! I can't be outsmarted by a damn rift!

*He looks around, realizing the drones and lizards are watching him with amused expressions. The laughter echoes around him, adding to his humiliation.*

**LEADER** *(sighing heavily)*

Alright, alright! Maybe this isn't my moment.

*With a dramatic flourish, he throws his arms up in surrender, trying to maintain some semblance of dignity.*

**LEADER** *(muttering)*

I didn't need this rift anyway... I'm too important for this nonsense!

*He takes a deep breath, finally acknowledging his reality. He takes a step back, attempting to ease himself away from the rift.*

**LEADER** *(grumbling)*

Stupid cosmic anomalies! Just you wait; I'll find a way to make this work!

*The rift shimmers slightly as if mocking him, and with one last huff, he turns and stomps away, his heavy footsteps echoing through the desolate landscape.*

**LEADER** *(sulkily)*

I'll regroup. I'll find a way to get back at those lizards. They won't laugh at me for long!

*As he retreats, the drones and lizards can't help but chuckle, watching him disappear into the shadows of the ruined city.*

**ARYNN** *(shaking his head, still amused)*

That was priceless. He might be dangerous, but he's certainly not the brightest bulb.

**JULIAH** *(laughing)*

He'll be back. You can't keep a good villain down... or a stubborn one, for that matter.

*They share a laugh as they prepare to leave the area, knowing they've won this round, but the battle is far from over.*

### INT. LIZARD-7759 – CAMPFIRE – NIGHT

*The atmosphere is relaxed as Arynn, Juliah, and the drones gather around the flickering flames, the sounds of the tropical night surrounding them. Arynn looks contemplative, breaking the comfortable silence.*

**ARYNN** *(serious tone)*

You know, sometimes I can't shake the feeling of what happened back on Copper 9.

*Juliah nods, her expression turning somber.*

**JULIAH**

Yeah. Those People—those ugly bastards—wiped it off the map. They didn't just destroy a planet; they erased countless lives.

**DRONE A** *(quietly)*

We drifted for eons after that, didn't we? Just wandering through space, hoping to find a new home.

**ARYNN** *(nods)*

It was brutal. For years, we were just... lost.

*Juliah glances up at the stars, a distant look in her eyes.*

**JULIAH**

I remember it well. After Copper 9 fell, I was one of the few left. It took me over five hundred years to find anything worth holding onto. I stumbled upon Lizard-953-E, and it felt like fate.

*Arynn leans in, intrigued.*

**ARYNN**

You came here when I was just a juvenile, huh? What was it like for you back then?

**JULIAH** *(smirking)*

Wild. I landed on a planet filled with potential and creatures I couldn't wait to learn about. But it was lonely, and I was still figuring myself out.

**Y** *(teasingly)*

And now look at you! From lost drone to a badass warrior.

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

Well, it wasn't all bad. I might've drifted for ages, but those experiences shaped who I am now. And then, finding you all? It was like finding a family.

*Arynn's expression softens, reflecting on the bond they've formed.*

**ARYNN**

And we're stronger for it. Together, we can stand against the People and whatever else comes our way.

*The fire crackles, and for a moment, they all feel a sense of unity, their shared past binding them together even tighter.*

**JULIAH** *(toasting her drink)*

To new beginnings and kicking ass together!

**ALL** *(cheering)*

To new beginnings!

*They clink their drinks together, the shadows of their pasts lingering but not overshadowing the hope for the future.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – BEACH – NIGHT

*The group moves from the campfire to the soft, warm sands of the beach. The stars twinkle overhead, and the atmosphere is calm and serene. They lie back, gazing up at the sky as the first meteors streak across the darkness.*

**ARYNN** *(relaxed)*

You know, meteor showers are pretty common on Lizard-953-E because of its gravity. It pulls in a lot of debris.

*Juliah shifts beside him, her eyes wide with wonder as a bright meteor blazes overhead, leaving a trail of shimmering light.*

**JULIAH** *(amazed)*

It's beautiful! I could watch this all night.

**T** *(playfully)*

And here I thought we'd only see explosions from battles, not from the sky!

*They all chuckle, watching as more meteors enter the atmosphere, each one illuminating the night with brilliant colors.*

**ARYNN** *(grinning)*

Yeah, this is a much better show than what we usually deal with. Just look at them dance!

*As they continue to gaze up, Arynn shares more about the planet.*

**ARYNN**

You see that cluster? Those are likely fragments from a larger comet. Lizard-953-E gets a fair share of cosmic visitors, but it's also what makes it unique. The gravity helps maintain a vibrant ecosystem.

*Juliah turns her head to look at him, curiosity sparkling in her eyes.*

**JULIAH**

So, every time we see a meteor shower, it's like nature's fireworks?

**ARYNN**

Exactly! It reminds us that even in chaos, beauty exists.

*They lie back in comfortable silence, the sounds of the waves crashing softly against the shore as more meteors streak across the sky.*

**Y** *(sighing contentedly)*

This is the life. No battles, just us and the universe.

**JULIAH** *(smiling)*

We deserve moments like this. After everything we've faced, it feels good to just... be.

*As another meteor blazes across the sky, they all share a collective moment of awe, feeling a renewed sense of purpose and connection.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – BEACH – NIGHT

*As the group continues to marvel at the meteor shower, Juliah suddenly sits up, her eyes narrowing at something streaking through the sky.*

**JULIAH** *(excitedly)*

Hey! Look over there!

*The others follow her gaze, spotting an unusual object hurtling downward—a sleek, fighter-jet-like craft spiraling out of control.*

**ARYNN** *(alarmed)*

What the hell is that?

*With a loud CRASH, the craft lands just beyond the beach, sending up a cloud of sand and debris. The group jumps to their feet, ready for anything.*

**D** *(warily)*

It could be hostile. We should approach with caution.

*As they move closer, the dust settles, revealing the wrecked jet. The hatch pops open, and out stumbles a short, cute little alien. It has big eyes, a round face, and a body reminiscent of the Gek from No Man's Sky, complete with greenish skin and an oversized helmet.*

**JULIAH** *(eyes widening)*

What the—? Look at that little guy!

*The alien shakes its head, disoriented but unharmed, and then looks up at the group with wide, innocent eyes.*

**ARYNN** *(amused)*

Is it... smiling?

*The alien lets out a series of high-pitched chirps, as if trying to communicate, its small arms flailing excitedly.*

**T** *(tilting its head)*

I think it's friendly.

**JULIAH** *(laughing)*

I mean, how could you not love that face?

*The little alien takes a few tentative steps toward them, then suddenly trips over its own feet, landing face-first in the sand.*

**ARYNN** *(chuckling)*

Careful there! You'll get buried!

*The alien pops back up, brushing off the sand, looking unfazed. It resumes its excited chirping, pointing back to the wrecked ship.*

**JULIAH** *(leaning closer)*

What do you think it wants?

*The alien pulls out a small, shiny object from its pocket—an unusual device that sparkles in the moonlight. It holds it out, as if offering it to Juliah.*

**ARYNN** *(interested)*

Maybe it's a peace offering?

*Juliah carefully reaches out to take the object, her curiosity piqued.*

**JULIAH** *(smirking)*

Well, this night just got a lot more interesting!

*As the group gathers around the little alien, laughter and excitement fill the air, the night taking an unexpected turn filled with new possibilities.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – BEACH – NIGHT

*The little alien hops excitedly as Juliah examines the shiny object. After a moment, he straightens up, looking determined to communicate.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(chirpy voice)*

Gek! Gek!

*The group exchanges puzzled glances.*

**ARYNN** *(leaning closer)*

What's a "Gek"?

*The alien points to himself with pride.*

**GEK ALIEN**

Gek! I am Gek! My home world... destroyed!

*He gestures dramatically, mimicking an explosion with his tiny arms, his big eyes filled with a mix of sadness and determination.*

**JULIAH** *(sympathetically)*

Oh no... What happened?

**GEK ALIEN** *(somberly)*

People! Big, ugly People! They came, and boom! Gone!

*The atmosphere shifts as the group realizes the Gek's home had suffered a similar fate to what they had experienced on Copper 9.*

**ARYNN** *(empathetically)*

I'm sorry. We've faced our own battles against those bastards.

**GEK ALIEN** *(nods, eyes gleaming)*

But I survive! I come here to find friends!

*He holds up the shiny object, revealing it to be a small holographic projector. With a flick of a switch, it projects images of lush landscapes and vibrant cities, showcasing what his world used to look like.*

**JULIAH** *(awestruck)*

It's beautiful!

**GEK ALIEN** *(enthusiastically)*

Yes! Gek world! Now lost. But we build again!

*He beams with determination, a glimmer of hope shining through his earlier sadness.*

**ARYNN** *(grinning)*

Then let's make sure you find a new home. You're safe with us.

**JULIAH** *(excitedly)*

Absolutely! Welcome to our family, little guy!

*The Gek's eyes widen with joy as he jumps up and down, clapping his hands.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(cheerfully)*

Gek friends! Gek strong!

*The group shares a laugh, their camaraderie growing stronger, united by their shared experiences and newfound friendship.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – BEACH – NIGHT

*The Gek hops with enthusiasm, eager to share more of his story. He gestures animatedly as he begins to explain.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(excitedly)*

Not just Gek! Three races! Vykeen! Korvax!

*He draws symbols in the sand with his finger, trying to illustrate the different races.*

**ARYNN** *(leaning in)*

Tell us more about them.

**GEK ALIEN** *(somberly)*

Vykeen warriors! Strong, proud! They fought hard! Korvax, wise! Smart, they build great machines!
