*He looks down, his expression shifting as he recalls the tragedy.*

**GEK ALIEN**

People come! Big ships! Kill all! No more Vykeen! No more Korvax!

*The group falls silent, the weight of his words sinking in.*

**JULIAH** *(shocked)*

They wiped out entire races?

**GEK ALIEN** *(nods vigorously)*

Yes! Gek survive! But alone. Many Gek lost friends, family.

*He gestures to the sky, his voice filled with both sadness and resolve.*

**GEK ALIEN**

Gek not forget! We fight back! Together with new friends!

*Arynn places a hand on the Gek's shoulder, offering comfort.*

**ARYNN**

We're with you. We'll make sure they pay for what they've done.

**T** *(firmly)*

The People won't know what hit them.

*The Gek's expression brightens, a spark of hope igniting in his eyes.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(grinning)*

Yes! Together! Gek strong! Lizards strong!

*They all nod in agreement, feeling a renewed sense of purpose and camaraderie as they look up at the stars, ready to face whatever challenges lie ahead.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – BEACH – NIGHT

*The Gek's excitement returns as he shares more about the worlds that were once home to his people.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(gesturing expansively)*

Many worlds! Bubble, Pillared, Lush, Frozen, Scalding, Radioactive!

*He draws each world in the sand, his tiny fingers tracing the outlines with fervor.*

**JULIAH** *(interested)*

Those all sound incredible! What were they like?

**GEK ALIEN** *(brightly)*

Bubble world, float! Pillared, giant rocks! Lush, green everywhere! Frozen, ice and snow! Scalding, hot like fire! Radioactive, glow and hurt!

*His face falls as he continues.*

**GEK ALIEN**

But People come! Wipe out! Ninety-three percent! Gone!

*Arynn clenches his fists, anger bubbling beneath the surface.*

**ARYNN** *(furious)*

They annihilated nearly all your worlds?

**GEK ALIEN** *(nods solemnly)*

Yes! Just Gek left. We run, hide.

*He looks up at Arynn, determination etched on his face.*

**GEK ALIEN**

But Gek not give up! We rebuild! Find new worlds!

*Juliah leans closer, her eyes shining with empathy.*

**JULIAH**

You're so brave. We'll help you find a place to thrive again.

*The Gek's eyes light up, hope flickering back to life.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(gratefully)*

Thank you! Gek not alone!

*They all share a moment of solidarity, united by their shared goals and experiences, ready to fight against the common enemy that had brought so much suffering.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – BEACH – DAY

*The sun shines brightly as Juliah sets up a training dummy made from driftwood and vines. She stretches, getting ready to practice her attacks. The Gek watches from a nearby rock, his eyes wide with curiosity.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

Alright, time to show this dummy who's boss!

*With a swift motion, she lunges at the dummy, her movements fluid and precise. She spins and strikes, her tail whips through the air, delivering powerful blows.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(cheerfully)*

Gek watch! Gek learn!

*As Juliah continues her practice, the Gek tries to mimic her moves, awkwardly flailing his arms and hopping around. He fumbles but is determined to imitate her agility.*

**JULIAH** *(laughing)*

Hey, little guy! You've got some spirit!

*She pauses for a moment, demonstrating a more controlled strike.*

**JULIAH**

Here, let me show you. Keep your balance, and use your whole body!

*The Gek nods vigorously, focusing intently on her movements. He tries again, attempting to spin, but ends up tripping over his own feet and landing in the sand.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(sprightly)*

Oof! Gek okay!

*Juliah giggles and offers a hand to help him up.*

**JULIAH**

Come on! You'll get it. Just remember, it's all about flow.

*With newfound determination, the Gek stands up and watches closely as she demonstrates a series of swift strikes and fluid dodges.*

**JULIAH**

Just like this! You can do it!

*He tries again, this time incorporating some of her movements, hopping and swinging his arms. Though he doesn't have a tail, he uses his body creatively, swirling and bouncing with enthusiasm.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(proudly)*

Gek strong!

*Juliah cheers him on, impressed by his effort.*

**JULIAH**

That's it! Keep practicing, and you'll be a natural in no time!

*The Gek smiles broadly, filled with determination, as they continue their training together, the bond between them growing stronger through laughter and shared experiences.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – BEACH – SUNSET

*The sun dips low on the horizon, casting a warm glow over the beach. Arynn, Juliah, and the Gek sit in a circle, the atmosphere relaxed. Arynn takes a deep breath, ready to share their story.*

**ARYNN** *(smiling)*

You know, little guy, we didn't always work together like this.

*The Gek leans in closer, intrigued.*

**GEK ALIEN**

Gek listen!

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

Yeah, it was a wild ride.

**ARYNN**

It all started back on Nukos-632. My planet was... well, let's just say it was a hellhole.

*He gestures to the sky, memories flooding back.*

**ARYNN**

I was just a juvenile, running from the chaos. That's when I stumbled upon these drones.

*The drones nod in agreement, their mechanical forms shimmering in the sunset.*

**Y**

We were on a mission to find survivors, to help rebuild after the devastation.

**JULIAH** *(enthusiastically)*

But we didn't expect to find Arynn.

**ARYNN** *(laughing softly)*

I was just hiding, scared out of my mind.

*The Gek giggles, imagining Arynn's juvenile self.*

**GEK ALIEN**

Gek can imagine!

**ARYNN** *(smiling)*

But when they found me, they didn't just see a scared lizard. They saw potential. They brought me on board.

*The drones puff out their chests proudly.*

**D**

You were more than just a survivor, Arynn. You had a vision.

**ARYNN**

And together, we started terraforming planets. I learned from them, and they learned from me.

*He looks at the Gek with determination.*

**ARYNN**

**GEK ALIEN** *(cheerfully)*

Gek like teamwork!

*Juliah nudges Arynn playfully.*

**JULIAH**

*The Gek beams with pride, feeling accepted and part of something bigger.*

**GEK ALIEN**

Gek strong! Together!

*The sun sets completely, leaving them under a blanket of stars, united in their mission and newfound friendship.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – SHORELINE – NIGHT

*The moonlight reflects off the waves as Arynn and the drones gather around the wrecked Gek ship, its hull battered but salvageable. Arynn kneels next to the ship, tools in hand, while the Gek watches eagerly.*

**ARYNN** *(cheerfully)*

*The Gek hops around excitedly, trying to help by picking up small pieces and handing them to Arynn.*

**GEK ALIEN**

Gek help!

**JULIAH** *(laughing)*

*They work together, Arynn showing the Gek how to use some of the tools. The drones provide support, tightening bolts and making adjustments.*

**T** *(examining the ship)*

We can reinforce the hull with some materials from the beach.

*As they repair the ship, Arynn's focus sharpens.*

**ARYNN**

**GEK ALIEN** *(enthusiastically)*

Gek follow!

*After a while, they finally finish repairing the ship. Arynn steps back, admiring their handiwork.*

**ARYNN**

There! Good as new!

*The Gek hops with joy, looking at the ship proudly.*

**GEK ALIEN**

Gek love ship!

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

**ARYNN**

Alright, just follow my lead.

*The Gek nods, his eyes sparkling with excitement.*

**GEK ALIEN**

Gek ready!

*As the engines roar to life, Arynn glances back at the drones.*

**ARYNN**

Hold on tight, everyone! We're about to take off!

*With a powerful thrust, the ship launches into the night sky, leaving the beach behind as they soar toward their next destination. The stars twinkle brightly around them, a symbol of hope and adventure.*

### INT. GEK SHIP – SPACE – NIGHT

**ARYNN** *(startled)*

**JULIAH**

### EXT. PILLARED PLANET – ORBIT – MOMENTS LATER

**D** *(keeping watch)*

### EXT. PILLARED PLANET – SURFACE – DAY

**ARYNN** *(looking around)*

**ARYNN**

It's 45% argon and 55% nitrogen. Not exactly what we need to survive.

**Y** *(shaking its head)*

**GEK ALIEN**

### INT. GEK SHIP – COCKPIT – LATER

**ARYNN**

Juliah?

*She sits up abruptly, her movements jerky and erratic. The glow in her eyes intensifies as she locks onto Arynn.*

**JULIAH** *(voice distorted)*

Target identified. Threat level: maximum.

**ARYNN**

Juliah, it's me! You're safe!

Gek scared!

**Y** *(alert)*

Corruption detected! Anomaly strength: 538 I/u.

**ARYNN**

What the hell does that mean?

**D** *(explaining quickly)*

Extremely high. The environment is affecting her programming.

*Juliah lunges forward, her tail transforming into a weapon, razor-sharp and ready to strike.*

**JULIAH**

Eliminate all threats!

**ARYNN** *(raising his hands)*

Juliah, stop! We're not a threat!

*But she doesn't listen, charging at the drones with wild intensity. Arynn quickly steps in front of them, trying to protect his friends.*

**ARYNN** *(pleading)*

**JULIAH** *(struggling)*

Must... eliminate...

*In a moment of clarity, she looks at Arynn.*

**JULIAH** *(confused)*

A-Arynn?

**ARYNN**

Yes! You're okay! We're here with you!

**Y** *(soothingly)*

**JULIAH** *(breathing heavily)*

The planet's anomaly is messing with your systems. We need to get out of here!

*The Gek nods vigorously.*

**GEK ALIEN**

Gek want to help Juliah!

### EXT. PILLARED PLANET – SURFACE – DAY

**ARYNN** *(fascinated)*

Gek happy! Juliah is back!

### EXT. PILLARED PLANET – SURFACE – MOMENTS LATER

*As they finish collecting the glowing crystals, Arynn pauses, looking at the data displayed on one of the drones.*

**ARYNN** *(turning to the group)*

We need to understand what we're dealing with. The anomaly strength is measured in I/u—it's a unit used to gauge the intensity of environmental disruptions in energy fields.

**D** *(clarifying)*

I/u stands for "Intensity Units." It indicates how unstable or potent an area is. The higher the number, the more chaotic and dangerous the energy fluctuations can be.

**GEK ALIEN** *(curiously)*

Why is 538 I/u dangerous?

**ARYNN** *(serious)*

At that level, the energy can corrupt biological and mechanical systems. It distorts reality, creating unpredictable effects. It's no wonder Juliah was affected.

**JULIAH** *(firmly)*

Now that I understand, we can prepare better. We have to be cautious as we move forward.

**ARYNN** *(looking around)*

*As she reaches Y, she quickly assesses the situation. She taps into her K̵̛̲̬͍̦̉̉̚͝ͅð̸̩̰̬̪͇̏̈́̈́͊͒k̶̬͙͔͚̪̄͗̆͂̆ṉ̴͓̃̈͛͐̏̏͜ͅͅk̴̛͔̯̖̻͖̋̑̋͊µ̷̢͙̙̩̳͐̔̀̓͋å abilities, her tail shimmering with energy.*

### EXT. LIZARD-953-E – BATTLEFIELD – CONTINUOUS

*As the tide of battle turns, the laughter and taunts continue, now mingling with shouts of anger and the crack of weapons fire.*

### EXT. LIZARD-953-E – BATTLEFIELD – MOMENTS LATER

*As the battle rages on, Juliah skillfully maneuvers through the chaos, her tail whipping around to fend off attackers. Just when she thinks she's in the clear, an enemy soldier lunges from the side.*

**PEOPLE SOLDIER** *(grinning maliciously)*

Got you now, you little freak!

*Juliah barely has time to react as the soldier wraps a strong, reinforced net around her, pinning her arms and tail against her body.*

**JULIAH** *(struggling)*

What the—? Let me go, you bastard!

*The net glows with energy, making it nearly impossible for her to break free. Panic sets in as she thrashes against it, but it only tightens.*

**LIZARD COMMANDER** *(shouting)*

Juliah!

*The Lizard Commander, caught up in his own battle, notices Juliah trapped and tries to fight his way toward her.*

**ARYNN** *(urgently)*

We have to help her!

*Arynn takes aim at the soldier holding Juliah captive, but another enemy quickly appears, forcing him to divert his attention.*

**PEOPLE SOLDIER** *(smirking)*

Not so tough now, are you?

*Juliah growls, her tail twitching in frustration as she realizes she's in deep trouble.*

**JULIAH** *(gritting her teeth)*

You'll regret this!

*Just as the soldier moves in closer, a sudden blast from Drone A sends him stumbling backward.*

**Y** *(cheering)*

Get your filthy hands off her!

*With that distraction, the Lizard Commander pushes through the chaos, using his strength to reach Juliah.*

**LIZARD COMMANDER** *(bellowing)*

Back off, or you'll find out what real pain is!

*With the combined efforts of Arynn and the drones, they manage to fend off the attackers long enough for the Lizard Commander to cut through the net with his blade.*

**JULIAH** *(breathing heavily)*

Thanks, guys! I thought I was a goner!

*As she breaks free, she quickly regains her composure, ready to rejoin the fight alongside her allies.*

**ARYNN** *(firmly)*

Stay close this time! We can't afford to lose anyone else.

*With Juliah back in the fray, they regroup, determined to turn the tide against the People.*

### EXT. LIZARD-953-E – BATTLEFIELD – LATER

*The chaos of battle continues to unfold, with blasts and shouts echoing around them. Just as Juliah finds her rhythm, darting around enemies and landing swift strikes, a sudden silence blankets the area.*

**JULIAH** *(breathing heavily)*

This is too quiet… Where'd they all go?

*Before she can react, a shadow looms overhead. A massive transport ship descends, its cargo bay opening with a loud hiss. From it, a specialized unit of People soldiers—dressed in advanced armor—descends, their eyes locked on Juliah.*

**LEAD PEOPLE SOLDIER** *(smirking)*

Well, well, look what we have here. The little monster thinks she can run.

*Before she can escape, the soldiers unleash a net that envelops her, electrifying her and causing her to convulse.*

**JULIAH** *(shouting)*

No! Get off me!

*The soldiers haul her toward the ship, her thrashing only making it worse as they secure her inside with reinforced restraints.*

**JULIAH** *(struggling)*

You won't get away with this! My friends will come for me!

*As the doors slam shut, Arynn and the Lizard Commander rush over, witnessing her abduction with horror.*

**ARYNN** *(furious)*

Juliah!

**LIZARD COMMANDER** *(grimly)*

We need to get her back! They can't take her!

*With Juliah trapped inside the transport ship, the People soldiers quickly pilot it away from the battlefield, leaving Arynn and the others scrambling to follow.*

**ARYNN** *(raising his weapon)*

We'll bring her back, I promise!

*As they prepare to chase after the transport, Arynn glances at the Lizard Commander, determination etched on their faces.*

**LIZARD COMMANDER**

Let's move! We're not letting her go without a fight!

*They sprint toward their ships, the adrenaline surging as they prepare to launch into the sky, determined to rescue Juliah before it's too late.*

### INT. PEOPLE TRANSPORT SHIP – HOLDING CELL – MOMENTS LATER

*The transport ship's interior is cold and sterile. Juliah is unceremoniously thrown into a dimly lit holding cell. The door slams shut with a heavy thud, echoing ominously in the small space.*

**LEAD PEOPLE SOLDIER** *(mockingly)*

Enjoy your stay, little monster!

*As the soldiers walk away, Juliah picks herself up, brushing off the dust from her limbs. She glances around the barren cell, its walls smooth and unyielding.*

**JULIAH** *(sarcastically)*

Great, just great. A lovely five-star prison with zero amenities.

*She paces the small cell, frustration building. With no windows or distractions, boredom quickly sets in.*

**JULIAH** *(muttering)*

Well, at least I have…

*Her gaze drifts to her tail, still fleshy and lively, swaying slightly as if teasing her.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

Guess it's just you and me, tail.

*She begins to playfully flick her tail back and forth, using it to mimic different moves she'd practiced earlier in the battle. It writhes and curls as she tries to use it like a weapon, pretending to strike at invisible foes.*

**JULIAH** *(laughing to herself)*

Take that! And that! You think you can keep me in here?

*As she plays, her mood lightens momentarily. She twists her tail into complex shapes and even pretends it has a mind of its own, creating a one-droid show.*

**JULIAH** *(smirking)*

If they're going to keep me locked up, I might as well make the most of it. Watch out, I'm a lethal force of nature!

*But the laughter soon fades as reality sinks in. Juliah stops, her expression turning serious.*

**JULIAH** *(sighing)*

I have to get out of here… I won't let them keep me from Arynn and the others.

*Determined, she starts examining the cell, looking for any weak points or possible escape routes, her tail twitching with newfound purpose.*

### EXT. BATTLEFIELD – LIZARD-953-E – MOMENTS LATER

*Arynn stands at the edge of the battlefield, his heart racing. The sounds of combat echo around him, but all he can think about is Juliah. He sinks to his knees, hands gripping his head in frustration.*

**ARYNN** *(sobbing)*

Why did she have to show off? If she hadn't been so reckless, she wouldn't be trapped right now!

*The Lizard Commander approaches, noticing Arynn's despair. He kneels beside him, placing a firm hand on Arynn's shoulder.*

**LIZARD COMMANDER** *(firmly)*

Arynn, listen to me. We can't lose hope. Juliah needs us, and we can't let her sacrifice be in vain.

*Arynn looks up, tears streaking down his face, his voice trembling.*

**ARYNN**

But what if we're too late? What if they hurt her?

*The Commander shakes his head, determination burning in his eyes.*

**LIZARD COMMANDER**

We won't let that happen. We're fighters, Arynn. We don't back down. She's counting on us to rescue her.

*Arynn wipes his tears, anger replacing his sorrow as he nods, finding strength in the Commander's words.*

**ARYNN** *(breathing deeply)*

You're right. We can't just sit here. We have to move!

*The Commander rises, helping Arynn to his feet.*

**LIZARD COMMANDER**

Good. Let's regroup with the others and formulate a plan. We're getting her back.

*With renewed determination, Arynn follows the Commander, the weight of their mission pressing down on them. They head toward their ships, ready to confront the People and save Juliah.*

### INT. PEOPLE TRANSPORT SHIP – HOLDING CELL AREA – MOMENTS LATER

*Arynn and the Lizard Commander rush through the dimly lit corridors of the transport ship, the sounds of battle ringing in the distance. As they approach the holding cells, Arynn's heart races, driven by a mix of fear and determination.*

**ARYNN** *(breathing heavily)*

Juliah! Where are you?!

*The Commander scans the cells, his eyes narrowing as he spots a familiar figure slumped inside one of the concrete enclosures.*

**LIZARD COMMANDER** *(pointing)*

There! That's her!

*Without hesitation, Arynn charges toward the cell, feeling a surge of adrenaline. When he reaches the wall, he grips the edges tightly, his fingers digging into the concrete.*

**ARYNN** *(focused)*

Hold on, Juliah! I'm coming!

*With a primal roar, Arynn rips the wall out of the way as if it were nothing more than paper. The concrete crumbles in his grip, and he throws it aside, revealing Juliah, still trapped and unconscious within.*

**ARYNN** *(relieved but frantic)*

Juliah!

*He rushes in, kneeling beside her. He checks her vitals, heart pounding as he shakes her gently.*

**ARYNN** *(sobbing)*

Wake up! Please, wake up!

*As he cradles her, the tail twitches slightly, signaling life within her. The Commander stands guard at the entrance, ensuring no one interrupts their reunion.*

**LIZARD COMMANDER** *(urgently)*

We need to get her out of here, Arynn!

*Finally, after a moment, Juliah stirs, her eyes fluttering open. She looks up at Arynn, confusion crossing her face.*

**JULIAH** *(weakly)*

What… happened?

**ARYNN** *(tears in his eyes)*

You're safe now. We're getting you out of here.

*With newfound strength, Arynn helps Juliah to her feet, his grip firm as he supports her. They exit the cell together, the weight of their escape only beginning to settle in.*

### EXT. BATTLEFIELD – LIZARD-953-E – MOMENTS LATER

*Emerging from the transport ship, Arynn, Juliah, and the Lizard Commander find themselves back in the chaos of battle. The sounds of clashing metal and furious shouts fill the air as the remaining People forces are engaged with the lizards and drones.*

**ARYNN** *(determined)*

We're not done yet. Let's finish this!

*With Juliah steadying herself beside him, they charge back into the fray. The Lizard Commander signals to their allies, rallying them with a fierce battle cry.*

**LIZARD COMMANDER** *(raising his weapon)*

For our home! For Lizard-953-E!

*As they push forward, Juliah's eyes narrow, her tail flicking behind her with renewed energy. She scans the battlefield, focusing on the nearest enemy—a hulking People soldier who had been causing chaos.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

Time to show these bastards what we're made of!

*With a swift motion, she lunges, her tail whipping around and striking the soldier hard, sending him crashing to the ground.*

**ARYNN** *(excited)*

That's it, Juliah! Keep it up!

*Together, they weave through the melee, Arynn using his agility to dodge attacks while Juliah unleashes a flurry of strikes with her tail. The drones join in, their disassembly arms tearing through enemies like paper.*

*The battlefield is a whirlwind of violence, with explosions and shouts echoing around them. Suddenly, Arynn spots the People leader trying to escape in the chaos.*

**ARYNN** *(angrily)*

Not on my watch!

*He charges after the leader, dodging incoming fire. Just as the leader reaches the edge of the battlefield, Arynn leaps forward, tackling him to the ground.*

**ARYNN** *(gritting his teeth)*

You're not getting away this time!

*Meanwhile, Juliah and the Commander flank the remaining People soldiers, forcing them into a retreat. With one final push, the lizards and drones overwhelm the enemy, cutting down the last of the resistance.*

**LIZARD COMMANDER** *(yelling)*

Victory is ours!

*As the dust settles, Arynn stands over the subdued People leader, panting heavily. He glares down at him, adrenaline still coursing through his veins.*

**ARYNN** *(breathing heavily)*

You thought you could take our home? You'll pay for what you've done.

*The remaining soldiers surrender, realizing they've lost. The battlefield, once a scene of chaos, now becomes a place of relief as the lizards and drones regroup, celebrating their hard-fought victory.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – TROPICAL BEACH – LATER THAT DAY

*After the intense battle, Arynn, Juliah, and the lizard forces arrive back at the tranquil shores of Lizard-7759. The warm sun shines overhead, and the gentle sound of waves crashing against the shore brings a welcome sense of peace.*

**ARYNN** *(relieved)*

We did it. We actually did it.

*Juliah looks around, her eyes sparkling with excitement as she runs her fingers through the soft sand.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

I could get used to this! No more fighting, just... relaxing.

*As they walk along the beach, the lizards begin to set up makeshift shelters and gather around to enjoy the beautiful scenery. Arynn and Juliah decide to dig in the sand, feeling the cool grains slip through their fingers.*

**ARYNN** *(playfully)*

Let's see who can dig the biggest hole!

*They both crouch down, digging enthusiastically. Juliah's tail moves playfully, helping her scoop out sand as Arynn laughs at her antics.*

**JULIAH** *(teasing)*

You're going to need to step up your game if you want to beat me!

*They continue to dig, each trying to outdo the other. Eventually, they create a small pit, and Arynn flops onto his back, looking up at the sky.*

**ARYNN** *(content)*

You know, after everything we've been through, this is exactly what we needed.

*Juliah lies down beside him, her tail swishing through the sand.*

**JULIAH** *(smiling)*

Yeah, I could definitely get used to this. Just the two of us, no crazy aliens trying to kill us.

*As they relax, Arynn turns his head to look at her, a warm smile on his face.*

**ARYNN** *(gratefully)*

I'm really glad you're okay. I don't know what I would've done if… well, you know.

*Juliah nudges him playfully with her tail, her eyes sparkling.*

**JULIAH** *(teasing)*

Come on, you know I can handle myself. Besides, I'm not going anywhere anytime soon.

*They both laugh, enjoying the moment of camaraderie. The sun begins to set, casting a golden glow over the beach as they continue to dig, the memories of battle fading into the background.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – TROPICAL BEACH – MOMENTS LATER

*As Arynn and Juliah enjoy their time on the beach, a sudden disturbance in the air ripples the atmosphere. A swirling rift begins to form in front of them, pulsing with an eerie light. Both of them instantly sit up, eyes widening in alarm.*

**ARYNN** *(confused)*

What the hell is that?!

*The rift expands, and the familiar figure of the People leader stumbles through, panting heavily and looking disheveled.*

**PEOPLE LEADER** *(breathless)*

You thought you'd seen the last of me? No—this time, I—

*Before he can finish, Juliah springs into action, her instincts kicking in. With a swift kick, she sends him sprawling back through the rift.*

**JULIAH** *(fiercely)*

Not so fast, you piece of trash!

*The leader flails as he's pushed back, struggling to regain his balance.*

**PEOPLE LEADER** *(shouting)*

You can't do this! I will have my revenge!

*Ignoring his threats, Juliah channels her energy, focusing on the rift. With a determined look, she raises her hands, summoning her abilities.*

**JULIAH** *(concentrating)*

Time to end this for good!

*The rift starts to destabilize, flickering as she channels her energy into it. The leader scrambles to get through, but the rift is closing.*

**PEOPLE LEADER** *(panicking)*

No! Wait! You can't—

*With one final surge of power, Juliah closes the rift completely, sealing it with a loud crack that echoes through the air.*

**ARYNN** *(relieved)*

Nice work, Juliah! I think he's finally out of our lives for good.

*Juliah brushes off her hands, a triumphant grin on her face.*

**JULIAH** *(smugly)*

And don't forget it! If he tries to come back again, he'll have to get through me first.

*As they share a laugh, the beach returns to its peaceful state, the threat now behind them. The sun continues to set, casting a warm glow over Lizard-7759 as Arynn and Juliah settle back into their moment of relaxation.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – CAVE ENTRANCE – LATER

*While Arynn and Juliah bask in the afterglow of their victory, the Gek alien, curious and adventurous, wanders off to explore a nearby cave. As he delves deeper, he stumbles upon a hidden chamber where a captured People soldier is trapped.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(surprised)*

Hey! Are you alright?

*The People soldier, looking disheveled and terrified, nods vigorously.*

**PEOPLE SOLDIER** *(breathless)*

Please! You have to help me! I know things—secrets about their plans!

*The Gek eyes him suspiciously, but curiosity piques his interest.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(cautiously)*

What do you know?

*The People soldier leans closer, whispering urgently.*

**PEOPLE SOLDIER** *(quickly)*

They're planning another attack—something bigger than before! They've been gathering resources and—

*Before he can finish, Y, one of the drones, enters the cave, hearing the hushed voices.*

**Y** *(cutting in)*

What's going on here?

*The Gek looks back at Y, panic in his eyes.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(frantically)*

He knows their plans! He could—

*But Y, not waiting for any more explanations, lunges forward with swift precision. In a single, clean motion, Y beheads the People soldier, the head rolling away and silence falling in the cave.*

**Y** *(flatly)*

He could also be a liability.

*The Gek stares wide-eyed, processing what just happened.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(shocked)*

You didn't have to do that! He could've helped us!

*Y turns to the Gek, unfazed.*

**Y** *(coolly)*

And he could've betrayed us. Better safe than sorry.

*The Gek frowns, still taken aback by the sudden violence.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(somberly)*

I guess... But what if we could have turned him to our side?

*Y shrugs, moving past the Gek toward the cave entrance.*

**Y** *(matter-of-factly)*

No point in worrying about the "what ifs." We have our own plans to focus on.

*As they exit the cave, the Gek shakes his head, still unsettled by the encounter.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(sighing)*

I just hope we're not losing our chance at something greater.

*The three regroup outside, Arynn and Juliah oblivious to the dark turn of events inside the cave.*

### EXT. LIZARD-7759 – NEAR THE CAVE – MOMENTS LATER

*As Arynn, Juliah, Y, and the Gek stand outside the cave, the peaceful atmosphere is shattered by the sudden roar of engines. A massive ship appears overhead, cloaked in shadows, and its weapons begin to charge.*

**ARYNN** *(alarmed)*

What the hell is that?!

*The ship looms closer, revealing its menacing design adorned with the insignia of the People. Without warning, it launches a volley of nuclear missiles toward them.*

**JULIAH** *(shouting)*

Get down!

*They dive for cover as the ground shakes with the force of the explosions, debris flying everywhere. The Gek, eyes wide with panic, scrambles to his feet.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(terrified)*

We're going to be vaporized!

*In the chaos, Juliah's instincts kick in. She feels the surge of energy building around her as she prepares to create a rift.*

**JULIAH** *(focused)*

Hold on tight!

*As the missiles approach, she concentrates, channeling her power. A swirling portal opens up beside them, pulsating with energy.*

**Y** *(urgently)*

We need to go—now!

*With no time to spare, they leap through the rift just as the missiles explode behind them, the shockwave barely missing them.*

### INT. RIFT – MOMENTS LATER

*They tumble through the rift, colors swirling around them. The sensation is disorienting, but they can feel the safety of escape drawing nearer.*

**ARYNN** *(trying to regain composure)*

Where are we going?!

**JULIAH** *(grimly)*

Anywhere but here!

*With a final burst of energy, the rift opens into a calm starry expanse, leading them to an uncharted location.*

### EXT. UNKNOWN SPACE – CONTINUOUS

*They land softly on the surface of a distant planet, the atmosphere serene and undisturbed. Arynn takes a deep breath, relief washing over him.*

**Y** *(smirking)*

Well, that was close. Anyone got a plan now?

*As they gather their bearings, the Gek looks up at the stars, filled with a mix of awe and fear.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(softly)*

This place… it feels different.

*Juliah nods, her expression turning serious as she scans the surroundings.*

**JULIAH** *(focused)*

Let's regroup and figure out our next move. The People won't stop until they've hunted us down.

*The group prepares to strategize, ready for whatever comes next.*

### EXT. UNKNOWN PLANET – DAY

*The group stands in the serene landscape, but Juliah's mood quickly darkens. She looks out at the distant horizon, her eyes narrowing as memories flood back.*

**JULIAH** *(voice trembling)*

They destroyed it… they destroyed my beach.

*Arynn glances at her, confused.*

**ARYNN** *(trying to comfort)*

Juliah, we'll find a way to rebuild. This isn't the end.

*Juliah clenches her fists, her flesh-like tail twitching with agitation.*

**JULIAH** *(voice rising)*

You don't understand! It was beautiful! The sand, the waves, the sunsets... all gone because of those bastards!

*Y steps closer, noticing the fire in her eyes.*

**Y** *(seriously)*

We can't let anger cloud our judgment. We need to focus on the mission.

*But Juliah isn't listening. Her rage boils over, and a faint glow begins to emanate from her tail, as if it's mirroring her fury.*

**JULIAH** *(snapping)*

Focus? While they're out there ruining everything we care about? No! They need to pay!

*She raises her arms, her energy pulsing as she channels her anger into a destructive force.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(worried)*

Wait! Juliah, don't—

*But it's too late. Juliah unleashes a wave of energy into the ground, creating a shockwave that rattles the earth around them.*

**ARYNN** *(shouting)*

Juliah, stop! You'll draw attention!

*Breathing heavily, Juliah stands amidst the chaos, the remnants of her beach flashing in her mind. The devastation she just caused echoes her pain.*

**JULIAH** *(breathing hard)*

I won't let them destroy any more of what we love. We fight back… harder!

*Arynn looks at her, seeing both the fury and the determination in her eyes.*

**ARYNN** *(firmly)*

Then let's make a plan. We strike back together, and we do it smart. We fight for everything we've lost.

*Juliah nods, her rage transforming into a resolute focus. She turns back to the group, determination etched on her face.*

**JULIAH** *(steely)*

Let's show them what we're made of.

*The group gathers around, fueled by Juliah's passion, ready to take action against the People and reclaim their world.*

### EXT. UNKNOWN PLANET – CONTINUOUS

*The group is steeling themselves for action when suddenly, a People alien springs from the shadows, eyes gleaming with malice. It lunges for D's tail, yanking off the syringe filled with Yabitanite.*

**D** *(surprised)*

Hey! What the—

*Before anyone can react, the alien slashes the syringe towards Juliah, stabbing it into her hand. Juliah gasps, pain shooting through her.*

**JULIAH** *(enraged)*

You little—

*In a swift, furious motion, she grabs the alien by the throat, lifting it off the ground. The pain in her hand only fuels her rage.*

**JULIAH** *(snarling)*

You think you can hurt me?

*With a powerful twist, she slams the alien into the ground, her tail flicking in a blur of motion. It doesn't stand a chance as she unleashes her fury.*

**ARYNN** *(yelling)*

Juliah, watch out for the—

*But it's too late. She crushes the alien beneath her boot, silencing it for good. Breathing heavily, she looks down at the syringe embedded in her hand, the Yabitanite seeping into her system.*

**JULIAH** *(grimacing)*

Damn it!

*Without hesitation, she brings her hand to her mouth, biting down hard on her palm, desperately trying to neutralize the Yabitanite with her own regenerative abilities.*

*The taste of blood mixes with the tang of the Yabitanite, but Juliah fights through the pain, focusing her energy.*

**JULIAH** *(muttering)*

You won't take me down that easily…

*As she continues to neutralize the substance, her tail shifts and glows brighter, the healing energy flowing through her.*

**ARYNN** *(concerned)*

Juliah, are you okay?

*With a fierce determination, she finally pulls the syringe free, tossing it aside.*

**JULIAH** *(breathing hard but resolute)*

I'm fine. Just a little reminder of why we need to finish this fight.

*The group nods, their resolve strengthened by Juliah's resilience, ready to confront whatever comes next.*

### EXT. UNKNOWN PLANET – MOMENTS LATER

*After neutralizing the Yabitanite, Juliah takes a deep breath, steadying herself. She glances at D, whose tail is now missing the syringe.*

**JULIAH** *(smirking)*

Alright, time to fix this.

*With a swift motion, she reaches down and grabs the syringe from where she discarded it. D watches with a mix of curiosity and concern.*

**D** *(nervously)*

Are you sure that's safe?

**JULIAH** *(confidently)*

Trust me. I've got this.

*Juliah carefully aligns the syringe back onto D's tail, making sure it fits snugly. With a quick twist, she reattaches it, ensuring the connection is secure.*

**D** *(relieved)*

Thanks, I guess. Just... don't stab me again, okay?

**JULIAH** *(chuckling)*

No promises if you keep that up.

*She steps back, inspecting her work, then looks at D with a grin.*

**JULIAH** *(cheerfully)*

All set! Now let's show those bastards what we can do.

*The group nods in agreement, their spirits lifted by the camaraderie and determination to fight back. They regroup, ready to confront the People and take back what's theirs.*

### EXT. UNKNOWN PLANET – CONTINUOUS

*As the group regains their composure, Arynn steps forward, looking at his companions with a serious expression.*

**ARYNN** *(voice steady)*

Alright, everyone. We need to understand why we're really in this fight.

*He gestures around at the barren landscape, the remnants of the recent battle still visible.*

**ARYNN**

I've been terraforming planets for years. It's what I was born to do. I turned Lizard-7759 into a paradise, a sanctuary for us and any who seek refuge.

*He takes a deep breath, his eyes narrowing as he continues.*

**ARYNN**

But the People… they don't see that. All they want is control. Control over my Dyson sphere, to harness its power and use it to fuel their own twisted ambitions.

*The group shifts uneasily, understanding the weight of Arynn's words.*

**JULIAH** *(pensively)*

So they want to drain the energy from your creation?

**ARYNN**

Exactly. The Dyson sphere is a source of unimaginable energy. If they get their hands on it, they could obliterate entire worlds.

*His fists clench at his sides, anger simmering beneath the surface.*

**ARYNN**

They've already wiped out countless races, and if we don't stop them, they'll turn their sights on us. We can't let them take what we've built.

*The group exchanges determined glances, the fire of resolve igniting within them.*

**D** *(steadfast)*

Then we need to fight. We can't let them win.

**JULIAH** *(smiling fiercely)*

Let's show them what happens when they mess with the wrong lizards and drones.

*Arynn nods, a fierce determination shining in his eyes as they prepare for the battles ahead.*

### EXT. SPACE – LIZARD-953-E ORBIT – MOMENTS LATER

*The group gathers aboard their ship, a sleek vessel equipped for battle. Arynn stands at the helm, staring out into the vastness of space, determination etched on his face.*

**ARYNN** *(turning to the crew)*

Alright, everyone. It's time to take the fight to the People. We can't do this alone. We need to call in our military.

*He moves to the communications console, fingers flying over the controls as he transmits a distress signal to their fleet.*

**ARYNN** *(over comms)*

This is Arynn of the Lizard Collective. I'm requesting immediate military support to engage the People at their stronghold on People-888.

*The ship shakes slightly as they enter warp, the stars stretching into lines around them.*

**JULIAH** *(leaning against the wall)*

Do you think they'll respond quickly?

**ARYNN** *(confidently)*

They have to. The longer we wait, the more power the People gather. We can't afford to give them that advantage.

*As the ship hurtles through space, the comm system crackles to life.*

**COMMANDER'S VOICE** *(over comms)*

Acknowledged, Arynn. We're mobilizing our forces now. Expect reinforcements shortly.

**D** *(pumping his fist)*

Yes! Let's show them what we're made of!

*The crew cheers, excitement and adrenaline coursing through them. Arynn turns back to the viewport, focusing on the path ahead.*

**ARYNN** *(steadily)*

Once we arrive, we'll strategize and hit them hard. We'll show those bastards they can't mess with the Lizard Collective.

*The ship accelerates, a sense of purpose enveloping them as they approach their destination.*

### INT. SHIP – TRAVELING THROUGH WARP

*The crew settles in for the journey to People-888, anticipation filling the air. D leans back in her seat, tail twitching impatiently.*

**D** *(grinning)*

Hey, Arynn. You got anything to snack on while we wait? I'm starving over here.

**ARYNN** *(smirking)*

You just can't sit still, can you?

*Arynn rummages through one of the supply crates, pulling out a large, oddly colored chunk of alien meat, still fresh.*

**ARYNN** *(tossing it to D)*

Here. Fresh from the last hunt. You'll like this one.

*D catches the meat with her claws, eyes gleaming with hunger. She sinks her teeth into it with ruthless efficiency, tearing through the flesh with savage bites.*

**D** *(with a mouthful, grinning)*

Mmm, this is good. You sure you don't want any?

**ARYNN** *(laughing)*

Nah, you go ahead. Just try not to tear up the ship while you're at it.

*The sound of D devouring the meat echoes through the cabin as the others look on in mild amusement. She rips through the chunk like a machine, savoring every bite, eyes still gleaming with that wild edge.*

**JULIAH** *(smiling)*

I swear, D, you've got more in common with those meat grinders on the People-888 farms than you do with drones.

**D** *(mouth full, grinning)*

That's the nicest thing you've ever said to me.

*They all laugh, the tension easing slightly as they continue their journey. Outside, the stars whip past, but inside, the team is ready, fortified by alien meat and unbreakable resolve.*

### INT. SHIP – TRAVELING THROUGH WARP

*D finishes her chunk of alien meat, wiping her mouth on her arm. Juliah watches with a smirk, her tail twitching slightly as she leans against the wall.*

**JULIAH** *(looking at Arynn)*

Alright, Arynn. You can't just feed D and leave the rest of us starving. What about me and the little guy?

**GEK ALIEN** *(perking up)*

Yeah! I could use something too. Haven't eaten since we left the beach!

**ARYNN** *(laughing)*

Alright, alright. Hold on. Let's see what else we've got here.

*Arynn rummages through another crate, pulling out a couple more alien snacks. He tosses a shiny, glowing fruit to Juliah, and a chunk of something smaller but still meaty to the Gek alien.*

**ARYNN** *(to Juliah)*

Try not to make a mess, will you?

*Juliah catches the fruit with her hand, her tail moving eagerly. She takes a bite, the juices glowing faintly as they drip down her chin. She looks pleased, savoring the taste.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

Oh yeah. This is good. Way better than whatever People-888's cooking up.

*The Gek alien sniffs the chunk of meat suspiciously before chomping down, eyes wide with excitement.*

**GEK ALIEN** *(mouth full)*

Wow! This tastes amazing. What is this?

**ARYNN** *(smiling)*

Let's just say it's something you won't find on your homeworld.

*As they eat, the group shares a few laughs, the tension of their mission momentarily fading as they enjoy their snacks.*

**D** *(grinning at Juliah)*

Guess we're all fueled up now. Next stop—People-888's capital. Let's turn that place into rubble.

*Juliah nods, finishing her glowing fruit as the Gek alien licks his fingers clean, both of them ready for whatever comes next.*

### EXT. SPACE ABOVE PEOPLE-888 – MASSIVE FLEET APPROACHES

*Hundreds of ships warp out of hyperspace, appearing above the atmosphere of People-888. At the head of the fleet is Arynn's flagship, flanked by drones, lizard fighters, and larger warships loaded with cannons. The crew, freshly fed and ready for action, gear up for battle.*

**ARYNN** *(standing at the helm)*

There it is. People-888. Let's show them what happens when you mess with us.

*Juliah and D exchange glances, their bodies thrumming with energy, while the Gek alien straps into his seat, eyes wide.*

**JULIAH** *(cracking her knuckles)*

Let's tear ‘em apart.

**D** *(grinning wildly)*

About time. Let's light ‘em up.

*As Arynn gives the signal, the fleet begins its attack. Massive bursts of energy fire from the warships, cannon shots streaking through space, impacting People-888's atmosphere. Explosions ripple across the surface as the People scramble to mount a defense.*

**COMMANDER (over comms)**

We've breached their defenses. Deploying ground forces!

*Drones and lizard forces begin deploying from the ships, hurtling towards the planet's surface. Arynn's ship follows behind, breaking through the atmosphere as the battle rages.*

### INT. ARYNN'S FLAGSHIP – COCKPIT

**ARYNN** *(into the comms)*

Ground units, engage! Hit their strongholds and crush their defenses.

*From the viewport, they can see smaller ships swarming the surface, hammering People-888's forces. Drones rip through enemy fighters, while the lizard fighters swoop down, unleashing their heavy weaponry.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

This is gonna be fun.

*As they descend, explosions ripple across the cities below, sending debris flying. People-888's military responds, launching their own fighters and anti-air defenses, but they're no match for the combined firepower of Arynn's forces.*

### EXT. PEOPLE-888 – FULL-ON ASSAULT

*Arynn's fleet bursts out of warp, guns blazing, raining hellfire on People-888's surface. Explosions rip through alien cities below as chaos erupts, engulfing the planet in destruction. Drones and lizard forces drop from orbit in waves, hitting the ground like thunder.*

**ARYNN** *(into the comms)*

Show them what happens when they mess with us. No survivors.

*The drones hit the ground hard, including Juliah, D, and the Gek alien, who's clinging to the transport for dear life. As soon as they touch down, Juliah pops out, immediately ready to cause some chaos, her tail swishing behind her like an eager predator.*

**JULIAH** *(smirking)*

Alright, losers, time to get wrecked!

*Without waiting for anyone else, Juliah charges into the fray, her eyes glowing with that familiar dangerous energy. Her tail lashes out like a living whip, grabbing an alien soldier and swinging him like a ragdoll into his comrades. She grins wickedly, tossing her hair back with a hint of that "I'm cooler than you" attitude.*

**JULIAH** *(taunting)*

What? Too scared to fight back? Lame.

*D follows behind, her arm cannon blasting plasma rounds with wild abandon. She laughs as alien soldiers scramble for cover, barely able to keep up with the drones' assault.*

**D** *(grinning)*

You sure you're not enjoying this a little too much, Juliah?

**JULIAH** *(mock scoffing)*

Oh please, like you're not having fun blowing these idiots to pieces!

*Juliah's tail grabs another alien, lifting him into the air before snapping him in half with a single chomp. She wipes some alien blood off her cheek, looking more annoyed than fazed by the violence.*

**JULIAH**

Ugh, can't these guys at least put up a fight? This is embarrassing.

*A squad of alien soldiers tries to set up a barricade, but Juliah's tail smashes through it like it's made of paper. She rolls her eyes as the aliens scatter, panicking as they try to regroup.*

**JULIAH** *(patronizing)*

A barricade? Really? What is this, an after-school special?

*Her tail, radiating with K̵̛̬̦̍̇ð̸̩͇̏̈́ energy, swings again, sending a shockwave that obliterates the barricade and knocks the aliens into the air. They scream as they're flung across the battlefield, smacking into walls with bone-crushing force.*

**D** *(laughing)*

Damn, you've got style. Gotta give you that.

**JULIAH** *(smirking, sarcastic)*

Obviously. It's called being awesome. You should try it sometime, D.

*As they push through the remaining defenses, the Gek alien stumbles along behind them, looking completely bewildered by the carnage around him. He watches in awe as Juliah and D tear through enemy lines like a pair of unstoppable forces.*

**Gek Alien** *(eyes wide)*

Is this... normal for you?

**JULIAH** *(shrugging casually)*

Eh, pretty much. You get used to it.

*Another wave of alien soldiers appears from the smoke, and one massive commander charges at them with a huge energy mace. Juliah raises an eyebrow, clearly unimpressed.*

**JULIAH** *(sighing)*

Really? This guy? Alright, fine.

*The commander swings his mace down with all his strength, but Juliah's tail intercepts the blow, catching the weapon in mid-air. She grins darkly, tightening her tail's grip and snapping the mace in half like it's nothing.*

**COMMANDER** *(roaring)*

You'll die for this!

**JULIAH** *(smirking)*

Yeah, good luck with that, buddy.

*Her tail shoots forward, wrapping around the commander's neck and squeezing tight. She pulls him down to the ground, his face smashing into the dirt as he struggles, but it's useless. With a roll of her eyes, she snaps his neck with a quick jerk of her tail and tosses the lifeless body aside like trash.*

**JULIAH** *(mocking)*

Next time, try not to suck so bad.

*As the battle rages on, Arynn's forces continue to decimate the People-888 soldiers. Plasma fire lights up the sky, and Juliah, D, and the lizards make their final push toward the stronghold. The remaining soldiers are fleeing, desperate to escape the carnage.*

**ARYNN (over comms)**

End this. No more running.

*Juliah spots a group of soldiers trying to retreat. Her tail lashes out, grabbing one of them by the legs and flinging him into the air. She watches with mild amusement as he flails before her tail chomps down, ending him with one bite.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning)*

Sorry, can't let you leave. It's nothing personal. Oh wait—it totally is.

*As the last of the alien forces fall, the battlefield is littered with corpses and debris. Juliah stands tall amidst the chaos, her tail twitching slightly, still hungry for more.*

### EXT. PEOPLE-888 – AN OCEAN OF ALIEN SOLDIERS

*The dust barely settles from the initial fight, but suddenly the ground rumbles beneath their feet. Arynn, Juliah, and the rest of the crew turn to see an overwhelming wave—a literal sea—of alien soldiers charging toward them. An entire square kilometer, packed tight, their battle cries shaking the air like a storm.*

**D** *(wide-eyed)*

You've gotta be fucking kidding me.

**ARYNN** *(gritting teeth)*

This is… insane.

**JULIAH** *(smirking, though there's an edge of panic in her voice)*

Well, shit. Guess we're doing this.

*The aliens charge full speed, their weapons gleaming in the sunlight, pounding the ground like a living tsunami. Juliah cracks her neck, her fingers twitching eagerly as her tail slithers out behind her, ready to unleash hell.*

**JULIAH** *(sarcastic, but intense)*

Alright then, who's first? Come on, assholes, I'm not gonna wait all day!

*The first wave hits hard, but Juliah's already in the thick of it, her tail snapping out and cleaving through half a dozen soldiers in one move. Her eyes flare as K̵̛̬̦̍̇ð̸̩͇̏̈́ energy courses through her, amplifying her strength as she rips through the enemy ranks like a goddamn hurricane.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning wildly)*

Let's fucking GOOO!

*She throws out her arms, and her tail whips into a frenzy, cutting down rows of aliens with lightning speed. Bodies fall, torn apart by the sheer power of her K̵̛̬̦̍̇ð̸̩͇̏̈́-fueled rage, her tail wrapping around soldiers, smashing them into the ground, throwing them into the air like ragdolls.*

**ARYNN** *(shouting over the noise)*

Hold the line! We have to break them!

*Arynn fires plasma rounds into the oncoming horde, his shots vaporizing aliens in brutal flashes of light. D, still enjoying the carnage, laughs maniacally as she guns down soldiers, her plasma cannon leaving nothing but charred remains.*

**D** *(grinning, covered in blood)*

You want some too?! COME GET IT!!

*Juliah, meanwhile, is practically dancing through the battlefield, her tail doing most of the work, smashing, slicing, and consuming enemies like some horrifying beast. But no matter how many she cuts down, there are always more.*

**JULIAH** *(taunting, in the heat of battle)*

Oh, come on! Is that the best you've got?! I'm barely breaking a sweat!

*An alien soldier charges her with a massive energy sword, swinging for her head. Juliah ducks low, then her tail lashes out—it wraps around his neck and twists with brutal force, the sickening crack of bones filling the air as she tosses him aside.*

**JULIAH** *(smirking)*

Nice try, jackass. Maybe next time don't suck.

*But the sheer number of enemies keeps pressing in, and they're starting to overwhelm them. For every alien that Juliah or Arynn takes down, five more replace them.*

**ARYNN** *(shouting)*

We need to push forward or we're going to get swarmed!

*A massive alien commander charges toward Juliah, a gigantic blade raised high above his head. Juliah's tail whips up, ready to defend, but the commander is fast—he brings the blade down, severing her tail in one brutal strike.*

**JULIAH** *(screaming, panicked)*

YOU FUCKER!

*For a split second, Juliah is stunned. Her tail—her primary weapon—is gone. She looks down at the stump, her mind racing, blood dripping into the dirt. But before the commander can press the attack, Juliah's eyes blaze with that familiar K̵̛̬̦̍̇ð̸̩͇̏̈́ energy, and her tail regenerates in an instant.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning darkly)*

Oh, you're so dead now.

*With a wild grin, she launches her new tail at the commander, wrapping it around his torso and squeezing until his body explodes in a shower of blood and guts.*

**JULIAH** *(cackling)*

Who's next?! Come on, I'm just getting started!

*But the alien soldiers keep coming. The tide is relentless, a never-ending wave. Juliah, covered in alien blood, rips through them with her tail, her laughter echoing over the battlefield.*

**JULIAH** *(snarling)*

You motherfuckers are going down!

*The drones, lizards, and Arynn continue to fight, pushing through the ocean of enemies. Blood sprays through the air, body parts are scattered across the battlefield, and the sound of carnage fills the air like a symphony of destruction.*

**ARYNN** *(shouting)*

Break their lines! We've got to end this!

*Juliah, her energy still crackling wildly, charges forward, leading the attack. Her tail rips through entire rows of soldiers, her eyes gleaming with pure rage. She's a force of nature, unstoppable, untouchable.*

**JULIAH** *(laughing like a maniac)*

LET'S FUCKING GO!

*Finally, after what feels like hours, the last alien falls, his body collapsing in a heap. The battlefield is quiet except for the sound of heavy breathing and the crackling of burning wreckage.*

### EXT. PEOPLE-888 – DURING BATTLE

*The drones and Arynn land on the surface of People-888, a hostile, craggy planet with thick, stormy clouds overhead. The terrain is uneven, jagged, and much of it is industrial—massive factories belching black smoke into the atmosphere. The gravity is unusually low, which the team quickly discovers.*

**D** *(floating slightly as she steps, landing awkwardly)*

Whoa, okay. Why is it so damn floaty here?!

**ARYNN** *(smirking)*

People-888's gravity is lower than average. Makes everything feel… lighter, but also a hell of a lot harder to move around.

**JULIAH** *(rolling her eyes, already annoyed)*

Great, another planet with stupid gravity. Perfect.

*As the battle begins, the swarm of alien soldiers—thousands strong—charges at them. The team opens fire, but Juliah is already struggling to stay steady. Her foot catches on a rock, and the low gravity sends her toppling forward into a slow-motion fall.*

**JULIAH** *(shouting in frustration)*

Oh, come on! Not again!

*She slams into the ground with a loud thud, her tail awkwardly whipping around behind her. D is too busy laughing to help, blasting through a wave of alien soldiers with ease.*

**D** *(laughing)*

Juliah, you're supposed to fight the aliens, not the gravity!

**JULIAH** *(muttering)*

This fucking planet… I'll kill them all just to fix this goddamn gravity.

*She scrambles back to her feet, but the low gravity throws off her balance again. Another stumble, another near-fall. But Juliah's tail lashes out instinctively, grabbing an alien soldier by the leg, yanking him off his feet.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning wickedly as she pulls the alien toward her)*

At least my tail still works.

*She swings the alien into a nearby rock face, splattering him across the surface with a brutal crunch. Despite her struggle with the low gravity, Juliah's combat instincts are still sharp.*

**ARYNN** *(firing his weapon at another wave)*

Focus! The leader's still out there—get your shit together, Juliah!

**JULIAH** *(snarling, tail twitching)*

I'm fine, I'm fine. Just gotta… stop floating.

*As the battle rages on, Juliah keeps tripping, the low gravity constantly messing with her movements. Despite this, she manages to use her tail to slice through enemies, her frustration fueling her attacks.*

**JULIAH** *(grumbling, taking down an alien with a brutal tail whip)*

This planet is the worst. I swear, I'll nuke the whole damn place if I trip one more time.

*She takes a step forward and—of course—stumbles again, this time managing to catch herself by jamming her tail into the ground.*

**JULIAH** *(seething)*

Fuck this planet.

### INT. PEOPLE-888 CITADEL – FINAL BOSS ENCOUNTER

*After tearing through wave after wave of alien soldiers, the group finally reaches the massive, fortress-like citadel at the heart of People-888. Inside, it's dark and ominous, with flickering lights and the sound of machinery humming in the background. The air is thick with tension as they approach the throne room.*

**ARYNN** *(sternly)*

This is it. The leader's inside.

**D** *(grinning, with a bit of blood still smeared on her cheek)*

About time. I'm starving. Hope this guy's got more fight in him than the rest.

**JULIAH** *(rolling her eyes)*

Yeah, or at least a working treadmill.

*They step into the throne room, and there he is—The People's Leader. A morbidly obese alien, sitting in a colossal mechanical chair that supports his weight. His body is grotesque, folds of flesh spilling over the sides. He's nearly immobile, but his beady eyes lock onto them with malice. His breathing is heavy, labored, and the room reeks of stale air.*

**THE LEADER** *(wheezing, voice dripping with arrogance)*

You… dare enter my domain? Insolent fools. I've controlled People-888 for centuries, and you think you can take me down?

**ARYNN** *(stepping forward, disgusted)*

You're just a bloated sack of corruption. Your reign ends now.

**JULIAH** *(grinning wickedly)*

Oh my God, what the hell is that? He's… He's huge! No wonder this planet's so messed up. Gravity's probably weaker just from trying to escape your orbit.

**D** *(bursting into laughter)*

Dude, does your throne come with a forklift?

**THE LEADER** *(snarling, though it's weak due to his heavy breathing)*

Silence! I am the ruler of People-888! You… are nothing! Prepare to die, fools.

*He tries to stand, but his massive body only shifts slightly, sending ripples through his flesh. His throne emits a groaning sound under the strain.*

**ARYNN** *(mocking)*

You seriously think you can take us on? You can't even get off that damn chair.

**JULIAH** *(smirking, tail flicking behind her)*

It's fine, Arynn. I'll handle this. It'll be like taking out a bag of gelatinous crap. I've killed scarier things in my sleep.

*She starts walking toward the leader, but her step is thrown off by the low gravity—she stumbles again, nearly falling flat.*

**JULIAH** *(gritting her teeth)*

Fuck this gravity!

*Before she can recover, the leader presses a button on his throne, and suddenly, massive mechanical arms shoot out from the walls, each holding advanced weaponry. The entire room lights up with a deadly array of blasters, rockets, and laser cannons.*

**THE LEADER** *(cackling weakly)*

You think I need to move to destroy you? Fools! Technology will do my bidding! You will burn!

*The battle begins—laser fire and rockets exploding all around them. Despite his immobility, the leader has rigged the throne room with enough firepower to decimate armies. Arynn, D, and Juliah dive into action.*

**ARYNN** *(shouting over the chaos)*

Take out those cannons! We need to close the distance!

**JULIAH** *(grinning, spinning her tail like a blade)*

Oh, hell yes.

*Even with the low gravity still messing with her balance, Juliah uses her K̵̛̲̬͍̦̉̉̚͝ͅð̸̩̰̬̪͇̏̈́̈́͊͒k̶̬͙͔͚̪̄͗̆͂̆ṉ̴͓̃̈͛͐̏̏͜ͅͅk̴̛͔̯̖̻͖̋̑̋͊ abilities to launch herself toward the ceiling, avoiding fire and slashing through the mechanical arms with her tail.*

**JULIAH** *(yelling)*

Say goodbye to your toys, fatass!

*She lands a blow on one of the central arms, severing it and causing a chain reaction of explosions throughout the room. The leader shrieks as his defenses are slowly dismantled.*

**D** *(laughing, blasting through a few smaller cannons)*

This guy's all talk! What a joke.

**THE LEADER** *(wheezing in panic)*

N-no… I am the ruler… I can't be defeated…!

*As the final defenses fall, Arynn strides forward, his plasma gun aimed directly at the leader's bloated body.*

**ARYNN** *(coldly)*

Your reign is over.

*Before Arynn can pull the trigger, the leader tries to stand again, but he's too heavy. In a final act of desperation, he reaches for something on his throne—a hidden switch. But before he can activate it, Juliah's tail lashes out, grabbing the switch and crushing it.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning darkly)*

Sorry, fatso, no escape this time.

*Arynn fires, and the plasma shot hits the leader square in the chest. His body convulses, the fat rippling as the energy blasts through him. He slumps back into his throne, defeated.*

**THE LEADER** *(voice fading)*

I… am… invincible…

**D** *(mocking)*

Yeah, sure you are, big guy.

*The leader's body finally goes still, his reign over People-888 coming to a fitting, undignified end.*

**JULIAH** *(smirking, brushing off her hands)*

Well, that was disgusting. Can we leave this shitty planet now?

**ARYNN** *(nodding, looking at the ruined throne)*

Yeah. Let's get the hell out of here.

### INT. PEOPLE-888 CITADEL – AFTER THE "DEATH"

*As Arynn, Juliah, and D prepare to leave the throne room, there's an eerie silence, broken only by the faint hum of the ruined machinery. The air feels heavy, but there's a sense of closure as the group turns to walk out. Just then, a sound—deep and guttural—rumbles through the citadel, sending chills down their spines.*

**JULIAH** *(smirking)*

Okay, seriously, what now?

*Before anyone can react, the grotesque body of the People's Leader begins to twitch. His chest heaves unnaturally, and his eyes snap open—bloodshot and furious. A horrifying, bone-chilling scream explodes from his bloated mouth, so loud it reverberates through the citadel, making the walls shake.*

**THE LEADER** *(voice warped, piercing, filled with rage)*

YOUUUUUUUUUUUUU!!!!

*The scream is deafening, rattling their bones and making it feel like their eardrums are about to explode. Juliah clutches her head, stumbling back from the sheer force of it.*

**JULIAH** *(shouting over the noise)*

What the fuck is that?! Why won't he stay dead?!

*The leader's massive body surges with unnatural energy. His skin ripples, and his bloated form seems to inflate further, growing even larger and more grotesque. The machinery in the room starts flickering to life again, as if feeding off his rage.*

**D** *(yelling)*

This asshole's like a cockroach!

**ARYNN** *(through gritted teeth)*

Everyone, fall back!

*The leader's scream reaches a horrifying crescendo, causing cracks to appear in the floor and walls. The air itself seems to vibrate with his fury. As they retreat toward the entrance, the leader rises from his throne, his swollen body towering over them, his eyes glowing with hate.*

**THE LEADER** *(voice distorted, filled with unnatural power)*

I AM YOUR GOD! YOU WILL ALL DIE!!!

*He lets out another earth-shattering scream, the sheer volume distorting the space around them. Arynn, Juliah, and D stagger from the force of it, struggling to keep their balance.*

**JULIAH** *(teeth gritted, tail thrashing)*

Oh, for fuck's sake, I am so done with this guy!

*Juliah, ignoring the crushing weight of the scream, summons all her energy and charges forward, her K̵̛̲̬͍̦̉̉̚͝ͅð̸̩̰̬̪͇̏̈́̈́͊͒k̶̬͙͔͚̪̄͗̆͂̆ṉ̴͓̃̈͛͐̏̏͜ͅͅk̴̛͔̯̖̻͖̋̑̋͊ abilities glowing along her tail. She leaps into the air, using her tail to slice through the energy field emanating from the leader.*

**JULIAH** *(snarling)*

You wanna scream, you fat fuck? Let's see how loud you are when I shut you up for good!

*With one powerful slash, she drives her tail straight into the leader's bloated throat, silencing his scream instantly. The room falls into an eerie, sudden quiet as the leader gurgles, his eyes widening in shock.*

**D** *(laughing, clapping)*

Holy shit, Juliah, that was brutal!

**ARYNN** *(grinning slightly)*

Nice work.

*The leader's body convulses one final time, his grotesque form deflating as his life force finally ebbs away for good. His corpse slumps to the floor with a heavy thud, and this time, it stays down.*

**JULIAH** *(wiping her hands, panting slightly)*

Now he's dead.

### EXT. MOON NEONEOS – CRIMSON HORIZON

*After the intense showdown, Arynn, Juliah, and D set their sights on Neoneos, a moon shimmering with a fiery glow, its surface dotted with molten rivers and volcanic craters. As they land, the heat radiates off the ground, waves of heat distortion rising in the air.*

**ARYNN** *(smirking, adjusting his gear)*

Welcome to Neoneos! I hope you like it hot, because it's about to get steamy.

*They step out of their ship, the ground beneath their feet almost sizzling. In the distance, the towering peaks of volcanoes erupt sporadically, sending glowing lava cascading down like molten waterfalls.*

**JULIAH** *(wincing at the heat)*

Are you kidding me? This place feels like a sauna on steroids!

**D** *(grinning)*

Maybe we should have brought some ice packs.

*They venture deeper into the moon, following the winding paths leading to the core. The air grows hotter, thick with sulfur and steam, as they approach a massive cavern entrance that radiates a pulsing orange glow.*

### INT. NEONEOS CORE – LAVA GLOWING CAVERN

*Inside the cavern, the heat is almost unbearable, but the sight is breathtaking. The walls glisten with molten rock, and strange bioluminescent plants bloom, thriving in the extreme conditions. Suddenly, they hear laughter—playful and chaotic.*

**ARYNN** *(curious)*

What the hell is that?

*As they step further into the cavern, they spot a group of alien beings gathered around a pool of bubbling lava. They are small, with bright red skin, long limbs, and oversized, expressive eyes. They dance around the lava, reveling in the heat and tossing glowing rocks into the molten pool.*

**ALIEN LEADER** *(spotting Arynn and the others, grinning widely)*

WELCOME, WARM-BLOODED FRIENDS!

**JULIAH** *(raising an eyebrow)*

Warm-blooded? You sure know how to flatter someone!

**ALIEN LEADER** *(laughing)*

Here on Neoneos, we love things HOT! The hotter, the better! We call ourselves the Ignix! What brings you to our fiery domain?

**ARYNN** *(smirking)*

Just exploring, but it looks like we found a party!

*The Ignix dance around the lava, tossing fire-infused stones that explode in showers of sparks. The atmosphere is electric, and the heat feels invigorating.*

**D** *(excitedly)*

Can we join in? I want to try tossing some of those!

*The Ignix invite them to join their festivities, and Arynn, Juliah, and D get swept into the chaotic celebration. They laugh and throw stones into the lava, the heat creating a euphoric atmosphere.*

**JULIAH** *(grinning, catching a glowing stone)*

This is wild! Who knew a molten moon could be this much fun?

**ALIEN LEADER** *(dancing)*

Join us, friends! Feel the heat! Embrace the flame!

*As they celebrate, the Ignix share stories of their home, how they thrive in extreme conditions, and their love for all things fiery. Arynn listens intently, fascinated by their resilience and joy in such an intense environment.*

**ARYNN** *(to the Ignix)*

Your energy is infectious! We could use a little more of this passion back on Lizard-953-E.

*As the festivities continue, Arynn, Juliah, and D prepare to learn more about the Ignix culture, ready to embrace the fiery spirit of Neoneos.*

*As the celebration continues, the drones decide to take a break from the festivities. Juliah, D, and Arynn wander into a stunning field where vibrant lava flowers bloom, casting an ethereal glow against the dark volcanic rock.*

**D** *(excitedly)*

Whoa! Look at these flowers! They're like glowing gems!

**JULIAH** *(teasingly)*

And they smell like roasted marshmallows! Perfect for a snack.

*D plucks a lava flower, taking a big sniff and grimacing at the intense heat.*

**D** *(chuckling)*

Okay, maybe not a snack. But they sure are pretty!

*As they explore, Arynn pulls out a data pad, scanning through information about their next mission.*

**ARYNN** *(scribbling)*

Alright, I need to fill out the paperwork for the demolition of People-888. If we're going to use their resources, we need to be legit about it.

**JULIAH** *(smirking)*

Legit? Is that really how you want to go about this? We just blew up half their forces!

**ARYNN** *(grinning)*

Hey, a little paperwork goes a long way! Plus, we need to keep things organized if we're going to utilize the Dyson sphere's resources.

**D** *(raising a brow)*

You really think they're gonna let us just stroll in and take their stuff after we leveled their planet?

**ARYNN** *(confidently)*

Why not? We'll just present it as a necessary collaboration. Besides, they're the ones who wanted to mess with us in the first place.

*They make their way back to the Ignix gathering, where Arynn continues to type on his data pad.*

### INT. IGNIX CELEBRATION – FRESH FRUIT AND FIRE

**ARYNN** *(enthusiastic)*

Business? In the midst of our fiery revelry? This is a time for heat and passion, my friend!

Like this?

**Arynn**

*(Wiping sweat from his brow)*

That was incredible! But I'm curious, O—who exactly are you? You seem… different from us.


**O**

I understand your curiosity. I am a disassembly drone, built for precision and efficiency. My primary function is to analyze and dismantle materials, but I have evolved beyond my original programming.

Evolved? What do you mean?

So you're not just a machine? You have thoughts and feelings?

Exactly. I can think, feel, and even adapt. My creators didn't anticipate this evolution, but here I am. I want to help others like you, those who are willing to push boundaries and challenge norms.


**Arynn**

*(Nodding in understanding)*

So, you're not just here to teach us to fly fast but also to share your knowledge and experiences?


**O**

*(Smiling warmly)*

Yes! I've seen many worlds and encountered countless beings. My journey has taught me that strength lies in unity and understanding. Together, we can forge a new destiny.

*Scene: The group stands in awe, absorbing O's words. They feel a newfound connection to her, recognizing her as a mentor and ally.*


**Juliah**

*(Excitedly)*

So, we're not just learning about speed; we're learning about ourselves too!

Exactly! And the faster you learn to fly, the more you'll discover about your own potential.

*(Grinning)*
