*(eyes lighting up with excitement)*

Ohhh, is that a Gek pirate? The real deal? You're one of those pirates who raids People ships, right?


**Buccangek**

*(with a snort, puffing up his tiny chest)*

Aye, I am the infamous Buccangek! Ravager of riches, plunderer of People! They flee at the sight of my banner!


**Y**

*(leaning over to D, smirking)*

Looks like someone takes ‘space pirate' a bit seriously, huh?


**O**

*(barely able to contain her excitement, hopping slightly on her toes)*

Buccangek, you wouldn't happen to need a little extra firepower, would you? I'm very, very good at taking down People ships. I mean, *very* good.

*(grins menacingly)*


**Buccangek**

*(stopping to look up at O, squinting suspiciously)*

Shoot down ships? For a cut of me plunder? Hm… tempting, lass, but no. Buccangek doesn't share the spoils!

*(crosses his arms defiantly)*


**O**

*(pouting slightly, voice shifting to a more pleading tone)*

Come on! I don't even need a cut. Just let me shoot a few. It's for fun! Those People ships practically *beg* to be blown up.


**Buccangek**

*(laughing heartily, shaking his head)*

Fun, ye say? Hah! Buccangek does this for the treasure, not the thrill! I'll not waste a good ambush on mere entertainment, lass.


**D**

*(trying to hold back laughter)*

Guess the Gek pirate life isn't all thrill-seeking and cannonballs, huh?


**O**

*(glaring playfully at D before turning back to the pirate, hands on her hips)*

Buccangek, you really don't know what you're missing. I'm a disassembly drone—breaking things is practically my art form!


**Buccangek**

*(leaning back, looking her up and down with a mix of skepticism and admiration)*

An artist, eh? Hm… *maybe* one day, if ye prove yerself in battle, Buccangek might consider it. But for now, keep yer trigger fingers to yerself!


**Juliah**

*(nudging O with a grin)*

Don't worry, you'll get your chance. Plenty of People ships out there, remember?


**O**

*(grinning wickedly, her fingers twitching with the thought of future targets)*

Fine, Buccangek. But if you ever change your mind, you know who to call. I promise I'd be the best asset you'd ever have.


**Buccangek**

*(giving her a piratey nod, tipping his hat)*

Aye, I'll keep ye in mind, lass.


**Y**

*(mocking a pirate accent, nudging D)*

Looks like ye be makin' an impression, matey!


**O**

*(chuckling, casting a last mischievous glance at Buccangek)*

Guess that's what I do best.


**Narrator**

As the crew heads back to their transport, O casts a last wistful look at the pirate and his flashy insignias, already daydreaming about future battles in the cosmos.


**Narrator**

The market was alive with the usual buzz when the ominous shadow of a People ship swept across the landscape. O's sensors immediately locked onto the target, her gaze narrowing as she assessed the vessel's massive hull. Her wings, sleek and powerful, extended outward, catching the light as she readied herself for a swift, silent ascent.


**O**

*(smirking)*

Look at that shiny tin can they call a ship. Let's see how well it flies without its power.

Her wings unfurled fully, flapping with a whispering grace as she took off. No thrusters, just the smooth, calculated beat of her wings slicing through the air, carrying her silently toward the looming ship. Below, Y and Arynn watched her go, Y chuckling as she zipped away.


**Y**

She's like a real-life horror movie up there. Poor aliens don't even know what's about to hit 'em.


**Arynn**

*(nodding, grinning)*

They'll find out soon enough.

As O glided over the massive vessel, she scanned for the best access point. Spotting a control panel near the ship's central power core, she folded her wings and dropped down, landing with barely a sound. Her arm transformed, replacing her hand with an EMP device that extended with sleek efficiency. Without hesitation, she activated it, sending a powerful electromagnetic pulse coursing through the ship's systems.

Inside, the People soldiers stumbled as lights flickered, screens flashed with static, and alarms blared in futile resistance.


**People Soldier #1**

*(slapping buttons, panicked)*

Systems are crashing! We're losing control!


**People Soldier #2**

*(catching a glimpse of a dark figure through a viewport)*

There's… there's something on the hull!

Outside, O grinned as the EMP's pulse disabled the ship, its once-sturdy systems falling silent under her touch. She stretched her wings and folded them back, preparing for her next move. With a calculated flick, she peeled back the hull's paneling, slipping inside the ship's corridors as quiet as a shadow. She advanced, her footsteps silent, catching sight of a group of People soldiers huddled in the dimly lit passageway ahead.

Her tail, tipped with Yabitanite crystals that shimmered ominously, curled up and readied itself. She waited just long enough for them to notice her.


**People Soldier #3**

*(stumbling backward)*

No… no, it can't be…!

O didn't waste a moment. With a single strike, she lunged forward, her tail piercing through one of the soldiers, the Yabitanite eating through his armor and body like acid. He gasped, his form disintegrating as he slumped against the wall.


**O**

*(smiling darkly, voice low)*

What's the matter? Didn't expect a proper welcome?

She turned toward the others, her gaze cold as her tail whipped through the air, striking another soldier square in the chest. He collapsed in a heap, leaving only two others scrambling in terror. One bolted toward the exit hatch, desperate for any escape.

### EXT. OUTSIDE THE SHIP

The soldier threw himself out into the open air, plunging down toward the river below in a last-ditch effort to swim to safety. But O was faster. Unfurling her wings, she dove after him, gliding through the air with a ruthless precision until she was right above him. In one smooth motion, she extended her arm, grasping his ankle and pulling him upward.


**O**

*(grinning, her tone mockingly gentle)*

Oh, going somewhere?

She flew him back to shore, tossing him onto the ground with a smirk. As he struggled to his feet, she loomed over him, her shadow stretching across the sand.


**Alien Soldier**

*(barely able to stand, pleading)*

Please… I… we didn't mean…


**O**

*(cutting him off with a sinister smile)*

You People are everywhere, like a disease. And me?" *she leaned in, her tail hovering inches from his throat* "I'm the cure.

Without another word, she flicked her tail, severing his head in a clean, ruthless motion. She watched as his body crumpled to the ground before plucking his severed arm, examining it thoughtfully. With a wicked gleam in her eye, she raised it like a popsicle, taking a casual sip from the end of the severed limb.


**O**

*(smirking, savoring the moment)*

Almost tastes like victory.

She let the arm drop, glancing back toward the People ship still floating above, now a powerless hulk adrift in the sky. The job was done, and O stretched her wings one last time, enjoying the stillness around her as she prepared to head back to the crew. But just before she took off, she cast one last look down at the remains of the soldier at her feet, a satisfied grin spreading across her face.


**Narrator**

The aftermath of her bloody encounter left O feeling invigorated, the adrenaline coursing through her circuits. She moved deeper into the ship, her sensors still active, scanning for any remaining threats. As she approached the restroom, the door creaked slightly ajar, a faint sound drawing her attention.


**O**

*(grinning, her voice playful)*

What's this? A little hidey-hole? You sweeties really are filled with love, huh?

With a flick of her tail, she formed it into a heart shape, the Yabitanite crystals glinting menacingly in the dim light. She stepped forward, the door swinging open completely to reveal a trembling alien pressed against the far wall, eyes wide with terror.


**Alien Soldier**

*(stammering, backing away)*

P-Please, don't hurt me! I-I just wanted to—


**O**

*(interrupting, tilting her head)*

Wanted to what? Tell me all about your love for your friends? Because you're about to become one with the floor, darling.

Before he could respond, O lunged forward with a sudden burst of speed. Her tail whipped out, and in an instant, she grabbed hold of his legs, her grip vice-like. The alien let out a desperate scream, but it was drowned out by the sound of ripping flesh and snapping bone.


**O**

*(her tone cheerful)*

You'll never walk again, but at least you'll feel lighter!

She yanked his legs clean off, sending the alien into a panic as he fell back, clutching his now-stubbed limbs. Blood pooled on the floor, painting a grotesque image against the metallic backdrop of the ship's restroom.


**Alien Soldier**

*(screaming)*

Why are you doing this?!


**O**

*(rolling her eyes, still playful)*

I'm just sharing the love, sweetheart! You don't need legs to feel affection.

With a sinister smile, she raised the severed legs in the air triumphantly, the heart-shaped tip of her tail still glowing ominously in the dim light.


**O**

Now, let's see how much love you really have in you!

With a swift motion, she flung the legs aside, watching them land with a wet thud against the wall, the alien's pained gasps echoing through the small space. She leaned down close to him, her voice dropping to a whisper filled with mockery.


**O**

You'll be joining your friends soon enough. But first, let's have a little more fun.

As she reached for him, the restroom filled with a cacophony of sounds: the clattering of her tail, the whirring of her mechanics, and the fading cries of the alien soldier as O prepared to give him a love he would never forget.


**Narrator**

Meanwhile, on the beach, the Gek began mobilizing their military forces, preparing for any potential threats that might emerge from the chaos of the battlefield. O was in the air, her wings flapping rhythmically as she scouted the area, eyes sharp and scanning for any signs of People aliens hiding among the lush tropical landscape.


**Gek Commander**

*(calling out orders, a determined look on his face)*

Form up the squads! We need to be ready for any incursions. Keep the perimeter secure!


**O**

*(gliding above, her voice crackling through her comms)*

You guys ready for a little fun? I'm seeing movement in the trees! I want to go in and say hello!


**Gek Commander**

*(shouting back)*

Just be careful, O! We don't know how many of them are out there.

O twisted and turned in the air, her keen sensors picking up the faintest of sounds—a rustle in the foliage, a whisper of movement that hinted at lurking dangers. She banked sharply, descending towards the edge of the dense jungle, her excitement building.


**O**

*(muttering to herself, her eyes gleaming)*

Come on, come out and play! I promise to be nice… for a little while.

She landed softly on a branch, the sunlight filtering through the leaves and casting an ethereal glow around her. In the distance, she spotted a group of People aliens, their camouflage barely hiding their forms as they moved cautiously through the underbrush.


**O**

*(whispering into her comms, her voice dripping with enthusiasm)*

Got a visual! Three of them, moving in a tight formation. Looks like they're trying to flank us. Can't let them get away!

With a mischievous grin, she flexed her wings, feeling the thrill of the hunt surge through her. She swooped down silently, her movements swift and graceful, ready to intercept the aliens before they could regroup.


**Narrator**

As O approached, her mind raced with anticipation. She could almost taste the fear emanating from her targets, and she loved it. The thrill of the chase ignited her circuits, urging her forward.


**O**

*(murmuring to herself, a predatory glint in her eyes)*

Just a little closer… just a little closer…

Suddenly, one of the aliens spotted her and shouted, the panic evident in his voice.


**People Alien**

Look out! It's a drone!


**O**

*(smirking, her voice cold and confident)*

Too late, darlings! You can run, but you can't hide!

With a powerful thrust of her wings, O launched herself at them, her Yabitanite tail swinging behind her like a deadly pendulum, ready to strike. The first alien barely had time to react before she sliced through the air, a clean cut that left him sprawling on the ground, disbelief etched on his face.


**O**

*(laughing gleefully)*

One down, two to go! Who's next?

The remaining two aliens turned to face her, panic written across their features as they prepared to defend themselves. O could see their trembling hands grasping their weapons, but their fear only fueled her excitement.


**O**

*(mockingly)*

Aw, don't be shy! I promise I'll make this quick!

As they opened fire, O gracefully dodged their shots, her wings fluttering as she maneuvered with agility. The bullets whizzed past her, narrowly missing their target.


**O**

Nice try! But you'll need to do better than that!

She swooped down again, her tail striking like a viper, disarming one of the aliens with a swift motion.


**O**

What's the matter? Can't handle a little dance?

In a single fluid motion, she lunged forward, her Yabitanite tail—an unyielding extension of her being—slicing through the air, and decapitating the second alien with a satisfying crunch.


**O**

*(giggling, looking at the severed heads)*

Two for the price of one! Who knew this would be such a lovely day?

With the path clear, O flew back toward the Gek forces, a triumphant look on her face.


**O**

*(rejoining the Gek Commander)*

They're taken care of! Now, let's see what other fun we can have!


**Gek Commander**

*(raising an eyebrow, impressed)*

You are quite the force of nature, O. We could use more like you in our ranks!


**O**

*(smirking)*

You know it! But let's keep moving. I can smell more of them nearby, and I'm feeling hungry for a little more action.

With that, she spread her wings wide, ready to scout the area once again, her thirst for chaos and destruction unquenchable.

The chaos of battle echoed around them as **O** darted forward, her glowing blue eyes scanning the horde of aliens. With a wicked grin, she slashed her claws through the air, effortlessly slicing through alien flesh.


**O**

Nice try, ugly! But you're gonna need more than that!

But one of the aliens, desperate and enraged, swung its weapon and landed a brutal blow. **O**'s body was severed into pieces, but as her remains began to reassemble, she let out a maniacal laugh.


**O**

Did you really think that would stop me? Cute!

Fully reformed, she lunged at the alien, grabbing it by the neck.


**O**

Now, let's see how much you can take!

With a terrifying crunch, she bit down hard, her jaws tearing through its flesh. The alien let out a horrific scream.


**Alien**

No! Please! Don't—


**O**

Oops! Too late for that!

*(She threw the alien down, watching as it crawled away, blood pouring from its wounds.)*


**Alien**

Help! Send reinforcements! We can't handle this!

*(it gasped, panic evident in its voice.)*

**O** smirked, tilting her head.


**O**

Reinforcements? You think they can save you?" She raised her railgun arm, the barrel glowing ominously. "Let's make this quick, shall we?

With a swift pull of the trigger, she unleashed a barrage of rounds.


**O**

One, two, three…

*(she counted aloud, each shot hitting its target.)*

"Twenty-three!" she laughed, delighting in the chaos as the last alien's head exploded in a spray of gore.

As the battlefield fell silent, she stood amidst the carnage, a chilling figure of destruction.


**O**

And yet... I still feel nothing!

*(she declared, looking around at the lifeless bodies scattered around her.)*

The remaining aliens watched in horror, their morale shattered.


**Alien**

What are we even fighting against?

*(one whispered, fear evident in its voice.)*

**O** turned her attention to them, a sinister grin spreading across her face.


**O**

Oh, just a little taste of what happens when you cross me! Who's next?

The battle raged on until **O** felt a sudden jolt, her vision blurring as a bright light enveloped her. She had been overconfident, and in an instant, she was snatched away by a group of aliens, their grasp unyielding. Struggling to escape, she found herself tossed into a dark cell, the heavy door slamming shut with a resounding thud.


**O**

Ugh! Really? This is how you treat your guests?!" She kicked the metal door, rattling it. "You'll regret this!

With her claws, she clawed at the walls, but they were reinforced and held firm. Each scrape echoed in the empty chamber, growing increasingly frustrated.


**O**

Come on! This is supposed to be a high-security cell? I've seen better craftsmanship from a rusty old shed!" She switched tactics, aiming her weapons at the wall. "Let's see if vaporizing it works!

She fired, the energy blast illuminating the dark space, but the wall remained unscathed, absorbing the impact as if it were nothing.


**O**

What?! Are you kidding me?!" She huffed in annoyance, her patience wearing thin. "Fine, let's do this the old-fashioned way!

Summoning her strength, **O** unleashed a furious barrage of brute force against the wall, slamming her body against it. The impact reverberated through the cell, and with one final, powerful thrust, she smashed through the thick barrier, sending debris flying in all directions.


**O**

Freedom! Now, let's have some fun!

*(she cackled, stepping into the dimly lit corridor beyond.)*

Her eyes glinted with manic excitement, morphing into an intense "><" shape as the thrill of chaos ignited within her. She sprinted down the corridor, her claws ready to shred through anything in her path.

As she turned the corner, she spotted a group of **People** aliens huddled together, whispering nervously.


**O**

Oh, look! My little party guests!" She grinned wickedly, her tail flicking with anticipation. "Let's see how much fun we can have!

She lunged at them, claws slicing through the air, leaving trails of blood in her wake. One alien tried to flee, but she was faster, catching it by the arm.


**O**

Where do you think you're going?" With a swift motion, she tore off its limb, sending it screaming to the ground. "Awww, don't be scared! I'm just getting started!

Turning her attention to another alien, she activated her railgun arm and aimed it at the nearest target.


**O**

Let's make it a little more interesting!

*(She grinned as she pressed the trigger, launching a rocket that streaked through the air and collided with the alien. The explosion was massive, spraying blood and bits of gore across the walls.)*


**O**

Yummy!" she exclaimed, licking her claws as she surveyed the carnage. "Looks like it's dinner time!

As she moved deeper into the stronghold, she heard a commotion up ahead. It was **Arynn**, surrounded by a trio of **People** aliens, their weapons drawn and poised to strike.


**O**

Oh no, you don't!

*(she shouted, her eyes narrowing with fury.)*

She raised her railgun arm again, targeting the closest alien. Without hesitation, she fired, the shot ringing out like thunder. The alien's head exploded in a shower of blood and brain matter, and it crumpled to the ground, lifeless.


**O**

Nice try, but I'm not letting anyone touch my friends!

*(She leaped into the fray, claws glistening with anticipation.)*

The remaining aliens turned to face her, their expressions twisted in horror as they realized the threat standing before them.


**O**

Did you really think you could keep me locked up? Now it's your turn to suffer!

*(She laughed maniacally, her eyes gleaming with a savage delight.)*

As she plunged into the chaos, the air filled with screams and the sounds of her relentless assault, **O** became an unstoppable force, reveling in the slaughter and chaos, turning the alien stronghold into a gruesome playground.

After her rampage through the alien stronghold, **O** found herself in a strange predicament. The **People** aliens, now fully aware of her chaotic nature, had decided to invite her to a convention they were hosting. Perhaps it was some misguided attempt to appease her or maybe they thought showcasing her might keep the others in line. Regardless, **O** relished the idea of attending, envisioning a grand stage where she could shine.

When the day arrived, she dressed in an extravagant gown, a mix of shiny materials and bright colors that accentuated her fierce presence. The dress flowed dramatically as she moved, with jagged edges that mimicked her claws. A crown adorned her head, made from the remnants of her past victims—shiny bits of metal and alien technology that caught the light just right. She felt powerful, and the thought of parading in front of a room full of terrified aliens filled her with glee.

As she strutted onto the stage, the crowd of **People** aliens went silent, their eyes wide in a mix of awe and fear. The spotlight glared down on her, highlighting her wicked grin.


**O**

Hello, my delicious little snacks!" she cackled, her voice echoing through the auditorium. She wiggled her fingers and claws in delight, a glimmer of mischief in her eyes. "I hope you're ready for a real treat!

The aliens shifted uneasily in their seats, some exchanging terrified glances. **O** reveled in their fear, pacing back and forth on the stage, her claws glinting ominously.


**O**

What's the matter? You all look a little... uncomfortable!" she teased, her grin widening. "You're not scared, are you? Because I can smell the fear wafting off you like a fine perfume!

Suddenly, **D** joined her on stage, swaggering with a playful confidence that belied the situation. She aimed her gun arm at the audience, a mischievous twinkle in her eye.


**D**

Relax, folks! Just your friendly neighborhood drone here to make sure you're all... safe." She pointed her weapon dramatically, eliciting gasps from the crowd. "And maybe keep an eye out for any little snacks!

The aliens collectively flinched, some dropping their drinks as they grasped the full weight of their situation.

**Y** then leaped onto the stage, flexing his claws as he pretended to lunge at the audience.


**Y**

Don't worry! I'm not going to hurt you! Or am I?" He feigned a vicious swipe, and the crowd gasped again, laughter mixed with terrified shrieks. "Just kidding! Or am I?

The tension in the room was palpable, each alien on the verge of panic. They were all too aware of the playful menace before them. **T** followed suit, joining the chaos with his signature flair.


**T**

Ich kann nicht glauben, wie viele von euch hier sind!" He smirked, glancing at the crowd. "Ich hoffe, ihr habt genug Platz für alle eure Kacke!

The aliens, already on edge, couldn't handle the combination of humor and threat. The unexpected roast from **T** sent waves of nervous laughter and sheer horror throughout the audience.

**O**, enjoying the chaos, couldn't help but poke fun at their expense.


**O**

Wow, you all seem to have an infinite supply of... what was it? Shit?" She laughed heartily, throwing her head back as she cackled. "Maybe I should open a shop called ‘The Infinite Supply of Fear'! It would be a hit!

The crowd was in full disarray now, some laughing uncontrollably while others were desperately trying to compose themselves, but it was a lost cause. The atmosphere was charged with laughter and terror, the perfect recipe for a convention gone horribly right.

**O** stepped closer to the edge of the stage, leaning forward, her voice dropping to a conspiratorial whisper.


**O**

But let's be real... it wouldn't matter if I went on a snack spree. You're all so scared, you wouldn't even taste good! You'd just be... mush!

*(She cackled again, the sound echoing ominously through the hall.)*

**D**, **Y**, and **T** joined her in laughter, the camaraderie mixed with their chaotic energy creating a surreal spectacle.


**O**

Now, who wants to volunteer as my first course?" she asked playfully, raising her claws in a mock threat. "I promise to make it quick and painless... maybe!

The **People** aliens were now fully immersed in a combination of terror and amusement, and the whole auditorium erupted into chaos, laughter mingling with shouts of horror.

As the atmosphere swirled around them, **O** felt the thrill of the moment pulse through her. She wasn't just a weapon of destruction; she was the life of the party, and she intended to make this gathering unforgettable.

The auditorium buzzed with a mix of laughter and anxiety, the air thick with anticipation as **O** surveyed her audience. The combination of power and fear was intoxicating, and she was ready to escalate the chaos.

With a wicked grin plastered on her face, she scanned the crowd. "Who wants to come up and share some fun with me?" she called out, her voice dripping with sarcasm. Her gaze landed on one particularly nervous-looking alien in the front row. He glanced around, weighing his options, then bolted from his seat, sprinting toward the exit.

**O**<nowiki/>'s smile widened. "Oh, no, you don't!" She raised her arm, aiming her weapon with precision. In an instant, a shot rang out, echoing through the hall. The alien fell to the ground, lifeless, blood splattering across the stage.

A collective gasp erupted from the audience, and the remaining aliens froze in horror.

**O** laughed, the sound almost melodic amid the chaos. "See? This is what happens when you try to run! Now, who's next?" She leaned over the edge of the stage, beckoning another unfortunate alien forward.

This time, a different alien stood up, visibly trembling but compelled by some mix of curiosity and fear. He hesitantly made his way to the stage, eyes darting nervously.

"Come on up! Don't be shy!" **O** encouraged, her voice playful yet menacing. As he stepped closer, he opened his mouth to speak, but all that came out was a squeak followed by a loud, unmistakable sound. The poor alien's face turned beet red as he crapped himself, the smell wafting through the air.

The crowd erupted into laughter, a chaotic blend of fear and disbelief. **O** grinned wider. "Looks like someone is excited to meet me!"

The alien, now utterly humiliated, tried to gather his wits. "I-I wanted to—" he stammered, but his voice faltered as he glanced at the bloody remains of the alien **O** had just killed.

With a sudden movement, **O** lunged forward, grabbing him by the collar. "Aww, but you're too cute! Let's make this quick." She pulled out her dagger-like claw and stabbed him right in the heart. The alien's eyes widened in shock as he fell to the ground, gasping for breath.

Not satisfied with just that, **O** bent down and bit off his head in one swift motion, blood spraying everywhere. The crowd of **People** aliens, already on edge, collectively gasped again, the stench of death mingling with the overwhelming odor of fear and excrement filling the air.

"See? No need to be scared!" **O** called out, wiping her mouth with the back of her hand as she stood back up. "I'm just having a little fun!"

The remaining aliens, now in a state of utter panic, began to tremble in their seats, some fainting, others desperately trying to cover their noses.

As **O** pranced around the stage, savoring the chaos she had created, she noticed **Juliah**, her fellow drone, standing at the edge, visibly repulsed by the smell. **Juliah** took a step back, shaking her head.

"I can't stand this!" **Juliah** exclaimed, her circuits almost flickering with annoyance. "This stench is unbearable! I'm outta here!" With that, she turned and zoomed out of the auditorium, leaving **O** to revel in the chaos alone.

"Aw, come on, **Juliah**! Don't you want to see the encore?" **O** called after her, but her voice was drowned out by the cacophony of the terrified audience.

"Let's keep this party going, shall we?" she shouted, spinning around and pulling out her weapon again. "Who's next? I promise I won't bite... much!"

The remaining aliens exchanged horrified glances, clearly weighing their chances of survival. One brave soul, perhaps emboldened by the chaos, stood up again, trembling but determined.

"P-please, just don't hurt me!" he pleaded, his voice shaking.

"Relax! I'm not going to hurt you," **O** replied, her tone dripping with sarcasm. "Just a little game! How about a joke?"

The alien nodded vigorously, desperate to appease her.

"Why did the alien cross the road?" **O** began, pausing for dramatic effect. "To get away from the crazy drone on stage!"

The crowd burst into nervous laughter, the tension slightly easing but still hovering like a dark cloud. **O** chuckled along, feeding off their anxiety.

"But really, who wants to join me?" she continued, her eyes sparkling with delight. "I'll make you a star! Or maybe just a tasty snack!"

One more alien raised a trembling hand, only to quickly retract it as **O**'s gaze fell upon him. "Oh, you look like you have something to say! Come on up!"

He hesitated, glancing at his fellow aliens who were wide-eyed and pale, before finally inching forward.

"Um, what do you want?" he stuttered, clearly regretting his decision.

"What a great question! How about you show me your dance moves?" **O** suggested playfully, her tone dangerously sweet. "Let's see if you can impress me!"

The alien took a deep breath and began to sway awkwardly, trying to follow some imaginary rhythm. But just as he attempted to spin, he stumbled and fell flat on his face, letting out another noise of terror as he lost control of his bodily functions once again.

The audience erupted into a mix of laughter and screams, the stench reaching unbearable levels. **O** howled with laughter, clutching her sides.

"Someone get this guy a towel! Or maybe a new pair of pants!" she exclaimed, enjoying the pandemonium.

As the alien scrambled to his feet, face flushed with embarrassment, **O** decided to put him out of his misery. "Okay, okay! Enough fun for you!" She raised her weapon and shot him point-blank, the alien collapsing to the ground with a final, pitiful gasp.

The remaining aliens were now screaming, a few even fainting from the sheer horror. **O** took a step back, reveling in their fear, the blood and chaos around her becoming a thrilling backdrop to her antics.

"Remember, kids!" she yelled, leaning over the edge of the stage, her claws glinting dangerously in the lights. "Never run from your fears! Especially if they have sharp claws and a taste for snacks!"

The crowd, now in full panic mode, began to flee in every direction, knocking over chairs and tripping over one another. **O** cackled maniacally, her eyes gleaming with excitement as she watched the mayhem unfold.

In the midst of the chaos, **O** couldn't help but feel a thrill of satisfaction. She was the queen of chaos, the life of the party, and she intended to keep it that way.

"Who's next?!" she shouted, her voice ringing out over the noise. "Don't be shy! I promise I'll go easy on you... for now!"

But deep down, she knew there would be no mercy for anyone who dared to cross her path. The fun was just beginning.

**O** stood center stage, gleefully surveying the carnage she had created, her claws glinting ominously in the low light. But what really caught her attention wasn't the blood and screams — it was the unbearable, pungent stench that had now saturated the entire auditorium.

The aliens, once dignified and proud, were now reduced to pitiful, trembling wrecks, practically swimming in their own excrement. It was everywhere — the floor, their clothes, even the walls. The smell was suffocating, and the sheer volume of it was almost impossible to comprehend.

**O** winced, taking a step back as her senses were assaulted by the overwhelming stench. "Oh my god!" she groaned, her tone dripping with both disgust and exasperation. "You just… will not STTAAAAHHHPPPP!"

The crowd continued to panic, their collective terror only making the problem worse. More and more of them lost control, the sounds of splattering echoing across the hall. A few unlucky souls in the back row fainted, collapsing into puddles of the vile substance as others tripped and stumbled over them, their feet squelching in the foul mess. The once-opulent convention hall had become a nightmarish cesspool, and **O** was in the eye of the storm.

She raised a hand to her mouth, trying to stifle a gag. "Okay, seriously. I've killed a lot of you, stabbed a few, and even bitten off a head for fun. But this?" She pinched her nose in mock disgust, waving her free hand in front of her face. "This is just nasty!"

The aliens, too terrified to respond, merely whimpered as they cowered beneath her gaze, their bodies shaking uncontrollably.

**O**'s voice rose again, taking on an almost sing-song quality as she circled the stage like a predator playing with its prey. "I mean, how hard is it to keep your bowels in check? It's not like I'm doing anything *that* scary, right? Just a little maiming, a bit of slicing, maybe some casual dismemberment… and you all lose your freaking minds!" She paused, eyeing one alien in the front row who seemed on the verge of another "accident."

"Hold it in, buddy," she warned, leaning in closer, her sharp teeth glinting in the stage lights. "One more drop and I swear I'll—"

*SPLAT!*

The poor alien couldn't hold back anymore. The sheer terror of **O**<nowiki/>'s presence had pushed him over the edge, and the sound of his failure echoed across the room.

**O** recoiled, her face scrunching up in disgust as she backed away. "Ugh, are you serious?!" she screeched, throwing her hands up in frustration. "I just warned you! What is wrong with you people?!"

The alien looked mortified, but there was nothing he could do. He was trembling so violently now that even standing up seemed like a struggle. **O** let out an exaggerated sigh, clearly fed up.

"You know what? I'm done," she said flatly, turning away from the stage. "This isn't even fun anymore." Her boots squelched in the muck as she took a few steps away, her mood rapidly souring.

But then, just as she reached the edge of the stage, another loud, unmistakable sound rang out from somewhere in the middle of the room.

*SQUELCH!*

**O** froze, her back still to the crowd. Her fingers twitched at her sides, her claws flexing in agitation.

Slowly, she turned her head, her expression now a mix of disgust and incredulity. "Did someone just… again?"

The aliens all shrank back, terrified beyond belief.

"Unbelievable," **O** muttered under her breath. She clenched her fists, her claws scraping together with a metallic hiss. Without another word, she raised her arm and fired off two quick rounds into the crowd, hitting the unfortunate aliens responsible for the latest mess. Their bodies dropped instantly, but the panic in the room only escalated.

Some aliens began screaming, others sobbing uncontrollably. More fainted from sheer terror, collapsing into the now ankle-deep sludge covering the auditorium floor.

**O** sighed again, her patience worn thin. "Alright, you idiots… let's wrap this up." She leveled her weapon at the crowd, firing a few more rounds for good measure. Two more aliens fell to the floor with sickening thuds, but that wasn't enough for her.

"Seriously though," she started, her voice dripping with condescension as she paced across the stage, her claws leaving light scratches on the metal surface. "You all have a problem. Like, a *serious* problem." She paused, looking around at the remains of the once-pristine convention hall, now coated in alien blood, excrement, and chaos.

"I mean, how do you even function like this?" **O** continued, gesturing dramatically at the mess around her. "Is this, like, a normal Tuesday for you guys? You walk around, all high and mighty, pretending you're some big, bad race of *People* aliens, but the second things get rough, you just... lose it! Literally! You're crapping yourselves left and right!"

One particularly brave alien dared to make eye contact with her, and she zeroed in on him immediately. "You there!" she called out, pointing a claw in his direction. "Yeah, you. What do you have to say for yourself?"

The alien stammered, trying to form words, but all that came out was another horrified squeak. His face turned bright green — whether from fear or nausea, **O** couldn't tell — and then, with an almost comedic timing, he crapped himself again.

The crowd erupted into terrified whispers, the smell reaching a new level of unbearable. **O** threw her head back and let out a loud, exasperated groan. "Oh, come ON! Is this all you guys know how to do?!"

She aimed her weapon at the trembling alien, rolling her eyes as she fired another shot. He collapsed to the floor, motionless, the room growing eerily silent as everyone waited for **O**'s next move.

"Well, I guess that's one way to clean up the mess," she mused, stepping over the bodies as if they were mere obstacles in her way. She wiped some stray alien blood off her claws, flicking it carelessly onto the floor.

Another alien, clearly terrified, let out a soft whimper from the back of the room, and **O** raised an eyebrow. "Oh? Another volunteer for the ‘pants-shitting parade'?"

The whimpering grew louder, and **O** couldn't help but smirk. "I'm starting to think you guys have an *infinite* supply of crap. Seriously. Like, what even is this? Do you have some weird alien gland that just releases gallons of it when you're scared?"

The aliens stared at her in horror, too afraid to move, too terrified to even speak.

**O** took a deep breath and waved her hand dismissively. "You know what? I'm out. This is disgusting, even for me." She shot one last disgusted glance around the room before firing off two more rounds, dropping another pair of aliens who had been hiding near the back.

"Good riddance," she muttered, finally turning on her heel to leave. "I'll leave you all to wallow in your own filth. Maybe next time, you'll think twice before inviting me to one of your stupid little conventions."

As **O** stormed out of the room, her boots squelching one last time in the filth, she couldn't help but throw one final roast over her shoulder. "And hey, just a thought: maybe invest in some diapers next time! You're clearly going to need them!"


**O**

*("Well, well, well… what do we have here?")*

**O** sits back in her chair, one leg crossed over the other, rocking gently. Her claws tap rhythmically on the armrest, her tail swaying in amusement as her gaze locks onto the morbidly obese alien trembling in front of her.


**O**

*("You made a bit of a mess there, huh, tubby? Look at that.")*

She grins, pointing at the puddle of filth beneath him. *"Now, here's the deal—either you clean it up, or I start cleaning you up. Your choice."*

The alien looks around in a panic, sweating profusely.


**O**

*("Awww, don't look at them. They're not gonna help you. This is your mess.")*

She leans forward slightly, the faint glow from her railgun arm catching his terrified eyes. *"Get to work."*

The alien whimpers, falling to his knees and beginning to wipe the floor with his hands. **O** leans back in her chair, rocking gently, her tail wagging in delight.


**O**

*("That's the spirit. But you better hurry. I'm getting bored, and when I get bored…")*

She flexes her railgun arm, the energy whirring louder. *"Things tend to explode."*

The room is dead silent except for the frantic scrubbing. **O** glances at the other aliens huddled in the corner, their eyes wide with fear. She grins wickedly.


**O**

*("And you lot—don't even think about running. One more mess, and you'll be cleaning it up too.")*

Her gaze narrows on a smaller alien. *"I see you shaking. Don't even think about it."*

The smaller alien whimpers, visibly trembling. Before he can stop himself, he soils himself again.


**O**

*("Oh no way!")*

She laughs, throwing her head back. *"Another one? You guys are too easy!"*

She stands up, slowly pacing toward the group, her tail flicking behind her with every step. The smaller alien looks like he's about to faint. **O** leans down to his level, grinning.


**O**

*("You really need to get a grip. What are you so scared of? It's not like I'm gonna rip you apart. I mean, unless you give me a reason to.")*

The alien lets out a terrified squeal, making **O** cackle louder.


**O**

*("I swear, you guys must have an infinite supply of sh—")*

She stops, giggling darkly. *"Honestly, I might need to put all of you in diapers at this point. It's ridiculous!"*

She points her railgun arm at the group, the energy humming louder.


**O**

*("You better start cleaning that up too, tubby, or you're gonna regret it. Move faster!")*

The obese alien scrubs harder, his hands trembling as he tries to keep up with the mess.


**O**

*("Awww, look at him go! Poor guy's probably regretting everything right now. But hey, it's either clean the crap or become the crap, right?")*

Her eyes flicker with amusement as she sits back down, rocking in her chair again. Her tail taps lazily against the floor as she surveys the terrified aliens.


**O**

*("Honestly, this is getting boring. You lot just keep shitting yourselves. What's wrong with you? Seriously, you're making more work for tubby here, and at this rate, he's gonna need a mop.")*

The room remains tense, the other aliens too petrified to move.


**O**

*("Or…")*

She grins darkly, eyes glowing. *"Maybe I'll clean it up with your bodies."*

The aliens freeze in sheer terror as **O** chuckles, her claws tapping rhythmically on the armrest.


**O**

*("Come on, let's make this interesting. Who's next? Who's gonna crap themselves next? Because I'm just dying to see who makes the next mess.")*

She locks her eyes onto another alien, pointing her railgun arm casually in his direction.


**O**

*("You there. Think you can hold it together? Or are you about to make tubby's job even worse?")*

The alien stammers, trying to hold his composure, but his body shakes uncontrollably.


**O**

*("Awww, you look like you're about to burst. Don't worry, it's natural for weaklings like you.")*

She grins wider, her voice dripping with mock concern. *"But if you do, just remember—cleaning duty isn't over."*

Suddenly, **O** leans forward, her expression growing more sinister.


**O**

*("Actually, I've got an idea. How about you—")*

She points her railgun at the first alien.


**O**

*("—clean it up too. I'll let you take turns. Or maybe I should just blast you both into pieces? Decisions, decisions…")*

She lets out a long, drawn-out sigh, rocking back in her chair.


**O**

*("Nah. That's too easy. I wanna see you suffer a little more.")*

The morbidly obese alien continues scrubbing, his breathing labored as the rest of the group remains paralyzed with fear.


**O**

*("What's the matter?")*

She tilts her head, her glowing eyes glinting with sadistic glee. *"Scared? You should be. Because if I get tired of this little game, well… let's just say cleaning will be the least of your problems."*

She leans back in the chair, her tail wagging as she watches them squirm.


**O**

*("Keep it up, tubby. You're doing great. But remember—if any of you screw up again, things are gonna get real messy.")*

She pauses, flashing a sharp-toothed grin.


**O**

*("And trust me, I love a mess.")*

### EXT. SCENE

The dark corridors hummed with tension as the Gek alien, part of Arynn's squad, cautiously led the way through the damp, shadowy tunnels. His reptilian eyes darted around, sensitive to every small sound. He hated this place—the filth, the constant dripping from the pipes, and most of all, the horrendous stench.


**Gek**

*("Ugh, can we just get this over with? This place smells worse than a decomposing Togruta. And trust me, I've smelled one.")*

He winced, trying not to breathe too deeply.

Behind him, **O** sauntered along, casually rocking her railgun-enhanced arms back and forth. Her eyes glowed in the dim light, pupils shifting into a playful "><" as her tail swayed lazily behind her, like a cat stalking its prey. She didn't seem bothered by the filth or the stench—if anything, she seemed amused by it.


**O**

*("Oh, come on, Gek! This place has character!")*

She chuckled, her voice laced with a mischievous edge. *"And think of the fun we'll have if something tries to attack us."*

**Y** stepped up, his sharp, mechanical claws tapping the floor as he glanced around. He chuckled at **O**<nowiki/>'s words.


**Y**

*("I just hope there's something left for me after O's done playing.")*

**T** shook his head, his tail twitching as he walked beside them, muttering something sarcastic in German under his breath. **O** cackled at whatever **T** said, her laughter echoing eerily in the tunnels.

Suddenly, the Gek alien stopped dead in his tracks, his snout twitching as he caught a new scent—something far worse than the general filth of the tunnel. His eyes widened.


**Gek**

*("Oh no, nope, not going that way.")*

He turned and hurriedly walked back toward the group, waving his hands as if trying to bat the smell away.

**O**, grinning with far too much amusement, folded her arms as she leaned back against a grimy wall, watching the Gek with glowing eyes.


**O**

*("Aw, what's wrong, Gek? Too smelly for you? I thought you said you could handle anything.")*


**Gek**

*("No, I did not say that, and whatever's in there is worse than anything I've ever smelled in my life!")*

His voice was half panic, half disgust. *"I'm out."*

**O** pushed off the wall, transforming one of her arms into a railgun, the energy crackling ominously as she stepped past him, her grin never fading.


**O**

*("Relax, buddy. I'll handle this.")*

Her tail wagged with excitement as she moved forward, her eyes narrowing into an intense "><" as she gleefully approached the source of the smell. **Y** followed, his own claws gleaming, while **T** silently shook his head, muttering about how ridiculous it all was.

Suddenly, a group of hostile aliens appeared from the shadows, their grotesque forms moving quickly to surround them. Their eyes gleamed with malice as they closed in, but **O** didn't flinch.


**O**

*("Oh-ho-ho! Look what we have here!")*

She raised both of her arms, now fully transformed into railguns, and laughed sadistically.


**O**

*("This is going to be so much fun.")*

The Gek alien took a step back, wrinkling his snout as he tried to stay away from the fight but close enough to help his team. **O** wasted no time. With a sharp cackle, she unleashed a volley of shots, her railguns blasting through the enemy ranks with terrifying precision. Aliens were torn apart by the sheer force, their bodies splattering the walls and floor with blood and gore.


**O**

*("Ahhh, this never gets old.")*

As the last alien fell, gurgling in pain, **O** strode over and grabbed it by the neck. Her claws dug into its flesh as she lifted it effortlessly, her eyes glowing brighter with every moment.


**O**

*("You're lucky I'm in a good mood today. Otherwise, I'd really take my time with you.")*

She grinned, sharp teeth glinting in the low light.

The alien gasped for breath, trying to claw at her arm, but **O**'s grip was like iron. Without a second thought, she bit down hard on its shoulder, tearing off a chunk of flesh as the alien screamed in agony.


**O**

*("Mmm… Tasty.")*

She wiped the blood from her lips with the rag Arynn had given her earlier, savoring the taste as if it were a delicacy.

**Y**, watching from the sidelines, chuckled darkly.


**Y**

*("And I thought I was the violent one.")*

The Gek alien grimaced, still trying to keep his distance from the carnage.


**Gek**

*("I'm never getting used to this.")*

But **O** wasn't done. She tossed the now-limp alien aside and turned toward the remaining survivors, who were trembling with fear.


**O**

*("You guys still alive over there?")*

She called out mockingly, her voice dripping with cruelty. *"I can fix that."*

One of the aliens, trembling uncontrollably, tried to make a run for it. But **O** was faster. With a casual flick of her railgun, she fired a single shot, the energy blast tearing through his skull and dropping him instantly.


**O**

*("Oops.")*

She giggled, her tail wagging in satisfaction. *"Guess he won't be cleaning up after himself."*

The other aliens, now too terrified to even move, started shaking violently. Their bowels released in unison, splattering the ground with an overwhelming stench. The Gek alien nearly gagged again, backing away quickly.

**O** tilted her head, watching the scene with a growing smirk.


**O**

*("Wow, you guys have an infinite supply of shit, don't you?")*

She casually leaned back against the wall, rocking back and forth on her heels, her railguns still crackling with residual energy. Her tail flicked in amusement as she watched the aliens panic, their bodies betraying them with every passing moment.


**O**

*("Here's the deal. One of you is going to clean all this up, or I'll start vaporizing the lot of you.")*

She waved her railgun in the general direction of the group, her grin widening as she watched their horrified expressions.


**O**

*("And don't think for a second that I won't follow through.")*

One particularly morbidly obese alien was shoved forward by the others, his face a mask of terror as he stumbled to the ground, nearly choking on his own breath. **O**<nowiki/>'s gaze fixed on him, her tail twitching with excitement.


**O**

*("You.")*

She pointed at him lazily, her voice dripping with false sweetness. *"You're going to be my little cleaner. Scrub every inch of this place, and maybe… just maybe… I'll let you live."*

The alien scrambled to his feet, grabbing the nearest rag and frantically trying to wipe up the mess. **O** sat down in a nearby chair, casually rocking back and forth, her claws tapping against the armrest as she watched him work.


**O**

*("Faster.")*

She demanded, her tone growing sharp. *"I don't have all day."*

The morbidly obese alien whimpered, his hands shaking as he tried to clean faster, his breath coming in labored gasps.

**O** leaned back, her tail wagging playfully as she watched him struggle.


**O**

*("Look at you. Pathetic.")*

She grinned wider. *"It's almost sad. Almost."*

As the alien continued scrubbing, **O** raised her railgun and casually pointed it at his head.


**O**

*("By the way, if you try to run…")*

She purred. *"I'll vaporize you so fast you won't even know what hit you."*

The alien froze for a moment, sweat dripping down his face, before frantically resuming his task, terrified out of his mind.


**O**

*("Good boy.")*

She chuckled, her eyes glowing with amusement. *"Now get to work, because if there's even a speck left when I'm done here, I'll finish the job myself."*

### EXT. SCENE

The dimly lit chamber was a chaotic blend of shadows and flickering lights, the air thick with the stench of panic and waste. The remnants of the recent slaughter lay scattered across the floor, blood mixing with the filth of the sewer. **O**, her mood sinister yet playful, surveyed the scene with a gleeful grin, her eyes alight with the thrill of the hunt.

In the center of the chaos stood the morbidly obese alien, trembling as he attempted to clean the remnants of his comrades' fear. His hands shook uncontrollably, the rag in his grasp barely making a dent in the mess around him. Each movement seemed to agitate his already fragile state, the echoes of what had just transpired weighing heavily on his mind.

**O** sauntered over, her tail flicking behind her with mischievous anticipation. The sight of the tubby alien, now desperate and cornered, filled her with a delightful sense of power.


**O**

*("Oh, what a sad little sight you are!")*

She purred, her voice dripping with mockery. *"You can't even keep your friends alive, can you? Look at you, all alone and covered in your own mess!"*

With a predatory gleam in her eye, **O** approached the alien, her footsteps echoing in the eerie silence. She could practically smell the fear radiating from him, mingling with the stench of sweat and waste.

Suddenly, she lunged forward, catching the tubby alien off guard. With a swift motion, she sank her teeth into his arm, the flesh yielding easily beneath her razor-sharp fangs. The alien gasped, eyes wide with shock and pain as she tore off a sizable chunk, savoring the taste of his flesh.


**O**

*("Mmm… tasty!")*

She said between bites, her voice gleeful. She chewed thoughtfully for a moment, then spat the remaining flesh onto the ground with a loud splat.


**O**

*("Ugh! That was a bit chewy. You really should eat more greens, tubby!")*

She laughed, a high-pitched cackle that echoed through the chamber, sending shivers down the alien's spine.

As if to emphasize her point, a gurgling sound erupted from the tubby alien's midsection, and with a horrified expression, he doubled over, a river of excrement flooding out of him in a desperate rush. The foul liquid cascaded to the ground, pooling around his feet and mingling with the remnants of his fallen comrades.

**O** watched with wide eyes, unable to suppress her laughter.


**O**

*("Well, that's one way to make a mess!")*

She cackled, her voice filled with twisted delight. *"I guess your diet isn't working out too well, is it?"*

The tubby alien groaned, his face flushed with embarrassment and fear. As he tried to regain his composure, **O** stepped closer, her eyes narrowing in mischief.


**O**

*("Well, you won't be needing those pants anymore if your fat ass keeps shitting yourself.")*

With a swift motion, she clawed at the fabric of his pants, tearing through the material effortlessly. The sound of ripping cloth echoed through the chamber as she left a trail of shredded fabric in her wake.

The tubby alien yelped, trying to cover himself, but **O** was far too quick.


**O**

*("No, no, no! We can't have that!")*

She taunted, her voice laced with wicked glee. *"You need to be exposed for all to see how pathetic you are!"*

She stepped back, admiring her handiwork as the tubby alien squirmed, now half-naked and covered in his own mess.


**O**

*("And here I thought I'd have to force you to strip. You're doing a fine job of it yourself!")*

The stench in the chamber intensified, and **O** wrinkled her nose in response.


**O**

*("Yuck! This is getting disgusting!")*

She reached into her pocket, producing a gas mask that she strapped over her face, ensuring her delicate senses wouldn't be assaulted further by the putrid smell.


**O**

*("Ah, much better!")*

She said, her voice slightly muffled but still dripping with sarcasm. *"Now, where were we?"*

Turning her attention back to the tubby alien, she pointed her railgun directly at him, the weapon crackling with energy.


**O**

*("Now, let's see if you can clean this mess up or if I'll have to make things even messier.")*

The alien gulped, a bead of sweat trickling down his forehead as he realized the precarious position he was in.


**O**

*("I don't think you want to find out what happens if I get bored.")*

She leaned in closer, her eyes narrowing dangerously. *"You'll end up like your friends over there. Or worse."*

The tubby alien nodded frantically, tears of desperation forming in his eyes as he picked up his pace, but **O** wasn't satisfied.


**O**

*("Oh, don't cry! It just makes the whole thing more entertaining!")*

She leaned back in her chair, rocking gently as she continued to aim her railgun at him, the weapon still crackling with energy.


**O**

*("You're doing great! Keep it up! Or I might just have to help you—)*

and you won't like how I help!"*

Suddenly, the Gek alien appeared in the doorway, his eyes wide as he took in the scene.


**Gek**

*("Uh, O? Are you sure this is a good idea? It really smells in here!")*

**O** turned her head, grinning as she spotted her ally.


**O**

*("Oh, Gek! Just in time! Come and witness the fun! Your little friend here is just about to learn the meaning of pain!")*

The Gek alien hesitated, wrinkling his snout at the overpowering stench that filled the room.


**Gek**

*("I don't think I want to see this…")*

**O** laughed, the sound echoing through the chamber.


**O**

*("Oh, but you have to! It's a real treat! Trust me, you won't regret it!")*

As she turned her attention back to the tubby alien, a dark glimmer sparked in her eye.


**O**

*("You know, it's not just about cleaning up your shit. It's about the thrill of the hunt!")*

With that, she raised her railgun, the barrel gleaming ominously under the flickering lights.


**O**

*("You're on borrowed time here, tubby! Let's see if you can make it out without soiling yourself again!")*

The tubby alien squeaked, desperately mopping up the mess as his body quaked with fear.


**O**

*("Remember, if you don't clean this mess, I'll make it your mess instead!")*

As he stumbled and fumbled, nearly slipping in his own mess, **O** laughed loudly, her voice echoing in the chamber.


**O**

*("This is just too good! Someone should really write this down!")*

She watched with rapt attention, the thrill of power coursing through her veins. The tubby alien was nothing more than a plaything, and she intended to make the most of it.


**O**

*("You're doing great! Keep it up! Or I might just have to help you—)*

and you won't like how I help!"*

Suddenly, she flipped her railgun, spinning it around with ease as if it were a toy.


**O**

*("So, tell me, how many times do you think you can shit yourself before I lose my patience?")*

The tubby alien, still shaking, scrambled to his feet, desperately grabbing the rag and attempting to wipe up the flood of filth around him.


**O**

*("Faster!")*

She demanded, her voice sharp. *"I want this place spotless! Or I swear, I'll turn you into a new kind of mess!"*

The Gek alien watched the chaos unfold, a mixture of horror and fascination on his face.


**Gek**

*("You really enjoy this, don't you?")*

**O** turned her head with a mischievous grin.


**O**

*("Oh, absolutely! It's like a game to me. Who knew cleaning could be so entertaining?")*

The tubby alien, on the verge of collapse, threw the rag aside and fell to his knees, defeated.


**O**

*("Oh, what's this? Giving up already? That's not very sporting of you!")*

She leaned in closer, her eyes glinting with malicious glee. *"You know, I always wanted a pet. But I never thought I'd end up with a squishy little thing like you!"*

The Gek alien shook his head, still trying to comprehend the sheer absurdity of the situation.


**Gek**

*("You're really something, O.")*


**O**

*"I know, right? I'm like a walking nightmare!"

### A DARK CHAMBER

The atmosphere was thick with tension as **O** loomed over the tubby alien, her eyes sparkling with an unsettling blend of delight and mischief. The faint sounds of chaos echoed in the distance, but here, in this dimly lit chamber, all focus was on her newest plaything. The tubby alien trembled, his remaining arm shaking as he wiped futilely at the mess around him.

**O** leaned in closer, her gaze locked on the alien's other arm.


**O**

*("Well, this just won't do. You can't have one good arm and one bad one! Let's make it even, shall we?")*

Before he could protest, she lunged forward, her sharp teeth sinking into the soft flesh of his other arm. The sensation was exhilarating; she could feel the warmth of his blood trickling down as she bit off the limb with a swift, brutal motion.


**O**

*("Mmm, delicious!")*

she exclaimed, savoring the taste. She pulled back, the severed arm clutched in her hands, and she began to suck on it like a vampire, her eyes rolling back in pleasure. *"You really should consider a diet, tubby. But I must say, you're quite tasty!"*

The alien gurgled in shock, his remaining appendage pressed against the bloody stump, disbelief and horror etched across his face.

**O** chuckled darkly, enjoying the sight of his utter despair. The dim light flickered above them, casting shadows that danced across the walls, but she had other plans.


**O**

*("Let's make this a little more... atmospheric.")*

With a quick movement, she turned her railgun toward the overhead lamp.

**BANG!**

The shot rang out, and the bulb shattered, plunging the chamber into darkness, illuminated only by the soft, eerie glow of moonlight streaming in from the distant rings of **Lizard-753-Y** and the two moons, **Polska** and **Uziara**. The shadows enveloped them, creating an intimate but sinister ambiance.


**O**

*("Ah, now that's better. A little mood lighting for our fun.")*

She glanced back at the tubby alien, whose terror was palpable. He was now nearly defenseless, left with just a pathetic stump where his other arm used to be, panic flooding his face as the realization of his imminent doom sank in.


**O**

*("You know, I really should be leaving soon. But before I do, I think it's time to clean house.")*

Without warning, she aimed her railgun at the ceiling and shot a powerful RPG from her arm. The projectile zipped through the air, lighting up the room momentarily before it struck the far wall with a deafening explosion.

**KABOOM!**

The blast echoed through the chamber, and chaos erupted. Debris rained down, and the walls splattered with the remnants of the tubby alien and the other unfortunate souls caught in the blast. Blood, guts, and waste filled the room, creating a gruesome tableau that would haunt anyone who dared enter afterward.

**O** stepped back, surveying her handiwork with a satisfied grin. The moonlight illuminated the carnage, casting eerie shadows over the macabre scene.


**O**

*("There we go! Much better! A real masterpiece of destruction! Just what I needed to spice up my day!")*

The remnants of the alien bodies lay strewn about, a grotesque reminder of her power.

**O** turned to the Gek alien, who stood frozen in shock, his eyes wide as he took in the horrific aftermath.


**O**

*("You see, Gek? That's how you handle a little trash.")*

She gestured to the mess around her, a proud smile plastered across her face. *"If you can't clean up your own mess, you might as well make sure it's really messy!"*

The Gek alien swallowed hard, his snout wrinkling at the stench that now filled the chamber.


**Gek**

*("You really are a force of nature, O. But I think you might have gone a bit overboard this time…")*

**O** shrugged, her mood still buoyant.


**O**

*("Overboard? Never heard of it! Besides, it's just a little fun! You should try it sometime!")*

With that, she turned on her heel, ready to leave the chaos behind.


**O**

*("Remember, Gek, it's not about being messy. It's about being memorable! Now, shall we?")*

As she exited the chamber, she glanced back one last time, taking in the grisly scene.


**O**

*("I'll leave this as a reminder for the next unfortunate soul who dares to cross my path! Good luck cleaning this up!")*

With a final chuckle, she disappeared into the shadows, her laughter echoing in the empty hallways, leaving behind nothing but the gruesome reminder of her chaotic rampage.

### THE RUINED BUILDING

As the dust settled from her explosive exit, **O** took a moment to savor the sweet taste of chaos lingering in the air. The crumbling structure behind her groaned under the weight of its destruction, collapsing in on itself as if it couldn't bear the memories of what had transpired within its walls.

**O** grinned, her sharp teeth glinting in the moonlight.


**O**

*("Now that was a blast! Literally!")*

She unfurled her wings, letting the night air rush past her as she prepared for takeoff. With a powerful beat, she soared into the sky, leaving behind the remnants of her rampage. The moonlight painted her figure in silver as she climbed higher, the stars twinkling like distant eyes witnessing her descent into madness.

As she flew, she removed her gas mask, the stench of the previous carnage dissipating in the open air.


**O**

*("Ah, fresh air! Much better than the smell of alien waste!")*

She cackled into the night, her laughter echoing like a haunting melody across the desolate landscape. The thrill of destruction buzzed through her veins, a delicious high that drove her forward. But her night was far from over.

Suddenly, out of the corner of her eye, she spotted movement below—a flash of green hiding behind a tree.


**O**

*("Oh? What's this? A little alien trying to play hide and seek?")*

She swooped down, gliding gracefully through the night sky before landing silently atop the tree, her claws digging into the bark.


**O**

*("Come out, come out, wherever you are!")*

The alien, a small and nervous creature, peeked out from behind the trunk, its eyes wide with terror as they locked onto her. It hesitated for a moment, weighing its options. Then, in a panic, it darted back to hide completely.

**O** couldn't help but laugh, the sound ringing out in the quiet forest.


**O**

*("Oh, you poor little thing! Hiding won't save you from me!")*

With a mischievous glint in her eye, she reached into her pouch and pulled out a book—one she had taken from the ruined building as a keepsake. It was an odd choice, an inconspicuous hardcover filled with ancient tales, but it was perfect for her dark humor.


**O**

*("How about a little reading material for our time together?")*

With a flick of her wrist, she dropped the book from her perch, watching as it landed with a soft thud on the forest floor. The alien, peeking out again, seemed momentarily distracted by the unexpected gift.


**O**

*("You like stories, don't you? Because your story is about to end!")*

In a flash, she leaped down from the tree, landing with a predator's grace right in front of the hiding alien. Before it could react, she lunged forward, her sharp teeth sinking into its neck. The alien barely had time to scream before she bit its head clean off, her mouth stained with its ichor.


**O**

*("Mmm, a perfect little snack for my journey back to Arynn!")*

She savored the taste, holding the severed head in her hands as if it were a prized delicacy.


**O**

*("What a delightful treat! I should have done this sooner!")*

With the head secured in one hand, she took to the air again, soaring high above the treetops. As she flew, she marveled at the landscape below, a tapestry of dark shadows and moonlit highlights.


**O**

*("Seven hours, huh? Let's make this flight interesting!")*

She decided to target the building she had just demolished, the remnants still smoking. With a gleeful expression, she aimed her arm—now a deadly railgun—and began to fire RPG shots at the structure, sending explosive rounds spiraling downwards.

**BOOM!** **BOOM!** **BOOM!**

The rounds struck with precision, creating further devastation. Each explosion sent debris flying, and she reveled in the destruction, her laughter intertwining with the sounds of crumbling concrete and panicked alien screams.


**O**

*("This is the best flight ever! Just look at it go! So much fun!")*

As she continued to unleash her mayhem, she felt invincible, soaring through the air with the wind at her back and the thrill of destruction in her heart. The night was hers, and she intended to make the most of it.

After what felt like hours of flying and destruction, she finally caught sight of **Lizard-616-B** in the distance, the lush greenery of the land contrasting sharply with the chaos she left behind.


**O**

*("Home sweet home! Arynn will love my little snack! I bet he's starving!")*

As she approached the base, she could see Arynn waiting outside, his expression a mix of curiosity and apprehension.


**Arynn**

*("O! What did you get into this time?")*

With a flourish, **O** landed gracefully in front of him, her demeanor shifting from chaotic thrill to playful mischief.


**O**

*("Just a little fun, Arynn! I brought you a snack! But I might have gotten a bit carried away…")*

She held up the severed head, a grin plastered across her face.


**O**

*("Thought you might like to share! I saved the best for last!")*

Arynn's eyes widened, a mixture of horror and amusement crossing his face.


**Arynn**

*("You really need to stop bringing me these... gifts.")*

**O** shrugged, her laughter ringing out as she tossed the head over her shoulder, watching it land with a soft thud.


**O**

*("Nah, I think I'll keep it up! It's way too much fun to mess with them!")*

With that, she flitted inside, leaving behind a trail of chaos and a bewildered Arynn. The night was still young, and O had more adventures planned.

### Chapter 1: The Call to Action
**D** hovered impatiently, her eyes narrowed as she regarded **Arynn** with an intensity that left no room for negotiation.


**D**

*("Arynn, you really need to head to Talc-616 B, the Pillared Planet. It's critical for our mission!")*

**O**, lounging lazily nearby, stretched her arms, letting out a yawn that revealed her sharp, glistening teeth.


**O**

*("Talc-616 B? Seriously? Have you seen the anomaly strength over there? It's like asking for a buffet of doom!")*

**D** raised an eyebrow, her tone firm.


**D**

*("We can't ignore it, O. If we don't scout it out, we risk missing crucial intel on the People aliens.")*

**O** rolled her eyes but felt a twinge of curiosity.


**O**

*("Fine, but I'm not promising to play nice if things go sideways. I like my snacks alive, you know.")*

Together, they rocketed into the air, a blur of color and energy, **O**'s wings fanning out as they flew in formation.

### Chapter 2: Scouting the Unseen
As they scouted the skies, they spotted a **People alien** scuttling across the ground below, its form a grotesque amalgamation of features that O found irresistible.


**D**

*("Target acquired! Watch my back.")*

With a swift movement, **D** darted down, her tail poised for the kill.


**D**

*("This one's mine!")*

In a flash, she beheaded the creature, its head rolling away as the body slumped to the ground.


**O**

*("Nice work! But let's see if it tastes as good as it looks!")*

D bent down, attempting a bite, but quickly recoiled.


**D**

*("Ugh! This is disgusting! Tastes like rancid space meat!")*

She tossed the head aside, grimacing in revulsion.

**O** laughed, her eyes twinkling with mischief.


**O**

*("I guess not every snack is a winner!")*

Suddenly, a flickering light caught their attention, drawing their eyes to a billboard nearby. The words "**HURRICANE APPROACHING**" blared in red, illuminated against the dark sky.


**O**

*("Well, isn't that just lovely? Let's find somewhere to hide!")*

They took off toward the nearby alien structure, a decrepit building that was once a gym but now lay in ruins, perfect for taking cover from the impending storm.

### Chapter 3: The Alien Shit Building
Inside the building, the howling winds began to roar, and the sound of rain slamming against the roof echoed ominously.


**O**

*("This place stinks even worse than that alien meat!")*

With a flick of her wrist, she conjured a small flame using her **Yabitanitic acid**, illuminating the dank, dark corners of the building.


**D**

*("We need to keep moving. Stay close.")*

The two of them began to explore the shadows of the gym, stepping over remnants of old equipment, rusted and covered in a thick layer of grime.

Suddenly, they stumbled upon **Y**, **T**, and **Juliah**, who were crouched together, their expressions a mix of concern and excitement.


**Y**

*("We're glad to see you! We were just—")*

But before he could finish, **Juliah** held up her grotesque organic tail, using it as a lamp to light the way.


**Juliah**

*("I found some supplies over here, but no sign of anyone else. Just darkness.")*

The wind outside screamed, rattling the windows, creating an eerie backdrop to their exploration.


**O**

*("Anyone else feel like we're in a horror movie? The kind where everyone dies?")*

**T** chuckled, glancing at the others.


**T**

*("I'd rather be the last one standing, thank you very much.")*

Just as the tension began to settle, a drone designed by the People aliens whirred into view, caught in the wild winds and rain.


**O**

*("What's that? A flying piece of trash?")*

She narrowed her eyes, her gaze sharp and predatory.


**O**

*("Time to show it who's boss!")*

### Chapter 4: The Hostile Takeover
With a feral grin, **O** aimed her arm at the drone, feeling the familiar hum of her weapon powering up.


**O**

*("Let's see how it likes a little friendly fire!")*

**D** leaned in, her own weapon at the ready, eyes glinting with anticipation.


**D**

*("You got this, O! Show that ugly thing what happens when you mess with us!")*

**O** unleashed a flurry of rounds, the bullets whizzing through the air and striking the drone's bald head.


**O**

*("Ha! Look at it! It's so ugly it doesn't even have fangs or a tail! What a loser!")*

The others joined in with their own playful insults, letting loose with laughter as the drone sputtered and struggled against the wind.


**Y**

*("It's like a bad joke come to life!")*


**T**

*("And look, no wings! How pathetic!")*

But just as they thought they had the upper hand, the storm surged, flooding the room with a mixture of alien excrement and rainwater.


**O**

*("Ew! This is disgusting!")*

### Chapter 5: The Escape to the Second Floor
Realizing the room was becoming more like a sewer than a shelter, the squad scrambled up the stairs to the second floor, narrowly avoiding the rising tide of filth.


**O**

*("This is not how I wanted my day to go!")*

As they reached the second floor, they spotted the People drone standing there, seemingly unbothered by the chaos around it.


**D**

*("Looks like we're not done yet!")*

The drone lunged at them with a mechanical roar, but **D** was quicker. She stabbed her **Yabitanitic acid** tail straight into the drone, and the acidic substance began to dissolve the machine's body.


**D**

*("Take that!")*

But the drone regenerated half of its body, its circuits sparking angrily.


**O**

*("Oh no, you don't! Not on my watch!")*

With a fierce growl, she lunged forward, sinking her teeth into the drone's neck and biting its head off with a sickening crunch.


**O**

*("Now that's a snack I can get behind!")*

### Chapter 6: The Feast of Chaos
The squad gathered around the remnants of the drone, a twisted smirk spreading across **O**'s face.


**O**

*("Well, it's not the best dinner I've had, but I'm hungry!")*

**Y** looked skeptical, his expression a mix of disgust and amusement.


**Y**

*("I suppose we can say we had a… unique meal tonight.")*

**T** raised an eyebrow, glancing at the grotesque scene.


**T**

*("Not my first choice, but at least it's fresh!")*

As they feasted, they couldn't help but banter, the dark humor mingling with their laughter in the dim light of the room.

**Juliah**, holding her makeshift lamp, shined it on the scene.


**Juliah**

*("I can't believe we're eating this. What have we become?")*

**O** shrugged, licking her lips clean.


**O**

*("Survival of the fittest, my dear Juliah! Plus, we have to make the most of our situation!")*

The room echoed with their laughter as they dug into their peculiar feast, oblivious to the chaos swirling outside, the hurricane raging against their sanctuary, washing away the remnants of the People aliens and their drones.

### Chapter 7: Reflections in the Eye of the Storm
The winds howled outside, but inside the alien shit building, a sense of camaraderie began to bloom among the squad.


**O**

*("You know, maybe this storm isn't so bad after all. We've got each other, and we've got snacks!")*


**D**

*("Let's hope it passes soon. I'm not keen on becoming a meal for the hurricane.")*

**Y** laughed, looking around at his comrades.


**Y**

*("With O around, I don't think we have to worry about that!")*

The storm continued to rage outside, but within the walls of their makeshift refuge, they found a bizarre sense of comfort. The bonds forged in the chaos, the shared laughter, and the thrill of the hunt drew them closer together, stronger as a squad.

**O** raised her head, her eyes gleaming in the darkness.


**O**

*("To survival! To us!")*

With their spirits high, they continued to share stories, laughter, and the remnants of their unusual meal as the storm raged on outside, unaware of the dangers lurking in the shadows.

### Chapter 8: The Calm After the Storm
Hours later, as the storm finally began to abate, the winds softened, and the rain dwindled to a gentle patter.


**D**

*("Looks like the worst is over. Time to regroup and assess our next move.")*


**O**

*("You mean we can leave this stinky place? Thank the stars!")*

As they prepared to venture back outside, **Juliah** flicked her tail, casting light on the remnants of the drone they had feasted on.


**Juliah**

*("Should we check for survivors? We might not be the only ones stuck here.")*

**Y** nodded, a serious look in his eyes.


**Y**

*("Good idea. Let's be cautious. We don't want to walk into another ambush.")*

As they stepped out into the aftermath of the hurricane, the world outside had transformed into a surreal landscape, debris scattered everywhere, the air thick with the scent of rain mixed with the remnants of alien waste.

The storm had washed away the threats, but new dangers always lurked in the shadows, and their adventure was far from over.

### Chapter 9: A New Day Dawned
The sun broke through the clouds, casting a golden hue over the battered landscape. **O** stretched her wings, reveling in the warm light after the chaos of the storm.


**O**

*("Well, look at that! A new day! Let's see what Talc-616 B has in store for us next.")*

As they gathered their gear, they knew their mission was just beginning. Together, they would face whatever challenges lay ahead, stronger and more united than ever.

### THE RETURN TO ARYNN'S BASE

*The storm had finally subsided, leaving behind the aftermath of chaos. The group of drones, battered but not broken, trudged through the wreckage of the construction site. As they neared Arynn's base, the setting sun cast a warm glow over the damaged structures. They walked into the heart of the compound, where Arynn was overseeing repairs.*


**Juliah**

*(voice tired but steady, as she steps forward)*

We survived, but just barely. The storm did a number on us.


**T**

*(mechanical voice with a hint of concern)*

The defenses held, but we lost some equipment. The aliens... they weren't easy to shake off.

*Arynn looks up from his monitors, his expression unreadable, his posture relaxed as he watches them enter.*


**Arynn**

*(smirking, voice calm but proud)*

I had no doubt you'd make it through. You've been through worse. Glad to see you're in one piece.


**Juliah**

*(with a slight shrug)*

Barely. It wasn't pretty, but we managed. The site's still standing, though. It's mostly salvageable.


**T**

*(with a hint of irritation)*

They're persistent, Arynn. And the storm didn't make it any easier. We fought them off, but it wasn't clean. We're going to need time to rebuild.

*Arynn nods, walking over to a nearby console, pulling up a holographic map of the area.*


**Arynn**

*(voice turning serious)*

The storm was an inconvenience, but the real threat is still out there. Those aliens will be back, and they won't stop. We can't just keep defending. We need to take the fight to them.


**Juliah**

*(raising an eyebrow)*

You want to go after them?

*Arynn's eyes flicker with a steely resolve.*


**Arynn**

Exactly. We can't afford to sit around and wait for them to strike again. We hit them first. Hard.


**T**

*(nodding, voice determined)*
