That's... a good strategy. We've been playing defense for too long. I'm ready for it.

*Juliah crosses her arms, still considering Arynn's words.*


**Juliah**

*(smirking slightly)*

You really think we're ready for an offensive? We've got some damage to patch up.


**Arynn**

*(turning to face them, his tone firm but confident)*

We've got enough. The Lizards didn't survive this long by sitting around. Tomorrow, we strike. The aliens won't expect us to come for them—let's show them what happens when you push the Lizards too far.

*He pulls up a new map, zooming in on one of Lizard-953-E's moons.*


**Arynn**

There's a signal coming from this moon. It's too strong to ignore. I think it's time we found out what's really going on.


**Juliah**

*(grinning, her tail flicking with excitement)*

Sounds like you've got a plan. So, we're going in after them?


**Arynn**

*(smiling darkly)*

We're going to make them regret ever thinking they could invade us. But we're not doing it alone. Get the others. We're going to need everyone.

*T's eyes glow as it processes the orders.*


**T**

*(in its precise tone)*

Understood. I will gather the others and prepare for deployment.


**Juliah**

*(with a wink, her voice playful)*

Guess I'd better get some rest then. We've got a big day tomorrow.

*Arynn watches her for a moment, then turns back to the monitors.*


**Arynn**

Rest while you can. Tomorrow, we fight. We reclaim what's ours.

### ARYNN'S PLAN

*As the group starts to disperse to prepare for the upcoming mission, Arynn turns, his mind already moving onto the next step. His eyes are sharp, focused—there's no time to waste. Juliah pauses mid-step, sensing a shift in the atmosphere.*


**Juliah**

*(turning back toward him)*

What's on your mind, Arynn? Something more than just the aliens?

*Arynn doesn't immediately respond, his eyes lingering on the map in front of him before he meets her gaze.*


**Arynn**

*(voice calm but resolute)*

We're not just dealing with these aliens alone. There's another group we need to consider. The shapeshifters.


**Juliah**

*(frowning slightly)*

Shapeshifters? What do you mean? They're not exactly known for being... reliable allies.

*Arynn steps closer, his eyes hardening as he speaks.*


**Arynn**

I know. But their abilities are something we need to leverage. I've been watching their movements for a while now. They've got the capacity to infiltrate, to disrupt our enemies in ways we can't. If we want to take the offensive, we're going to need their skills.


**T**

*(processing the information, its voice steady but with a hint of skepticism)*

The shapeshifters are not to be trusted easily. Are you sure they'll cooperate, Arynn?


**Arynn**

*(nodding firmly)*

They will. If we offer them something they want—something more than just our territory. We'll need to meet with their leader, arrange a deal. But this isn't just about force. We need their... flexibility.

*Juliah looks thoughtful for a moment, her eyes narrowed.*


**Juliah**

A deal, huh? Sounds risky. And if they turn on us?


**Arynn**

*(his voice cold with certainty)*

Then we'll make sure they regret it. But we can't afford to be overly cautious. If we want to make a statement, we need all the cards on the table.

*The group falls silent for a moment, considering the implications of what Arynn is saying. The shapeshifters could be a wildcard—one that could either be the key to victory or a major liability.*


**T**

*(with a mechanical sigh)*

Understood. We will need to prepare for both outcomes. It's a dangerous game, but... I am ready for it.


**Juliah**

*(grinning, her tail flicking with excitement)*

Well, I'm not one to back down from a good challenge. Alright, Arynn. We're with you. Let's go meet these shapeshifters.

*Arynn gives a sharp nod, his eyes intense as he moves toward the exit, the others following closely behind.*


**Arynn**

Prepare yourselves. We're heading out to their territory. This meeting could change everything.

*The drones and Arynn make their way toward the rendezvous point, the mood shifting from cautious optimism to a quiet, determined readiness. Whatever happened next, they would face it together.*

### THE SHAPESHIFTERS' TERRITORY ON LIZARD-753-N
*The group traveled through the thick atmosphere of Lizard-753-N, its oceans visible from orbit beneath the swirling clouds. Arynn's ship, a sleek, powerful vessel, plunged into the planet's dense air. The re-entry was anything but smooth, the ship shaking violently as turbulence ripped through the atmosphere.*


**Juliah**

*(holding onto a handle above her seat, grinning through the jolts)*

This is... a *lovely* ride, Arynn. Are you sure you've got this under control?


**T**

*(flipping switches and checking the instruments, voice steady)*

No need to worry, Juliah. I've analyzed the ship's stabilization systems. It's just the atmosphere. It's a rough re-entry, but manageable.


**Arynn**

*(eyes fixed on the ship's dashboard, his voice calm but focused)*

We'll be down in a few minutes. Brace yourselves.

*The ship shudders as they push through the final layers of the planet's thick clouds, suddenly bursting through into the calm blue skies. Below, the vibrant ocean stretched as far as the eye could see, islands dotting the landscape like tiny jewels. The ship glides smoothly now, cutting through the air toward a secluded beach lined with lush vegetation.*

*As the ship touches down, the noise of the storm that had torn through the area earlier becomes a distant memory. The team disembarks from the ship, the warm air and rich scents of saltwater and tropical flowers hitting them immediately. Arynn steps out first, his boots sinking slightly into the soft sand, while the drones follow, scanning the surroundings with their advanced sensors.*


**Arynn**

*(taking a deep breath, eyes scanning the area, with a mix of curiosity and suspicion)*

Let's move. They should be close.

*The path toward the shapeshifter's clan is marked with totem-like stones and the faint echo of ancient rituals carried on the breeze. As they approach a clearing near the water's edge, they see the clan leader waiting for them—a tall, imposing figure, standing with a calm yet intense presence. Behind them, a strange rope-like contraption hangs from a nearby tree. From it, a creature thrashes wildly, its body contorted in strange, almost aquatic movements.*


**Clan Leader**

*(with a hint of pride, eyes gleaming as he gestures toward the creature)*

You've arrived. Welcome to our domain. You are looking at something extraordinary—a rare catch from the deep waters.


**Juliah**

*(staring at the creature curiously, her voice dry and teasing)*

Is that... a mermaid? It looks kind of *short* and cute, don't you think?


**T**

*(its voice slightly amused, calculating, voice almost mechanical)*

Certainly smaller than expected. I would say *adorable* would be an understatement.

*The clan leader blinks at their comments, clearly taken aback for a moment, then his face flushes with embarrassment. He shifts his posture slightly, an awkward chuckle escaping his lips as he avoids their eyes.*


**Clan Leader**

*(slightly blushing, muttering under his breath)*

It's... it's not just a *mermaid*... It's an *Aqualith.* They're rare and difficult to catch. We're fortunate.

*Juliah can't help but smirk, sensing the discomfort in the clan leader.*


**Juliah**

*(grinning)*

No worries, I was just joking. It's still cute.

*The clan leader takes a moment to recover, visibly awkward as he moves to the creature, which is still wriggling in midair, its slick scales glistening under the light. The creature's tail flicks wildly, splashing droplets of water in all directions.*


**Clan Leader**

*(addressing Arynn as he gestures toward the creature)*

You see, this one is 9 feet long, the size of a fully grown Aqualith. They're both beautiful and dangerous. These creatures can take down entire hunting parties if you're not careful.

*Arynn steps forward, inspecting the creature more closely. His gaze shifts between the thrashing Aqualith and the clan leader, impressed by both the creature's size and the skill required to capture it.*


**Arynn**

*(nodding, admiration in his voice)*

Impressive. How did you catch that *little fella*?

*The clan leader smiles, his pride clearly returning as he explains the method of capture. He moves closer to the creature, his hands carefully adjusting the ropes that hold it suspended.*


**Clan Leader**

We use a special technique—*luring* them with the scent of a certain type of kelp. They can't resist it, and when they surface, we strike quickly. But it takes patience. And coordination.


**Arynn**

*(watching intently as the clan leader releases the creature from the ropes)*

I can see that. This is a very delicate process.

*As the Aqualith is lowered to the ground, it flops onto the sand with a soft, wet thud. The creature struggles against its restraints for a moment before slowly settling. It looks up at Arynn with curious, wide eyes, its long, webbed fins twitching.*


**Arynn**

*(impressed, he crouches down, his large hands gently lifting one of the smaller shapeshifters from the ground and bringing him close to inspect)*

And this one? How did you catch this *little fella*?

*The small shapeshifter, a child no more than four feet tall, laughs nervously as Arynn holds him in his massive hands. The child's limbs are thin, covered in smooth scales, and his eyes shimmer with the same mischievous energy as the adults in the clan. With a soft hop, the little shapeshifter slides off Arynn's hand and lands lightly on the ground.*


**Small Shapeshifter**

*(giggling as he bounds away)*

You're big, but I'm faster!

*The little shapeshifter races toward his parents, who stand by the water's edge, watching with a soft, amused gaze. The child's tiny tail flicks behind him, sending sand spraying in all directions as he runs.*


**Arynn**

*(chuckling, watching the child run)*

Impressive... they're all agile, even the young ones.

*The clan leader turns to Arynn, his gaze softening as he watches the child join his family, who now stand together at the edge of the water. The little shapeshifter's parents smile at him, their tails swishing in the water as the child splashes gleefully.*


**Clan Leader**

*(with a slight, proud grin)*

We're a close-knit family. The young ones learn quickly, adapting to both the land and the sea.

*The sounds of the waves crashing softly against the shore fill the air, the scent of saltwater growing stronger as the clan leader steps toward the water. He turns back to Arynn with a knowing expression.*


**Clan Leader**

*(voice serious)*

But we are not here for just *mermaids* and playful creatures, are we?

*Arynn stands up, his face hardening as he steps forward, joining the clan leader by the water. The Aqualiths were fascinating, but Arynn was here for more than just curiosity about the creatures. His voice drops to a lower, more determined tone.*


**Arynn**

No. I'm here because we need to talk about the Aqualiths. The shapeshifters... I know you're hunting them. We can help with that.

*The clan leader turns to face Arynn fully, his posture shifting. His eyes narrow, and for a moment, there's a flicker of something unreadable in his gaze. Then, he nods slowly, recognizing the gravity in Arynn's words.*


**Clan Leader**

*(in a low voice, eyes steady)*

Yes. We've been tracking their movements for weeks. The Aqualiths have been raiding our territories, taking what they want, leaving destruction in their wake. We need to eliminate them, and we need your help to do it.


**Arynn**

*(nodding, resolve in his voice)*

Then let's make a deal. We will work together to hunt the Aqualiths. But in exchange, we need your help with something else—something larger. You have my word, we'll get them, but we need your loyalty for the battles ahead.

*The clan leader watches Arynn for a long moment, sizing him up. The waves crash softly against the shore as silence settles between them, but it's a silence that speaks of something more—a shared understanding.*


**Clan Leader**

*(finally, with a tight nod)*

You've got my word. Let's hunt them down, together.

### THE SHAPESHIFTERS PREPARE FOR THE HUNT
*The air is thick with the sound of waves crashing against the shore, the salty breeze stirring the palm trees. Arynn and the rest of the group stand by the water's edge, eyes fixed on the clan leader as the shapeshifters prepare for their next task.*

*From behind the trees, a squad of shapeshifters emerges, each one carrying a spear with intricate, obsidian-tipped heads. Their bodies ripple with energy, as they shift slightly to prepare for what is to come. With synchronized fluidity, the squad steps toward the water, their tails flicking behind them, kicking up sprays of sand and water with each movement.*


**Shapeshifter Squad Leader**

*(yelling in their language, excited yet focused)*

Into the waves, brothers and sisters! The hunt begins!

*With that command, the squad leaps into the water, their bodies transforming mid-air into sleek, fish-like forms. Their tails thrash, sending powerful sprays of water over the beach, sending droplets shimmering in the air as they dive into the deep, their spears held high in their hands.*

*The clan leader watches them go with a proud but focused expression. His eyes flicker toward the Aqualith hanging from the rope, still thrashing and hissing in the air, struggling against its restraints. Its long, glistening body coils in an almost serpentine motion, its wide, webbed fins flapping violently, sending waves of tension throughout the air.*


**Clan Leader**

*(quietly, almost to himself, voice low but filled with authority)*

You won't escape this time.

*He steps forward, his boots crunching on the sand as he reaches the rope that holds the Aqualith aloft. With a swift motion, he pulls the cloth away, revealing the full extent of the creature's sleek, glistening scales. The Aqualith's body, covered in bioluminescent patterns, seems to pulse with an eerie glow as it lets out a guttural hiss, its long, razor-sharp teeth bared in anger.*


**Aqualith**

*(hissing, its voice a strange, melodic growl)*

Release me... or face the depths... *I will drown you all.*

*The clan leader steps closer, his expression darkening as he gazes at the creature. Despite the Aqualith's threatening words, the leader remains unfazed, a sense of calm radiating from him. The creature struggles harder now, its scales shifting like liquid as it attempts to break free.*


**Clan Leader**

*(grinning faintly, voice mocking)*

You think you can threaten me? You're *ours* now.

*In one swift, brutal movement, the clan leader steps directly in front of the Aqualith. The creature's eyes flare with anger, and it bares its teeth again, snapping toward him. Without warning, the clan leader slaps the creature hard across the face, the sound of the slap echoing across the beach.*

*The Aqualith lets out an outraged screech, its body jerking violently in the air as the sting of the slap reverberates through its scales. It thrashes harder, but the ropes hold it firm. The clan leader stands unfazed, glaring into the Aqualith's furious eyes.*


**Clan Leader**

*(with authority, almost as though speaking to a child)*

Enough. This is the price of your attacks on our lands. The price of your arrogance. You'll be taken back to our village, and you'll understand why no one threatens the shapeshifters.

*The Aqualith glares, but its struggles begin to weaken, the initial fury of its outburst slowly dissipating as it regains its composure. It hisses one last time, its sharp, predatory eyes fixed on the clan leader.*


**Aqualith**

*(voice now quieter, filled with venom)*

You will regret this... *we will rise from the depths...*


**Arynn**

*(watching the exchange, a sense of admiration in his eyes, but his tone sharp)*

Impressive control. But don't let your guard down. Creatures like that aren't easily broken.


**Clan Leader**

*(glancing back at Arynn, a knowing look in his eyes)*

Trust me, Arynn. The Aqualiths are relentless, but so are we. They won't escape again. We'll end this now.

*The clan leader gestures for one of the nearby shapeshifters to help him with the creature. Two of the warriors, their spears still in hand, step forward. They move swiftly, one wrapping a coil of rope around the Aqualith's body to further secure it, while the other checks its restraints.*

*The air feels charged with anticipation as the clan leader turns back to Arynn and the rest of the group.*


**Clan Leader**

*(nodding to the team)*

We've had enough of their raids. You said you would help. Now it's time to see what you can do. The Aqualiths have been terrorizing us for too long.

*Arynn looks back at the rest of the squad. Juliah's eyes are narrowed, a grin tugging at the corners of her mouth. T remains calm and collected, already calculating strategies in its mind. The group is ready for the hunt.*


**Arynn**

*(glancing at the group, his voice firm)*

We'll help you. But we need to make sure we end this for good. No more threats, no more Aqualiths—only an alliance.


**Clan Leader**

*(with a knowing look)*

Agreed. The hunt begins now. Follow us, and let's end this.

*With that, the clan leader motions for the group to follow. As they head toward the water, the Aqualith still bound and struggling behind them, Arynn watches the shapeshifters disappear into the waves, their forms sleek and agile as they blend with the ocean, preparing for the next stage of the hunt.*

### THE CLAN LEADER'S REVELATION
*As Arynn and his group walk along the shore, the Aqualith in tow, the clan leader's expression shifts from one of confidence to concern. He pauses mid-stride, glancing back at the group, and his voice softens as he turns to address Arynn.*


**Clan Leader**

*(eyes narrowed, tone serious)*

There's... someone among us having trouble laying an egg. It's not something we've encountered before, but I believe we might need assistance.

*Arynn raises an eyebrow at this sudden, unexpected development. Juliah tilts her head in curiosity, while T remains motionless, observing the situation silently.*


**Arynn**

*(a little confused, but his tone professional)*

Lay an egg? We can help with that. What exactly is the issue?

*The clan leader leads the group to a shaded area near the cliffs, where a small but noticeable mound of sand is surrounded by several younger shapeshifters. They're gathered around one of their own, who's clearly struggling. The creature, an older-looking shapeshifter, is sitting on the ground, clearly in some distress. Her tail is curled tightly around her body, and her face is contorted with concentration as she breathes heavily.*


**Clan Leader**

*(calmly, though a bit worried)*

This has never happened before. We've always been able to do it without any complications. But it seems... this one is having trouble.

*Arynn steps forward, crouching near the distressed shapeshifter. He looks up at the clan leader.*


**Arynn**

*(examining the situation closely)*

It looks like she's having trouble with the egg's release. Have you tried any techniques to help her?


**Clan Leader**

*(shaking his head)*

We don't typically need help in this. But this is... unusual.

*Arynn steps closer to the shapeshifter, placing a hand gently on her shoulder. He speaks softly in an attempt to calm her.*


**Arynn**

*(with reassurance)*

It's okay. We'll take care of this. Just breathe and relax.

*The shapeshifter lets out a long exhale, her body slowly relaxing under Arynn's calming touch. After a few moments of steady breathing, Arynn observes a subtle shift in the energy of the group as the egg finally begins to move. The others around her make supportive noises, watching with interest.*


**Arynn**

*(nodding as the egg finally releases from the shapeshifter's body, now resting in the sand, safe and secure)*

There, see? That wasn't so bad.

*The shapeshifter releases a deep breath, visibly relieved. She looks up at Arynn with gratitude in her eyes, though the clan leader is the one who speaks next.*


**Clan Leader**

*(voice low but thankful)*

Thank you, Arynn. We don't have the same kind of understanding as you might, but your methods... they helped.

*Arynn steps back, giving the now-relieved shapeshifter a nod. The group gathers around the egg, its smooth surface shimmering in the light. It's nearly translucent, glowing faintly as though alive with energy. The others seem to be more relaxed, the tension easing from the air.*


**O**

*(looking puzzled, almost too casual about the situation)*

Wait, you guys lay eggs?

*The question seems to catch the group off guard for a moment, and the clan leader glances over at O with a smirk of amusement before responding, his tone calm but slightly amused by O's confusion.*


**Clan Leader**

*(with a chuckle)*

Yes, we do. It's how we reproduce. But we are genderless. We don't require sexual interaction between one another to reproduce. It's part of who we are. We don't have the biological need for males or females as you might think.


**O**

*(still confused, eyes blinking a few times)*

Wait, so… you don't... you don't have sexes? How does that even work?


**Clan Leader**

*(explaining patiently)*

Our species doesn't have gender. We reproduce through laying eggs, but it's not a process that involves any mating. The eggs are formed inside us naturally, and we simply release them when the time comes. It's more a matter of... energy transfer than biology. It's a bit difficult to explain, but it's how we've always existed.

*O stares at the clan leader for a few moments, clearly processing this revelation. Arynn, standing a little behind O, chuckles softly at her confusion, but his expression remains thoughtful.*


**Arynn**

*(nodding thoughtfully)*

Fascinating. It's a completely different way of existence. And the eggs are... are they all the same, or do they vary?


**Clan Leader**

*(glancing down at the egg in the sand, his expression softening)*

They vary. Each one is unique. It's our way of ensuring our lineage continues. The energy within them is important, and once hatched, the young shapeshifters grow quickly and bond with the land.

*O nods slowly, still absorbing the information, though her expression betrays her continued confusion. Juliah leans over to Arynn, her voice low and teasing.*


**Juliah**

*(grinning, whispering)*

Weird, huh? No sex and they still get eggs. I guess we can't all be like humans… or drones.

*Arynn shakes his head, a small chuckle escaping his lips as he focuses back on the situation at hand.*


**Arynn**

*(shrugging with a grin)*

Let's move on.

*After a brief moment of silence, the clan leader gestures toward the horizon where the sun is beginning to dip into the water, casting a golden glow across the entire beach. The group follows his gaze, and the clan leader's voice rings out with a newfound seriousness.*


**Clan Leader**

*(firmly)*

We are about to enter a sacred area. There are rules that must be followed here.

*The clan leader leads them toward the mouth of a lush, green oasis nestled among a cluster of massive rock formations. The air grows thick with the scent of flowers, and the sounds of rushing water fill the air. The land feels almost magical, alive with energy as the group approaches.*

*As they get closer, Arynn feels an odd tension in the air, something more than just the beauty of the oasis. It feels... spiritual, like they're about to witness something important. The clan leader speaks again, this time with a sense of reverence in his voice.*


**Clan Leader**

*(seriously)*

Before we go further, there is a rule that must be respected. Here, in the sacred heart of our land, clothes are not allowed. It is part of our religious customs. It's not just a matter of tradition—it's an expression of our connection to the earth, the water, and all things natural.

*Arynn's eyes widen slightly at this, and he exchanges a quick, unsure glance with the rest of his team. O raises an eyebrow, and Juliah looks entirely unbothered, her smirk growing wider. Arynn shifts uneasily, rubbing the back of his neck, unsure of how to respond to this unexpected cultural practice.*


**Arynn**

*(raising an eyebrow, slightly apprehensive)*

Uh... okay. So... no clothes, huh?

*The clan leader nods solemnly, clearly expecting this response, but there's no judgment in his tone. He motions toward the oasis, his hands outstretched, urging them to follow.*


**Clan Leader**

*(calmly)*

It's the way of our people. If you want to experience the true heart of our culture, you must embrace it fully. There are no exceptions.

*Arynn nods, a little taken aback, but knowing the importance of respecting local customs. With a deep breath, he signals to the group to continue. They all follow the clan leader into the oasis, where the warmth of the water, the soft soil beneath their feet, and the natural beauty of the environment envelop them. Despite the awkwardness of the situation, Arynn can't help but be awestruck by the serene, sacred nature of the place.*

### THE AQUALITH HUNT
*As the group walks deeper into the oasis, they hear splashing and commotion ahead, faint shouts of encouragement and exasperation carried on the wind. The clan leader turns toward the sound, his expression changing to one of mild concern.*


**Clan Leader**

*(pointing toward the shore, his voice tense)*

There's a small one struggling. Looks like they need help with an Aqualith. Come quickly.

*The group hurries forward, Arynn leading the charge. They reach the edge of the oasis, where a small shapeshifter—no more than 10 years old—struggles in the shallows. The young shapeshifter, a sprightly little one with shimmering scales and quick movements, is grappling with a massive Aqualith thrashing around in the water. The creature, nearly the size of the child, is slippery and fast, darting through the waves with terrifying agility.*

*The Aqualith is an imposing creature—its body a smooth, elongated form, covered in aquatic scales that shimmer in the sunlight. It's an apex predator in these waters, and its strength is evident as it fights desperately to break free from the little shapeshifter's grasp.*


**Arynn**

*(surveying the situation, stepping forward)*

Hang on, I've got this.

*He crouches, carefully observing the Aqualith's movements. With a calm and steady hand, Arynn pulls from his utility belt a small device—something between a fishing line and a trap—designed for just this sort of task. He attaches it quickly to a nearby rock and throws it out toward the struggling Aqualith, expertly calculating its trajectory.*

*The Aqualith notices the lure and, instinctively, begins to follow the shimmering object. Arynn's experienced hands pull the line taut, drawing the creature closer to the shore with a practiced ease. The young shapeshifter, exhausted from their earlier efforts, watches with wide eyes as the Aqualith is guided closer and closer to the shallow waters.*

*The Aqualith makes a final, desperate lunge, but Arynn's quick reflexes pull the line just in time, bringing the creature's head to a stop at the water's edge.*


**Arynn**

*(calmly, to the clan leader)*

Do you have a knife or spear?

*The clan leader, his eyes briefly scanning the scene, reaches to his side and pulls out a sleek, gleaming spear. He hands it over to Arynn with a nod.*


**Clan Leader**

*(quietly)*

Here, take this. It's sharp enough.

*With a nod of gratitude, Arynn grips the spear and moves forward. The Aqualith, now fully on the shore, thrashes weakly, its body convulsing as it tries to escape. Arynn wastes no time, thrusting the spear directly into the creature's brain. It lets out a final, guttural hiss before falling completely still.*

*The young shapeshifter, who had been struggling just moments before, looks up in awe, their eyes wide with admiration. Arynn steps back, wiping the spear clean of blood before offering it back to the clan leader.*


**Arynn**

*(with a nod of approval, addressing the young shapeshifter)*

Good effort. You almost had it yourself. But it's not easy catching them.

*O watches the scene with interest, her tail wagging in delight. As soon as the Aqualith is confirmed dead, she steps forward with a mischievous grin, her eyes gleaming.*


**O**

*(smiling, excitedly)*

My turn!

*Without missing a beat, O unsheathes her sword and steps up to the dead Aqualith. She strikes with precision, slicing through the creature's thick hide with ease. Her blade glints in the sunlight as she carves through the Aqualith's body, breaking it into pieces, each one being tossed aside with efficiency.*

*The clan members, young and old alike, watch O's quick work, some even nodding in appreciation at her skill. The clan leader steps closer, a pleased expression on his face as he watches the bounty of their hunt being carved into manageable pieces.*


**Clan Leader**

*(approvingly)*

Impressive, O. You are skilled with that blade.

*The Aqualith is soon fully dismembered, the pieces ready for transport. As the group gathers the meat, the clan leader gestures toward the water again.*


**Clan Leader**

*(with a grin)*

Come, it's time for the feast. We'll eat underwater. The tail gives us mobility to fight over the meat and spot any other Aqualiths. Follow me.

*The group follows the clan leader as he leads them to a large, shallow pool within the oasis. The water here is clear, the sunlight filtering down through the surface. The shapeshifters—some already diving in, others preparing the meat—move with fluid grace. Their tails, powerful and agile, cut through the water with ease as they position themselves.*

*Arynn watches them for a moment, his eyes following the smooth, practiced movements of the shapeshifters as they dive and swirl beneath the surface. He turns to Juliah, who seems to be grinning in anticipation.*


**Juliah**

*(teasing)*

A little underwater feast, huh? Guess we won't be needing plates.

*The group wades into the water, and Arynn is immediately impressed by the shapeshifters' fluid movements. It's almost as though they're born from the water, the way their tails give them such freedom of movement. As they dive down to retrieve pieces of the Aqualith, the hunt continues with a newfound urgency. They fight over the meat in a way that's almost playful, though still competitive. Arynn can't help but admire their resourcefulness.*

*O dives in alongside the others, her tail splashing water over the surface as she grabs a piece of Aqualith meat, holding it triumphantly in her hands before diving deeper. The sound of laughter and playful splashing fills the air, the water becoming a feast ground for the shapeshifters.*

*After some time, the group sits together on the banks of the oasis, having consumed their fill. Arynn, still amazed by the shapeshifters' deep connection with their environment, looks around at his companions.*


**Arynn**

*(content but thoughtful)*

This place... it's more than just a home. It's part of who they are. Their whole way of life is shaped by this water.


**O**

*(grinning, her mouth still full of Aqualith meat)*

And they know how to party underwater. Can't argue with that.

*The clan leader, now relaxing near the edge of the water, looks up with a nod of agreement.*


**Clan Leader**

*(reflectively)*

The water is our ally. It's the source of life and the means of our survival. We fight here, we eat here, and we connect with the land in ways you cannot fully understand... but I hope you feel it, Arynn.

*Arynn nods slowly, taking in the serene atmosphere around him. The last rays of the setting sun reflect off the water, creating a golden glow across the landscape. The shapeshifters continue their underwater feast, their laughter and joy carrying across the water. Despite the rough journey they've had, Arynn feels a sense of calm here, in this strange and fascinating world.*

### THE ANATOMY TENT
*After the feast, the clan leader motions for the group to follow him. He leads them toward a large tent set up near the oasis, its entrance shielded by thick cloth, flapping gently in the evening breeze. Inside, the air is cool and fresh, and a fire crackles in the center, casting soft shadows across the walls. The soft murmur of voices from outside fades as the group steps inside, their footsteps muffled on the soft ground.*

*The clan leader, always a figure of authority, now seems more relaxed. He gestures for everyone to take a seat around the fire, his gaze lingering on Arynn, O, and Juliah.*


**Clan Leader**

*(with a slight smile)*

I wanted to show you more... of our people. Some of the things you might not understand yet. Our bodies, our nature, and how we live with the world around us.

*He stands and pulls a piece of cloth away from a nearby pedestal, revealing a detailed model of a shapeshifter's anatomy. The model is intricate, clearly crafted with great care. Its translucent material catches the firelight, and the detailed features are clearly designed to demonstrate the unique biology of the shapeshifters.*

*The clan leader begins his explanation, his voice calm but serious.*


**Clan Leader**

*(pointing to the model)*

As you can see, we share many traits—male and female alike. We don't have sexual distinctions like humans do. No breasts, no genitals as you would understand them. We are... genderless in the sense that we don't need to reproduce through sexual intercourse.

*He gestures to the finned tail of the model, which is long and streamlined, its edges sharp. The tail is one of the most prominent features of the shapeshifters, and it glistens under the firelight.*


**Clan Leader**

*(continuing)*

Our tails are an extension of ourselves. It's what gives us the speed and mobility in the water, what allows us to fight and survive in this harsh environment. We also use them for balance and communication. The fins on our tails are sensitive, able to detect even the smallest changes in the water around us.

*The clan leader pauses, his eyes flicking over to the group as if gauging their reactions. His tone softens, as if this is a more personal subject for him.*


**Clan Leader**

*(gently)*

We produce eggs. It's how we give birth, similar to humans but different in our own way. The egg is held inside us, incubated, until it's ready to be laid. Then, we bring it into the world and care for it until it hatches. It's our way of creating new life.

*The group listens intently, absorbing the information. Arynn, who has seen many alien species in his time, remains quiet, his sharp eyes observing every detail. O, on the other hand, is clearly fascinated by the complexity of the shapeshifters' anatomy.*


**O**

*(curious, with a raised brow)*

So... you don't have any of those parts at all? No males or females in the way humans have them?


**Clan Leader**

*(shaking his head)*

Correct. We are all the same. We do not have what you might think of as ‘breasts' or ‘pe**ses.' We do not need them. Our reproduction is efficient and balanced in its own way. It is the strength of our species, and it is what makes us unique.

*He continues, pointing out the sharp canines that fill the mouth of the model, a feature that is both intimidating and necessary for survival in the waters. The canines are sharp, perfect for hunting and defending against threats.*


**Clan Leader**

Our canines are sharp, not for eating soft food, but for fighting and tearing through tougher creatures. These, along with our ability to hold our breath for 34 minutes, give us the advantage when we hunt or defend ourselves. We are built for this environment.

*The group is silent for a moment as they process everything, but O can't help herself. A mischievous smile forms on her lips, and her tail swishes behind her as she glances at the clan leader.*


**O**

*(grinning, teasing)*

Well, that explains a lot. You guys are so short and... cute. I mean, look at you! You're like little water sprites, all finned and sharp-toothed.

*The comment catches everyone off guard, and the clan leader's face instantly flushes a deep shade of crimson. He stands a little straighter, clearly embarrassed by the remark. His hand briefly brushes against his face as he looks away, trying to maintain his composure.*


**Clan Leader**

*(stammering slightly, a rare vulnerability in his voice)*

I... I am not... We are not cute...!

*The entire group breaks into quiet laughter, O's teasing remark hitting the right note. Arynn watches the clan leader with a smirk, clearly entertained by the way he reacts to the comment. Juliah, never one to let an opportunity slip by, gives O a sideways glance and winks.*


**Juliah**

*(smiling, to O)*

You really know how to make a guy blush.

*O's grin widens, her mischievous nature on full display.*


**O**

*(playfully, to the clan leader)*

It's a compliment, really. You're short and cute. It's charming.

*The clan leader, his face now as red as his scales, looks around awkwardly at the rest of the group, his attempt to maintain his dignity failing as everyone, even the usually stoic Arynn, chuckles quietly.*


**Clan Leader**

*(clearing his throat, trying to regain control of the situation)*

Yes, well... Let us move on.

*The shift in the conversation is almost palpable. The clan leader, still flustered but determined, moves on to show the rest of the anatomy model, now pointing out the intricacies of the shapeshifter's physical traits. He discusses the efficiency of their internal organs, their ability to adapt to the water, and the way their bodies are perfectly suited to life in the oasis.*

*But even as he talks about their anatomy, a small part of his mind lingers on O's comment, and it's clear that, for all his pride and authority, the clan leader will not easily forget the playful remark.*

### THE INVASION OF TALC-616 B
*After the tension in the tent finally dies down, the group gathers their thoughts and prepares to move on. Arynn, however, is deep in thought, his mind already shifting from the current moment to the mission ahead. The sounds of the clan bustling outside the tent are faint, but his expression hardens as he turns to address the group.*


**Arynn**

*(voice steady, with a hint of urgency)*

I just received word. There's an invasion at the Gek trade outpost on Talc-616 B. It's a People alien strike. We need to head there immediately.

*The words hang in the air for a moment, and the change in atmosphere is instant. The calm, peaceful moment spent in the oasis now feels distant, replaced by the harsh reality of war. O's ears perk up, her posture stiffening with purpose. The shapeshifters, still processing the earlier conversation, now shift their attention to Arynn.*


**O**

*(eyes narrowing, her tail twitching with readiness)*

People aliens? Aren't they the ones who—


**Arynn**

*(cutting her off, his voice sharp)*

Yes. And they're attacking a Gek trade outpost. We can't let them take it. The Gek might not be the most trustworthy, but they don't deserve to be wiped out by invaders.

*The clan leader, who had been silent up until now, seems to understand the gravity of the situation. His expression shifts to one of concern, his sharp canines barely visible as he speaks, his voice low but strong.*


**Clan Leader**

*(with authority)*

The Gek... We've traded with them before. If they are in danger, then we'll help.

*Juliah, ever ready for combat, cracks her knuckles, her tail swaying with an anticipatory energy.*


**Juliah**

*(grinning, her voice laced with excitement)*

Sounds like a good time to show those People aliens what happens when they mess with the wrong group.


**Arynn**

*(glancing at the clan leader, his gaze firm)*

We could use your help. These invaders are no small threat.

*The clan leader nods, his usual calm demeanor returning, but the edge of battle is now in his eyes.*


**Clan Leader**

We are ready. Lead us to Talc-616 B.

*With the decision made, the group prepares to leave. The shapeshifters gather their weapons and gear, the heavy tails of the smaller ones brushing against the ground as they ready themselves for the journey ahead. The air is filled with the hum of anticipation, the weight of what is to come clear in their movements.*

### SPACE TRAVEL
*The group boards their ship, the familiar hum of the engines starting up as they depart the oasis and head into the stars. The planet Lizard-753-N fades from view as the ship quickly gains speed, the distant glow of their home planet disappearing behind them.*

*Arynn stands at the helm, his eyes scanning the stars ahead. The urgency of the situation presses down on him, but his focus remains unwavering. O, perched nearby, watches as the stars streak by, her fingers idly tapping against her weapon. Juliah takes a seat next to her, grinning as always.*


**Juliah**

*(teasingly to O)*

You ready for this, O? Or are you gonna spend the whole trip looking out the window?


**O**

*(rolling her eyes, but with a smirk)*

I'm ready. Just don't mess this up, Juliah.


**Juliah**

*(mock hurt, placing her hand over her chest)*

You wound me, O. I never mess up.


**O**

*(deadpan)*

That's what you always say.

*Their banter fades as Arynn focuses on the mission ahead. The shapeshifters, still unfamiliar with the vastness of space travel, sit in silence, watching the stars and the ship's systems come to life around them.*

*As they approach Talc-616 B, the tension in the ship rises. The once peaceful space now feels charged with the weight of their task. The crew has only moments before they arrive at the trade outpost, and they know that time is critical.*

### ARRIVAL AT TALC-616 B
*The ship exits hyperspace with a sudden jolt, the planet Talc-616 B coming into view. It's a stark, rugged world with towering, rocky formations that seem to reach for the sky like ancient pillars. The Gek trade outpost sits at the base of one such formation, its buildings sprawling outwards, interconnected by bridges and walkways. However, the once-bustling hub is now under siege.*

*In the distance, the plumes of smoke rise into the sky, evidence of the ongoing conflict. Ships—many of them sleek and dark—hover around the outpost, firing upon it with rapid precision. The People aliens, large and imposing, can be seen moving in waves, attacking with ruthless efficiency.*


**Arynn**

*(to the crew, his voice commanding)*

We're not wasting time. Prepare for landing. We hit them fast, we hit them hard.

*The shapeshifters move quickly, their agility and silent coordination making it clear that they're prepared for battle. Juliah's expression hardens as she readies her weapons, while O's tail swishes with the thrill of the hunt. Arynn looks to the clan leader, whose sharp eyes are already scanning the situation.*


**Clan Leader**

*(quietly, his voice filled with a strange calm)*

We will fight beside you. These invaders will regret their choice.

### THE INVASION BEGINS
*The ship touches down with a soft thud, the roar of the engines echoing as the group disembarks. The air smells of burnt metal and smoke, and the ground beneath their feet trembles with the sounds of battle. The Gek are doing their best to defend the outpost, but it's clear they are outmatched. People aliens are everywhere, attacking with brutal efficiency.*

*Arynn immediately takes charge, his eyes focused on the chaos around him.*


**Arynn**

*(shouting orders)*

Split up! Juliah, O, cover the left flank. Clan Leader, stay with me—we'll take the center.

*Without hesitation, the group moves into action. Juliah and O dart to the left, their weapons ready, while the clan leader and Arynn advance towards the center of the battle. The clash of weapons fills the air, and the sound of explosions and gunfire rings out as the fight intensifies.*

*The People aliens are formidable, their bodies built for combat, but they are not invincible. Arynn strikes with precision, his blade cutting through the enemy with practiced ease. The clan leader is a blur of motion, his tail slicing through the air as he takes down invader after invader.*

*Meanwhile, Juliah and O make their way through the left flank, taking down enemies in quick succession. O's movements are smooth and fluid, her tail swishing with deadly intent. She grins as she cuts down another invader.*


**O**

*(laughing to herself)*

Is that all you've got?

*Juliah, always ready for a challenge, grins back at her.*


**Juliah**

*(mockingly)*

Come on, you've had worse!

*As the battle rages on, the People aliens begin to retreat, their forces faltering against the sheer determination of the group. But Arynn knows this is only the beginning. There are more to come.*

### O'S RAMPAGE AND SINISTER PLAN
*The dust of battle hangs thick in the air as O's blood-red eyes gleam with a feral excitement. The sounds of gunfire and explosions reverberate around her, but for a brief moment, she feels a sense of calm amidst the chaos. Her tail sways in rhythm, like a predator anticipating its next kill. Her muscles are coiled with tension, and the air around her crackles with energy.*

*She stands amidst the remains of several fallen People aliens, their bodies sprawled across the battlefield, evidence of her work. Her blade, slick with the viscera of her foes, gleams darkly in the dim light. O's breath is steady, her eyes shining with the thrill of the fight—this is where she thrives, where she is most herself. She wipes a smear of blood off her cheek with a calmness that contrasts the madness surrounding her.*


**O**

*(grinning widely, her voice a low chuckle)*

Is that all you've got? Come on, show me something more exciting.

*The remaining invaders, seeing the destruction O has left in her wake, hesitate. They know that what they're facing is no ordinary opponent. The tales of the Lizards' combat prowess have spread across the stars, and O's brutality only adds to the legend. With a sudden, bone-chilling laugh, O leaps into action.*

*Her movements are like a blur. She cuts through the remaining enemies with an efficiency that would make any seasoned warrior flinch. Her tail slashes like a whip, cutting through armor, bone, and flesh alike, leaving behind a trail of carnage. The invaders, desperate, attempt to fight back, but they are no match for her speed and power. Her strikes are precise, merciless, and each blow feels like a promise of their inevitable demise.*

*O's voice rings out over the battlefield, her tone cold and mocking.*


**O**

You know, you really should've picked a better fight. I'm not in the mood for this, but I'll gladly oblige.

*She cleaves through another group of invaders, her grin never faltering as the blood splatters around her. With every movement, she becomes a living weapon, an unstoppable force of nature. Her tail moves with purpose, crushing skulls and slicing through thick armor. A guttural scream erupts from one of the invaders as O flings him into the air, only to catch him mid-flight with a quick slash of her blade, severing him in two.*

*The remaining enemies, now fully aware that they're outmatched, try to retreat, but O is relentless. She doesn't let them get far. She pounces on them with an almost predatory grace, her claws raking through the air, finding their mark with terrifying precision. The enemies are scattered, falling one by one as O's laughter echoes across the battlefield. It's a sound that chills the bones of anyone unfortunate enough to hear it.*

*In the distance, Arynn and the clan leader are still engaged in their own skirmish, but they pause for a moment, watching as O continues her onslaught. The sheer power and brutality of her attack are unlike anything they've ever seen before. The clan leader, who has fought countless battles in his time, cannot help but respect the savagery and efficiency with which O slays her enemies.*


**Clan Leader**

*(murmuring, a touch of awe in his voice)*

She's... incredible.


**Arynn**

*(his voice firm, but with a hint of pride)*

Don't underestimate her. O's one of the best. She was born for this.

*As the last of the invaders fall to the ground, O's eyes narrow, scanning the battlefield for any remaining threats. But the fight has been won—at least, for now. She steps over the fallen bodies, her expression cold, almost detached, as if the carnage she's left behind means nothing to her. The grin never leaves her face, a twisted mix of satisfaction and bloodlust.*

*With a sudden burst of energy, O launches herself into the air. Her wings—hidden beneath her armor—unfold with a soft hiss as they catch the wind, propelling her higher and higher above the battlefield. Her movement is graceful, almost ethereal, as she soars upwards, her tail trailing behind her like a serpent poised to strike.*

*She lands effortlessly atop one of the towering structures of the Gek trade outpost, her feet barely making a sound as she perches on the edge, surveying the battlefield below with a predator's gaze. The city sprawls out beneath her, the Gek bustling in the distance, and the smoke from the battle curls up into the sky. From her perch, O can see everything—the destruction, the chaos, the lives lost, and the enemies she's obliterated.*

*Her tail flicks back and forth as she sits, cross-legged, her posture calm and contemplative as she watches the aftermath of her work. The sinister smile on her face never fades as she scans the horizon, her mind already calculating her next move.*


**O**

*(softly, to herself, her voice dripping with malice)*

This... this is just the beginning. I've got plans, big plans... and it'll be so much fun to watch them unfold.

*Her eyes gleam with an unsettling mix of intelligence and madness as she watches the remaining invaders scramble, confused and terrified. They think they've lost, but she knows better. They haven't seen the last of her. O knows how to play the long game, and her grin widens as she watches the People aliens attempt to regroup, their morale shattered.*

*For a brief moment, the battlefield is quiet, save for the distant sounds of retreating ships and the occasional shout from a retreating enemy. O's eyes narrow as she looks down at them, calculating, strategizing.*

*Her tail moves again, flicking in a serpentine motion, as if it, too, shares in her anticipation. She's waiting for the next part of the game to begin—the next move in her twisted, intricate plan. The thrill of the hunt is never truly over for her. Not while there's blood to spill and enemies to destroy.*

*As the last few retreating invaders scramble to escape, O finally speaks, her voice almost a whisper but filled with a dark promise.*


**O**

*(grinning darkly)*

You've made your move. Now... it's my turn.

*With a swift motion, O vanishes into the shadows, her wings folding tightly against her back as she takes flight once more, ready to pursue her next objective. Her sinister smile lingers in the air long after she's gone, leaving a palpable sense of dread behind her.*

*The invasion may have been won, but for O, the game is far from over. The true battle is just beginning, and she's already five steps ahead.*

### O'S SINISTER PURSUIT
*The battlefield had quieted, the sounds of retreating footsteps and scrambling invaders fading into the distance. But O wasn't done. Her blood still sang for more destruction, and her eyes gleamed with cruel anticipation. High above the ground, perched on a sturdy tree branch, she was a vision of unsettling calm—a predator awaiting the perfect moment to strike.*

*Her claws twitched restlessly, an expression of sadistic glee crossing her face as she balanced effortlessly on the branch, her body coiled and ready for action. Her eyes narrowed into the form of an '><'—those wicked, predatory eyes that seemed to anticipate pain and fear before it even reached her enemies.*


**O**

*(whispering to herself, voice dripping with malicious amusement)*

You think you're safe, don't you? Hiding, running, but I'm not finished yet. Not by a long shot.

*She shifts slightly, the soft rustling of the tree leaves blending with the eerie silence of the night. Her tail curls tightly around the branch for support, her wings tucked beneath her armor, waiting for the exact moment to unleash hell.*

*From the distance, she sees them—the retreating invaders. A small group of them, straggling behind, moving with the kind of desperation only a defeated force can have. They're unaware of the imminent danger lurking above them. O watches, her gaze fixed on them like a hawk eyeing its prey.*


**O**

*(grinning wider, her voice almost childlike in its excitement)*

Oh, you poor, poor things. You thought I was done? How cute.

*Her tail swishes, making a soft, menacing sound. She leans forward slightly, her claws digging into the branch, her eyes never leaving her targets. The railgun on her back, usually hidden, is now ready for use. With a smooth, practiced motion, she slides it off her shoulder, her smile growing darker as she prepares to strike.*

*The retreating invaders, still oblivious to their impending doom, continue moving forward, their voices carrying through the air.*


**Invader 1**

*(grumbling, looking over his shoulder)*

I can't believe we lost. I thought we were gonna wipe them out. Stupid Gek. Stupid outpost.


**Invader 2**

*(panting heavily)*

Just keep moving. We need to regroup. We'll call for reinforcements, and then we'll—

*The words are cut off abruptly as a sharp, unnatural sound fills the air—a sudden whoosh, the kind of sound a weapon makes when it's about to unleash destruction. The air crackles with tension. The invaders freeze, their heads snapping up instinctively.*


**O**

*(her voice a low, mocking sing-song tone)*

Guess who's back? And guess who's about to make your lives a whole lot shorter.

*Her claws flex, and she aims the railgun, her gaze focused and cold. The moment feels like an eternity, the quiet before the storm. The invaders are tense, but they don't know where the attack is coming from. O watches them squirm in their uncertainty, their eyes darting around, searching for the threat.*


**O**

*(giggling darkly, her smile twisted in sadistic delight)*

Don't worry, boys, I won't make it too painful. After all, I like to make things quick. But not too quick.

*With a sickeningly slow precision, O pulls the trigger of the railgun. The weapon roars to life, sending a concentrated, high-speed blast straight at the retreating group. The beam streaks through the air with a loud crack, the energy cutting through the atmosphere like a force of nature.*

*The invaders have just enough time to turn, their faces painted with horror, before the blast slams into them. The railgun's shot hits with devastating force, tearing through their ranks in an instant. There's no time to scream, no time for anything but the sudden, overwhelming impact.*

*In one shot, three invaders are obliterated, their bodies reduced to smoldering heaps of nothing. The rest of the group is scattered, thrown off balance by the shockwave of the blast. They scramble to their feet, panic setting in as they realize the full extent of their danger.*


**Invader 3**

*(yelling in fear)*

What the hell was that?! Who's—?


**O**

*(mockingly, her voice smooth and full of dark amusement)*

Who's next?

*The invaders finally see her—perched high in the tree, like some sort of demonic creature. Her silhouette is outlined against the night sky, the twisted, bloodthirsty grin on her face glowing in the moonlight. The railgun rests casually in her hands, the barrel still smoking from its last shot. Her tail swishes lazily from side to side, as if she's bored by the whole ordeal.*


**Invader 4**

*(shaking, his voice barely above a whisper)*

It's her... It's the Lizards. The one that—


**O**

*(interrupting with a voice dripping in sweet sarcasm)*

Oh, you've heard of me? How cute. I do get around.

*She tilts her head, considering them like a predator eyeing its prey. The smile on her face is something twisted, almost delighted at the fear she's instilling in them.*


**O**

*(mocking)*

You guys should've stayed home. Should've never picked this fight. But now? Well, you're mine. And you're all gonna die.

*She lets the words hang in the air, her eyes gleaming with malice. The invaders, desperate and terrified, fumble for their weapons, but they know it's too late. They're not going to escape. O is already a step ahead, her movements predatory and fluid.*


**Invader 2**

*(panicking, shouting at the others)*

We have to run! There's no time to fight! She's—

*But before he can finish his sentence, O's tail snaps forward with terrifying speed. The tip of it strikes like a viper, knocking the last invader's weapon from his hands, sending him tumbling to the ground. She watches him struggle to rise, her claws twitching with impatience.*


**O**

*(with a soft, amused chuckle)*

Oh, don't bother. You'll only embarrass yourself.

*She shifts, her tail curling as she stands up on the branch with ease. She looks at the remaining invaders with a predatory grin, every inch of her body exuding a sadistic energy that feels almost intoxicating to her.*


**O**

*(mockingly, as if speaking to children)*

Run along now, little ones. Go ahead and scurry. I promise you'll make it just a little bit longer before I catch up.

*Her voice has a sing-song quality to it, but there's no mistaking the threat beneath it. The invaders hesitate, too afraid to run and too afraid to fight. O watches their indecision with cruel delight. She waits for them to make the mistake of moving. And when they do—*


**O**

*(suddenly, her voice colder than ice)*

I wouldn't if I were you.

*The command in her voice is unmistakable. One of the invaders makes the foolish decision to turn and flee. That's all it takes. O's patience snaps, and in the blink of an eye, she's down from the tree, the railgun aimed and ready once more. She pulls the trigger again—this time, the shot is even faster, the beam cutting through the air with lightning speed.*

*The blast hits the fleeing invader directly in the back, the force of the shot leaving nothing behind but a charred crater in the dirt. The other invaders turn in shock, but it's too late. O is already there, her claws tearing through the air as she lunges toward them.*

*One by one, she eliminates them, each strike more brutal and savage than the last. Her tail whips and lashes, slicing through the air, and her laughter rings out, a chilling sound of pure sadistic pleasure. With every fallen enemy, O's grin widens, her eyes never leaving the now-shattered group of invaders.*

*In the end, there's nothing left but smoke, broken bodies, and O's satisfied laughter echoing across the ruined battlefield.*


**O**

*(panting lightly, her voice a hushed whisper to herself, still grinning)*

See? I told you... you wouldn't make it.
